        };
        const safeName = (v) =>
          String(v || "배송").replace(/[\\/:*?"<>|]/g, "_");
        const readJSON = (key, fallback) => {
          try {
            return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || "null") ?? fallback;
          } catch {
            return fallback;
          }
        };
        const driverEmail = (employeeCode) =>
          `${String(employeeCode || "")
            .trim()
            .toLowerCase()
            .replace(/[^a-z0-9_-]/g, "")}@${driverConfig?.driverEmailDomain || "drivers.invalid"}`;

        async function loadDriverConfig() {
          try {
            const response = await fetch("/api/config", { cache: "no-store" });
            if (!response.ok) throw new Error("환경설정을 확인할 수 없습니다.");
            return await response.json();
          } catch {
            return { configured: false };
          }
        }
        function setDriverAuthMessage(message, good = false) {
          const el = $("#driverAuthMessage");
          if (!el) return;
          el.textContent = message || "";
          el.style.color = good ? "var(--green)" : "var(--red)";
        }
        function showDriverAuth(message = "") {
          $("#driverApp")?.classList.add("hidden");
          $("#driverAuth")?.classList.remove("hidden");
          setDriverAuthMessage(message);
          const remembered = localStorage.getItem(DRIVER_AUTH_ID_KEY) || "";
          if ($("#driverLoginId")) $("#driverLoginId").value = remembered;
        }
        function showDriverApp() {
          $("#driverAuth")?.classList.add("hidden");
          $("#driverApp")?.classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        async function fetchAssignedProfile(userId) {
          const { data, error } = await supabaseClient
            .from("profiles")
            .select("id, role, employee_code, full_name, vehicle_number, active")
            .eq("id", userId)
            .maybeSingle();
          if (error) throw error;
          if (!data || data.role !== "driver")
            throw new Error("배송원으로 등록되지 않은 계정입니다.");
          if (!data.active) throw new Error("관리자가 사용 정지한 계정입니다.");
          if (!data.vehicle_number)
            throw new Error("관리자가 아직 호차를 배정하지 않았습니다.");
          return data;
        }
        async function applyAuthenticatedDriver(session) {
          const profile = await fetchAssignedProfile(session.user.id);
          supabaseSession = session;
          assignedDriverProfile = profile;
          state.profile = {
            companyName: "장백수산",
            driverName: profile.full_name,
            vehicleNumber: String(profile.vehicle_number),
          };
          localStorage.setItem(DRIVER_AUTH_ID_KEY, profile.employee_code);
          await restoreNewerCentralSnapshot();
          state.profile = {
            companyName: "장백수산",
            driverName: profile.full_name,
            vehicleNumber: String(profile.vehicle_number),
          };
          saveState("로그인·관리자 호차 배정 적용");
          showDriverApp();
          await loadCentralWork();
          render();
          startCloudSync();
          scheduleCentralSync("로그인");
          clearInterval(centralSyncTimer);
          centralSyncTimer = setInterval(
            () => syncCentralStatus("1분 접속 확인"),
            60000,
          );
          clearInterval(centralTaskTimer);
          centralTaskTimer = setInterval(loadCentralWork, 20000);
        }
        async function driverLogin() {
          if (!supabaseClient) return;
          const code = String($("#driverLoginId")?.value || "")
              .trim()
              .toLowerCase(),
            password = String($("#driverLoginPassword")?.value || "");
          if (code.length < 3 || !password)
            return setDriverAuthMessage("아이디와 비밀번호를 입력해 주세요.");
          setDriverAuthMessage("로그인 확인 중입니다.", true);
          $("#driverLoginButton").disabled = true;
          try {
            const { data, error } = await supabaseClient.auth.signInWithPassword(
              { email: driverEmail(code), password },
            );
            if (error || !data.session)
              throw new Error("아이디 또는 비밀번호가 맞지 않습니다.");
            await applyAuthenticatedDriver(data.session);
            $("#driverLoginPassword").value = "";
          } catch (error) {
            await supabaseClient.auth.signOut();
            showDriverAuth(error?.message || "로그인하지 못했습니다.");
          } finally {
            $("#driverLoginButton").disabled = false;
          }
        }
        async function driverLogout() {
          clearInterval(centralSyncTimer);
          clearInterval(centralTaskTimer);
          clearTimeout(centralSyncDebounce);
          stopQrScanner();
          if (supabaseClient) await supabaseClient.auth.signOut();
          supabaseSession = null;
          assignedDriverProfile = null;
          centralUrgentOrders = [];
          centralStores = [];
          centralIncidents = [];
          centralDeparture = null;
          centralWorkday = null;
          showDriverAuth("안전하게 로그아웃했습니다.");
        }
        async function initDriverAuth() {
          driverConfig = await loadDriverConfig();
          if (
            !driverConfig.configured ||
            !window.supabase?.createClient
          ) {
            showDriverAuth(
              "관리자 시스템 연결 설정이 필요합니다. 관리자에게 알려 주세요.",
            );
            $("#driverLoginButton").disabled = true;
            return;
          }
          supabaseClient = window.supabase.createClient(
            driverConfig.supabaseUrl,
            driverConfig.supabaseAnonKey,
            { auth: { persistSession: true, autoRefreshToken: true } },
          );
          $("#driverLoginButton").addEventListener("click", driverLogin);
          $("#driverLoginPassword").addEventListener("keydown", (event) => {
            if (event.key === "Enter") driverLogin();
          });
          const { data } = await supabaseClient.auth.getSession();
          if (!data.session) return showDriverAuth();
          try {
            await applyAuthenticatedDriver(data.session);
          } catch (error) {
            await supabaseClient.auth.signOut();
            showDriverAuth(error?.message || "다시 로그인해 주세요.");
          }
        }
        const normalizeCategory = (value) =>
          ({
            필렛제품: "필렛 제품",
            "패류.해산물": "패류",
            "연어.포장품": "필렛 제품",
          })[value] || (categories.includes(value) ? value : "활어");
        let state = loadState(),
          view = "today",
          workDate = localDate(1),
          selectedDeliveryId = null,
          deliveryEditId = null,
          customerEditId = null,
          formDraft = null,
          reorderMode = false,
          weighDeliveryId = null,
          weighItemId = null,
          tankDeliveryId = null,
          tankItemId = null,
          tankPendingNumber = 0,
          tankReturn = "manager",
          tankInfoNumber = 0,
          tankDrag = null,
          tankDragSuppressUntil = 0,
          tankDragToastTimer = null,
          storeGuideDeliveryId = null,
          storeGuideReturn = "today",
          guideSecretTimer = null,
          cloudTimer = null,
          alarmTimer = null,
          cancelTimer = null,
          loadingDeliveryId = null,
          loadingItemId = null,
          loadingWeightId = null,
          loadingFilterDeliveryId = 0,
          loadingFilterItemId = 0,
          loadingError = "",
          qrStream = null,
          qrTimer = null,
          qrReturnView = "loading";

        function emptyState() {
          return {
            version: 5,
            profile: { companyName: "", driverName: "", vehicleNumber: "" },
            customers: [],
            deliveries: [],
            departureChecks: {},
            preferences: {
              autoNextLoading: true,
              weightRules: JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(DEFAULT_WEIGHT_RULES)),
            },
            workClosures: {},
            workClosureHistory: [],
          };
        }
        function normalizeWeightRules(rules = {}) {
          const result = {};
          Object.entries(DEFAULT_WEIGHT_RULES).forEach(
            ([species, defaults]) => {
              const source = rules?.[species] || defaults,
                min = Math.max(0.001, Number(source.min) || defaults.min),
                max = Math.max(min, Number(source.max) || defaults.max);
              result[species] = { min, max };
            },
          );
          return result;
        }
        function normalizeWeighing(
          entry = {},
          legacyLoaded = false,
          legacyLoadedAt = null,
        ) {
          const legacyAt = legacyLoaded
            ? legacyLoadedAt || entry.at || new Date().toISOString()
            : null;
          return {
            id: Number(entry.id) || newId(),
            taskNumber: Math.max(0, Math.floor(Number(entry.taskNumber) || 0)),
            weight: Math.max(0, Number(entry.weight) || 0),
            at: entry.at || new Date().toISOString(),
            calledAt: entry.calledAt || legacyAt,
            calledBy: entry.calledBy || (legacyLoaded ? "기존 상차 기록" : ""),
            repeatConfirmedAt: entry.repeatConfirmedAt || legacyAt,
            repeatConfirmedBy:
              entry.repeatConfirmedBy || (legacyLoaded ? "기존 상차 기록" : ""),
            bandVerifiedAt: entry.bandVerifiedAt || legacyAt,
            bandVerifiedBy:
              entry.bandVerifiedBy || (legacyLoaded ? "기존 상차 기록" : ""),
            tankVerifiedAt: entry.tankVerifiedAt || legacyAt,
            tankVerifiedBy:
              entry.tankVerifiedBy || (legacyLoaded ? "기존 상차 기록" : ""),
            verifiedVehicle:
              entry.verifiedVehicle || (legacyLoaded ? "기존 호차" : ""),
            verifiedTank: Math.max(
              0,
              Math.min(6, Number(entry.verifiedTank) || 0),
            ),
            loadedAt: entry.loadedAt || legacyAt,
            loadedBy: entry.loadedBy || (legacyLoaded ? "기존 상차 기록" : ""),
            lastError: entry.lastError || "",
            verificationLog: Array.isArray(entry.verificationLog)
              ? entry.verificationLog.slice(-20)
              : [],
          };
        }
        function normalizeTankChange(entry = {}) {
          return {
            id: Number(entry.id) || newId(),
            from: Math.max(0, Math.min(6, Number(entry.from) || 0)),
            to: Math.max(0, Math.min(6, Number(entry.to) || 0)),
            reason: entry.reason || "현장 수조 변경",
            at: entry.at || new Date().toISOString(),
          };
        }
        function normalizeItem(item = {}) {
          const category = normalizeCategory(item.category),
            unit = item.unit || "마리",
            legacyLoaded = Boolean(item.tankLoaded),
            legacyTank = Math.max(0, Math.min(6, Number(item.tankNumber) || 0)),
            weighings = Array.isArray(item.weighings)
              ? item.weighings
                  .map((w) =>
                    normalizeWeighing(w, legacyLoaded, item.tankLoadedAt),
                  )
                  .filter((w) => w.weight > 0)
              : [],
            weighed = Number(
              weighings.reduce((s, w) => s + w.weight, 0).toFixed(3),
            ),
            manual =
              item.actualWeight === "" || item.actualWeight == null
                ? null
                : Number(item.actualWeight);
          if (legacyLoaded)
            weighings.forEach((w) => {
              if (!w.verifiedTank) w.verifiedTank = legacyTank;
            });
          const taskLoaded = weighings.length
            ? weighings.every((w) => Boolean(w.loadedAt))
            : legacyLoaded;
          return {
            id: Number(item.id) || newId(),
            category,
            species: item.species || item.item || "광어",
            size: item.size || "기본 규격",
            originCountry: item.originCountry || item.origin || "국내산",
            requestedQty: Math.max(
              0,
              Number(item.requestedQty ?? item.qty) || 0,
            ),
            unit,
            actualWeight: weighings.length ? weighed : manual,
            weighings,
            weighingConfirmed:
              Boolean(item.weighingConfirmed) && weighings.length > 0,
            weighingConfirmedAt: item.weighingConfirmedAt || null,
            priceUnit:
              item.priceUnit ||
              (category === "냉동제품"
                ? unit
                : category === "패류"
                  ? unit
                  : "kg"),
            unitPrice: Number(item.unitPrice) || 0,
            processingFeePerKg: Number(item.processingFeePerKg) || 0,
            processing: item.processing || item.process || "찍어바리",
            tankNumber: legacyTank,
            tankHistory: Array.isArray(item.tankHistory)
              ? item.tankHistory.map(normalizeTankChange)
              : [],
            tankLoaded: taskLoaded,
            tankLoadedAt: taskLoaded
              ? item.tankLoadedAt ||
                weighings[weighings.length - 1]?.loadedAt ||
                null
              : null,
            rubberBand: Boolean(item.rubberBand),
            rubberBandQuantity: Number(item.rubberBandQuantity) || 0,
            rubberBandColor: item.rubberBandColor || "",
            includedNote:
              item.includedNote ||
              (item.memo && item.memo !== "없음" ? item.memo : "") ||
              "",
            checked: Boolean(item.checked),
          };
        }
        function normalizeBox(box = {}, index = 0) {
          return {
            id: Number(box.id) || newId(),
            boxNumber: index + 1,
            contents: box.contents || "",
            checked: Boolean(box.checked),
          };
        }
        function normalizeCustomer(customer = {}, index = 0) {
          return {
            ...customer,
            id: Number(customer.id) || newId(),
            routeOrder: Number(customer.routeOrder) || index + 1,
            name: customer.name || "",
            deliveryPlace: customer.deliveryPlace || "",
            address: customer.address || "",
            phone: customer.phone || "",
            accessPassword: customer.accessPassword || "",
            entryMethod: customer.entryMethod || "",
            dropLocation: customer.dropLocation || "",
            deliveryCautions: customer.deliveryCautions || "",
            receivingTime: customer.receivingTime || "",
            parkingInfo: customer.parkingInfo || "",
            handoverNote: customer.handoverNote || "",
            handoverUpdatedAt: customer.handoverUpdatedAt || null,
            handoverUpdatedBy: customer.handoverUpdatedBy || "",
          };
        }
        function normalizeDelivery(delivery = {}) {
          const urgent = Boolean(delivery.isUrgentAdditional);
          return {
            ...delivery,
            id: Number(delivery.id) || newId(),
            customerId: Number(delivery.customerId) || 0,
            deliveryDate: delivery.deliveryDate || localDate(1),
            routeOrder: Math.max(1, Number(delivery.routeOrder) || 1),
            status: ["new", "ready", "completed", "cancelled"].includes(
              delivery.status,
            )
              ? delivery.status
              : "ready",
            previousBalance: Number(delivery.previousBalance) || 0,
            notes: delivery.notes || "",
            coPackNote: delivery.coPackNote || "",
            isUrgentAdditional: urgent,
            urgentAcknowledged: urgent
              ? Boolean(delivery.urgentAcknowledged)
              : true,
            urgentAcknowledgedAt: delivery.urgentAcknowledgedAt || null,
            handoverAcknowledgedVersion:
              delivery.handoverAcknowledgedVersion || "",
            handoverAcknowledgedAt: delivery.handoverAcknowledgedAt || null,
            handoverAcknowledgedBy: delivery.handoverAcknowledgedBy || "",
            handoverAcknowledgedVehicle:
              delivery.handoverAcknowledgedVehicle || "",
            loadedBoxCount: Math.max(
              0,
              Math.floor(Number(delivery.loadedBoxCount) || 0),
            ),
            boxCountConfirmed: Boolean(delivery.boxCountConfirmed),
            boxCountConfirmedAt: delivery.boxCountConfirmedAt || null,
            items: Array.isArray(delivery.items)
              ? delivery.items.map(normalizeItem)
              : [],
            boxes: Array.isArray(delivery.boxes)
              ? delivery.boxes.map(normalizeBox)
              : [],
          };
        }
        function loadState() {
          const raw = readJSON(STORAGE_KEY, null);
          if (
            !raw ||
            !raw.profile ||
            !Array.isArray(raw.customers) ||
            !Array.isArray(raw.deliveries)
          )
            return emptyState();
          return {
            version: 5,
            profile: {
              companyName: raw.profile.companyName || "",
              driverName: raw.profile.driverName || "",
              vehicleNumber: raw.profile.vehicleNumber || "",
            },
            customers: raw.customers.map(normalizeCustomer),
            deliveries: raw.deliveries.map(normalizeDelivery),
            departureChecks:
              raw.departureChecks && typeof raw.departureChecks === "object"
                ? raw.departureChecks
                : {},
            preferences: {
              autoNextLoading:
                raw.preferences?.autoNextLoading === undefined
                  ? true
                  : Boolean(raw.preferences.autoNextLoading),
              weightRules: normalizeWeightRules(raw.preferences?.weightRules),
            },
            workClosures:
              raw.workClosures && typeof raw.workClosures === "object"
                ? raw.workClosures
                : {},
            workClosureHistory: Array.isArray(raw.workClosureHistory)
              ? raw.workClosureHistory.slice(-200)
              : [],
          };
        }
        function saveAutoSnapshot(raw, reason = "자동 저장 전") {
          if (!raw) return;
          try {
            const list = readJSON(AUTO_BACKUP_KEY, []),
              last = list[list.length - 1];
            if (last?.data === raw) return;
            list.push({
              id: newId(),
              at: new Date().toISOString(),
              reason,
              data: raw,
            });
            localStorage.setItem(
              AUTO_BACKUP_KEY,
              JSON.stringify(list.slice(-8)),
            );
          } catch {}
        }
        function saveState(reason = "자동 저장") {
          try {
            const before = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY),
              next = JSON.stringify(state);
            if (before && before !== next) saveAutoSnapshot(before, reason);
            localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, next);
            localStorage.setItem(LAST_SAVED_KEY, new Date().toISOString());
            renderHeader();
            scheduleCentralSync(reason);
          } catch {
            alert(
              "저장 공간이 부족합니다. 자동 백업을 정리하거나 브라우저 저장 공간을 확인해 주세요.",
            );
          }
        }
        function centralStatusPayload() {
          const rows = deliveries(),
            active = rows.filter((d) => d.status !== "cancelled"),
            done = active.filter((d) => d.status === "completed").length,
            tanks = tankLoadRows(),
            boxes = boxCompareRows(),
            urgent = urgentRows(),
            issues = departureIssues(),
            errors = errorStats(),
            closed = isWorkClosed();
          let workState = "not_started";
          if (active.length) workState = "working";
          if (departureReady()) workState = "departure_ready";
          if (active.length && done > 0 && done < active.length)
            workState = "delivering";
          if (closed || (active.length && done === active.length))
            workState = "completed";
          return {
            driver_id: assignedDriverProfile.id,
            work_date: workDate,
            work_state: workState,
            delivery_total: active.length,
            delivery_completed: done,
            tank_total: tanks.length,
            tank_loaded: tanks.filter(({ i }) => i.tankLoaded).length,
            box_total: boxes.length,
            box_checked: boxes.filter(
              (d) =>
                d.boxCountConfirmed && d.loadedBoxCount === d.boxes.length,
            ).length,
            urgent_pending:
              urgent.length +
              centralUrgentOrders.filter((x) =>
                ["new", "acknowledged", "loaded"].includes(x.status),
              ).length,
            issue_count: issues.length,
            prevented_errors: errors.prevented || 0,
            last_sync_at: new Date().toISOString(),
          };
        }
        function scheduleCentralSync(reason = "자료 변경") {
          if (!supabaseClient || !supabaseSession || !assignedDriverProfile)
            return;
          clearTimeout(centralSyncDebounce);
          centralSyncDebounce = setTimeout(
            () => syncCentralStatus(reason),
            900,
          );
        }
        async function syncCentralStatus(reason = "상태 갱신") {
          if (
            centralSyncBusy ||
            !supabaseClient ||
            !supabaseSession ||
            !assignedDriverProfile
          )
            return;
          centralSyncBusy = true;
          try {
            const profile = await fetchAssignedProfile(
              supabaseSession.user.id,
            );
            if (
              profile.vehicle_number !== assignedDriverProfile.vehicle_number ||
              profile.full_name !== assignedDriverProfile.full_name
            ) {
              assignedDriverProfile = profile;
              state.profile = {
                companyName: "장백수산",
                driverName: profile.full_name,
                vehicleNumber: String(profile.vehicle_number),
              };
              localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(state));
              render();
            }
            if (centralWorkday?.is_closed) {
              const network = $("#networkText");
              if (network) network.textContent = "관리자 업무 마감·자료 잠금";
              await supabaseClient.rpc("touch_driver_presence");
              return;
            }
            const status = centralStatusPayload();
            const departurePayload = {
              driver_id: assignedDriverProfile.id,
              work_date: workDate,
              vehicle_number: assignedDriverProfile.vehicle_number,
              orders_checked: activeDeliveries().every(
                (d) => d.status !== "new",
              ),
              tanks_checked:
                status.tank_total === 0 ||
                status.tank_total === status.tank_loaded,
              boxes_checked:
                status.box_total === 0 ||
                status.box_total === status.box_checked,
              urgent_checked: status.urgent_pending === 0,
              handover_checked: activeDeliveries().every((d) => {
                const c = customerOf(d);
                return !hasHandover(c) || handoverAcknowledged(d, c);
              }),
              driver_ready: departureReady(),
              updated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
            };
            const [
              { error: statusError },
              { error: snapshotError },
              { error: departureError },
            ] =
              await Promise.all([
                supabaseClient
                  .from("driver_daily_status")
                  .upsert(status, { onConflict: "driver_id,work_date" }),
                supabaseClient.from("driver_state_snapshots").upsert(
                  {
                    driver_id: assignedDriverProfile.id,
                    work_date: workDate,
                    payload: state,
                    updated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
                  },
                  { onConflict: "driver_id,work_date" },
                ),
                centralDeparture?.approved
                  ? Promise.resolve({ error: null })
                  : supabaseClient
                      .from("departure_checks")
                      .upsert(departurePayload, {
                        onConflict: "driver_id,work_date",
                      }),
              ]);
            if (statusError) throw statusError;
            if (snapshotError) throw snapshotError;
            if (departureError) throw departureError;
            await supabaseClient.rpc("touch_driver_presence");
            const network = $("#networkText");
            if (network)
              network.textContent = `${assignedDriverProfile.vehicle_number}호차 중앙 저장 완료`;
            if (reason === "로그인") renderHeader();
          } catch (error) {
            const network = $("#networkText");
            if (network) network.textContent = "중앙 저장 재시도 중";
            if (/정지|active driver/i.test(error?.message || "")) {
              await driverLogout();
              showDriverAuth("관리자가 사용 정지한 계정입니다.");
            }
          } finally {
            centralSyncBusy = false;
          }
        }
        async function restoreNewerCentralSnapshot() {
          if (!supabaseClient || !supabaseSession) return;
          const { data, error } = await supabaseClient
            .from("driver_state_snapshots")
            .select("payload, updated_at")
            .eq("driver_id", supabaseSession.user.id)
            .eq("work_date", workDate)
            .maybeSingle();
          if (error || !data?.payload) return;
          const localSaved = localStorage.getItem(LAST_SAVED_KEY),
            localTime = localSaved ? new Date(localSaved).getTime() : 0,
            remoteTime = new Date(data.updated_at || 0).getTime();
          if (remoteTime <= localTime) return;
          const before = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
          if (before) saveAutoSnapshot(before, "중앙 자료 복구 전");
          localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify(data.payload));
          state = loadState();
          localStorage.setItem(LAST_SAVED_KEY, data.updated_at);
        }
        async function loadCentralWork() {
          if (!supabaseClient || !assignedDriverProfile) return;
          try {
            const [urgent, stores, incidents, departure, workday] =
              await Promise.all([
                supabaseClient
                  .from("urgent_orders")
                  .select("*")
                  .eq("work_date", workDate)
                  .order("created_at", { ascending: false }),
                supabaseClient
                  .from("stores")
                  .select(
                    "id,store_code,name,address,phone,contact_name,assigned_driver_id,assigned_vehicle,delivery_order,preferred_time,entry_method,placement,prohibited,parking_note,handover_note,photo_urls,active,updated_at",
                  )
                  .eq("active", true)
                  .order("delivery_order"),
                supabaseClient
                  .from("incident_reports")
                  .select("*")
                  .eq("work_date", workDate)
                  .order("created_at", { ascending: false }),
                supabaseClient
                  .from("departure_checks")
                  .select("*")
                  .eq("driver_id", assignedDriverProfile.id)
                  .eq("work_date", workDate)
                  .maybeSingle(),
                supabaseClient
                  .from("workday_controls")
                  .select("*")
                  .eq("work_date", workDate)
                  .maybeSingle(),
              ]);
            if (!urgent.error) centralUrgentOrders = urgent.data || [];
            if (!stores.error) centralStores = stores.data || [];
            if (!incidents.error) centralIncidents = incidents.data || [];
            if (!departure.error) centralDeparture = departure.data || null;
            if (!workday.error) centralWorkday = workday.data || null;
            if (view === "today" && !$("#driverApp")?.classList.contains("hidden"))
              renderToday();
          } catch {
            /* 다음 자동 확인에서 재시도합니다. */
          }
        }
        function centralUrgentLabel(status) {
          return (
            {
              new: "새 긴급 발주",
              acknowledged: "확인 완료",
              loaded: "상차 완료",
              delivered: "납품 완료",
              impossible: "처리 불가",
              cancelled: "취소",
            }[status] || status
          );
        }
        function centralPanelHTML() {
          const pending = centralUrgentOrders.filter((x) =>
              ["new", "acknowledged", "loaded"].includes(x.status),
            ),
            approval = centralDeparture?.approved,
            guideCount = centralStores.filter(
              (s) =>
                s.entry_method ||
                s.placement ||
                s.prohibited ||
                s.preferred_time ||
                s.handover_note,
            ).length;
          const alerts = pending
            .map((x) => {
              const next =
                x.status === "new"
                  ? ["central-urgent-ack", "긴급 발주 확인"]
                  : x.status === "acknowledged"
                    ? ["central-urgent-loaded", "상차 완료"]
                    : ["central-urgent-delivered", "납품 완료"];
              return `<article class="central-alert"><strong>🚨 ${esc(x.store_name || "거래처")} · ${esc(x.item_summary)}</strong><small>${esc(x.quantity_summary || "")} · ${esc(x.note || "추가 메모 없음")} · ${centralUrgentLabel(x.status)}</small><div class="central-alert-actions"><button class="primary" type="button" data-action="${next[0]}" data-id="${x.id}">${next[1]}</button><button type="button" data-action="central-urgent-impossible" data-id="${x.id}">처리 불가 보고</button></div></article>`;
            })
            .join("");
          return `<section class="central-hub"><div class="central-hub-head"><div><h2>🏢 중앙 관리자 연결</h2><small>긴급 발주·점포 인수인계·출차 승인 상태가 20초마다 갱신됩니다.</small></div><span class="central-state ${approval ? "ok" : centralWorkday?.is_closed ? "bad" : ""}">${approval ? "✓ 관리자 출차 승인" : centralWorkday?.is_closed ? "업무 마감 잠금" : "승인 대기"}</span></div>${centralWorkday?.is_closed ? `<div class="central-closed">관리자가 ${esc(workDate)} 업무를 마감했습니다. 변경이 잠겼습니다.</div>` : ""}<div class="central-alert-list">${alerts}</div><div class="central-tools"><button type="button" data-action="central-store-guides">📝 중앙 인수인계 ${guideCount}곳</button><button type="button" data-action="central-incident-new">⚠️ 오배송·오류 보고</button><button type="button" data-action="central-refresh">↻ 관리자 자료 새로고침</button></div></section>`;
        }
        async function updateCentralUrgent(id, status, extra = {}) {
          const changes = {
            status,
            updated_at: new Date().toISOString(),
            ...extra,
          };
          if (status === "acknowledged")
            changes.acknowledged_at = new Date().toISOString();
          if (status === "loaded")
            changes.loaded_at = new Date().toISOString();
          if (status === "delivered")
            changes.delivered_at = new Date().toISOString();
          const { error } = await supabaseClient
            .from("urgent_orders")
            .update(changes)
            .eq("id", id);
          if (error) throw error;
          await loadCentralWork();
          scheduleCentralSync("중앙 긴급 발주 상태 변경");
        }
        function openCentralStores() {
          const rows = centralStores
            .map(
              (s) =>
                `<article class="central-store-row"><strong>${s.delivery_order || "-"}번 · ${esc(s.name)}</strong><small>${esc(s.preferred_time || "입고 시간 미입력")} · ${esc(s.address || "주소 미입력")}</small><small><b>진입:</b> ${esc(s.entry_method || "미입력")}<br><b>놓는 곳:</b> ${esc(s.placement || "미입력")}<br><b>금지사항:</b> ${esc(s.prohibited || "없음")}<br><b>기타:</b> ${esc(s.handover_note || "없음")}</small></article>`,
            )
            .join("");
          $("#centralModal").innerHTML = `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>중앙 점포 인수인계</h2><p>${assignedDriverProfile.vehicle_number}호차 담당 점포 정보입니다.</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="central-modal-close">×</button></div><div class="modal-body"><div style="display:grid;gap:8px">${rows || `<div class="empty">관리자가 등록한 점포 정보가 없습니다.</div>`}</div><div class="notice">출입 비밀번호는 보안을 위해 배차 관리자에게 확인하세요.</div></div></div>`;
          $("#centralModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function openCentralIncident() {
          $("#centralModal").innerHTML = `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>오배송·현장 오류 보고</h2><p>관리자에게 즉시 전달되고 조치 이력이 남습니다.</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="central-modal-close">×</button></div><form id="centralIncidentForm" class="modal-body"><label class="field"><span>오류 종류</span><select class="control" name="incidentType"><option value="wrong_delivery">오배송</option><option value="shortage">수량 부족</option><option value="excess">수량 초과</option><option value="damage">파손</option><option value="band_mismatch">밴드 색상 오류</option><option value="tank_mismatch">수조 오류</option><option value="delay">배송 지연</option><option value="other">기타</option></select></label><label class="field"><span>중요도</span><select class="control" name="severity"><option value="normal">일반</option><option value="important">중요</option><option value="critical">긴급</option></select></label><label class="field"><span>거래처</span><select class="control" name="storeId"><option value="">거래처 미지정</option>${centralStores.map((s) => `<option value="${s.id}">${esc(s.name)}</option>`).join("")}</select></label><label class="field"><span>상세 내용</span><textarea class="control" name="description" rows="5" required placeholder="어떤 문제가 있었는지 구체적으로 입력하세요."></textarea></label><div id="centralIncidentMessage" class="message"></div><button class="full-button danger-button" type="submit">관리자에게 오류 보고</button></form></div>`;
          $("#centralModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function byOrder(a, b) {
          return (
            (Number(a.routeOrder) || 999) - (Number(b.routeOrder) || 999) ||
            (Number(a.id) || 0) - (Number(b.id) || 0)
          );
        }
        function customers() {
          return [...state.customers].sort(byOrder);
        }
        function deliveries(date = workDate) {
          return state.deliveries
            .filter((d) => d.deliveryDate === date)
            .sort(byOrder);
        }
        function activeDeliveries() {
          return deliveries().filter((d) => d.status !== "cancelled");
        }
        function customerOf(d) {
          return (
            state.customers.find((c) => c.id === d.customerId) ||
            normalizeCustomer({
              name: d.fallbackStoreName || "알 수 없는 거래처",
            })
          );
        }
        function handoverFields(c) {
          return [
            "accessPassword",
            "entryMethod",
            "dropLocation",
            "deliveryCautions",
            "receivingTime",
            "parkingInfo",
            "handoverNote",
          ].map((key) => String(c?.[key] || "").trim());
        }
        function hasHandover(c) {
          return handoverFields(c).some(Boolean);
        }
        function handoverVersion(c) {
          return String(c?.handoverUpdatedAt || "legacy");
        }
        function handoverAcknowledged(d, c = customerOf(d)) {
          return (
            !hasHandover(c) ||
            (String(d?.handoverAcknowledgedVersion || "") ===
              handoverVersion(c) &&
              String(d?.handoverAcknowledgedBy || "") ===
                String(state.profile.driverName || "") &&
              String(d?.handoverAcknowledgedVehicle || "") ===
                String(state.profile.vehicleNumber || ""))
          );
        }
        function pendingHandoverRows() {
          return activeDeliveries().filter(
            (d) =>
              d.status !== "completed" &&
              hasHandover(customerOf(d)) &&
              !handoverAcknowledged(d),
          );
        }
        function quantityText(i) {
          if (i.actualWeight != null && Number(i.actualWeight) > 0)
            return `${i.actualWeight}kg`;
          return `${i.requestedQty}${i.unit}`;
        }
        function priceQuantity(i) {
          if (i.priceUnit === "kg")
            return Number(i.actualWeight ?? i.requestedQty) || 0;
          return Number(i.requestedQty) || 0;
        }
        function baseAmount(i) {
          return priceQuantity(i) * (Number(i.unitPrice) || 0);
        }
        function itemAmount(i) {
          const fee =
            i.category === "필렛 제품"
              ? (Number(i.actualWeight ?? i.requestedQty) || 0) *
                (Number(i.processingFeePerKg) || 0)
              : 0;
          return baseAmount(i) + fee;
        }
        function isWeighable(i) {
          return i.category === "활어";
        }
        function targetFishCount(i) {
          return isWeighable(i) && i.unit === "마리"
            ? Math.max(0, Math.round(Number(i.requestedQty) || 0))
            : 0;
        }
        function weightTotal(i) {
          return Number(
            (i.weighings || [])
              .reduce((s, w) => s + (Number(w.weight) || 0), 0)
              .toFixed(3),
          );
        }
        function syncWeightTotal(i) {
          i.actualWeight = i.weighings?.length ? weightTotal(i) : null;
        }
        function weighingRows() {
          return activeDeliveries()
            .filter((d) => d.status !== "completed")
            .flatMap((d) =>
              (d.items || [])
                .filter(isWeighable)
                .map((i) => ({ d, i, c: customerOf(d) })),
            );
        }
        function weighingStats() {
          const rows = weighingRows(),
            target = rows.reduce((s, x) => s + targetFishCount(x.i), 0),
            entered = rows.reduce(
              (s, x) => s + (x.i.weighings || []).length,
              0,
            ),
            confirmed = rows.filter((x) => x.i.weighingConfirmed).length;
          return {
            rows,
            target,
            entered,
            confirmed,
            totalItems: rows.length,
            allDone: rows.length > 0 && confirmed === rows.length,
          };
        }
        function loadingTaskRows(date = workDate) {
          const rows = state.deliveries
            .filter(
              (d) =>
                d.deliveryDate === date &&
                !["cancelled", "completed"].includes(d.status),
            )
            .sort(byOrder)
            .flatMap((d) =>
              (d.items || []).filter(isWeighable).flatMap((i) =>
                (i.weighings || []).map((w) => ({
                  d,
                  i,
                  w,
                  c: customerOf(d),
                })),
              ),
            );
          let max = rows.reduce(
            (m, { w }) => Math.max(m, Number(w.taskNumber) || 0),
            0,
          );
          rows
            .filter(({ w }) => !Number(w.taskNumber))
            .sort((a, b) => String(a.w.at).localeCompare(String(b.w.at)))
            .forEach(({ w }) => (w.taskNumber = ++max));
          return rows.sort(
            (a, b) =>
              (Number(a.w.taskNumber) || 999999) -
              (Number(b.w.taskNumber) || 999999),
          );
        }
        function nextTaskNumber(date = workDate) {
          return (
            loadingTaskRows(date).reduce(
              (m, { w }) => Math.max(m, Number(w.taskNumber) || 0),
              0,
            ) + 1
          );
        }
        function taskCode(w) {
          return `#${String(Number(w?.taskNumber) || 0).padStart(3, "0")}`;
        }
        function taskBandRequired(i) {
          return Boolean(i?.rubberBand) && Number(i?.rubberBandQuantity) > 0;
        }
        function taskBandText(i) {
          return taskBandRequired(i)
            ? `${i.rubberBandColor || "색상 미입력"} ${i.rubberBandQuantity}개`
            : "밴드 없음";
        }
        function taskStatus(i, w) {
          if (w.loadedAt) return "상차 완료";
          if (w.tankVerifiedAt) return "수조 확인 완료";
          if (w.repeatConfirmedAt && (!taskBandRequired(i) || w.bandVerifiedAt))
            return "수조 확인 필요";
          if (w.repeatConfirmedAt) return "밴드 확인 필요";
          if (w.calledAt) return "복창 확인 필요";
          return "콜 대기";
        }
        function taskStepCount(i, w) {
          return [
            Boolean(w.calledAt),
            Boolean(w.repeatConfirmedAt),
            !taskBandRequired(i) || Boolean(w.bandVerifiedAt),
            Boolean(w.tankVerifiedAt),
            Boolean(w.loadedAt),
          ].filter(Boolean).length;
        }
        function loadingStats() {
          const rows = loadingTaskRows(),
            called = rows.filter(({ w }) => w.calledAt).length,
            repeated = rows.filter(({ w }) => w.repeatConfirmedAt).length,
            loaded = rows.filter(({ w }) => w.loadedAt).length;
          return {
            rows,
            called,
            repeated,
            loaded,
            total: rows.length,
            allDone: rows.length > 0 && loaded === rows.length,
          };
        }
        function findLoadingTask() {
          const d = state.deliveries.find(
              (x) => x.id === Number(loadingDeliveryId),
            ),
            i = d?.items.find((x) => x.id === Number(loadingItemId)),
            w = i?.weighings?.find((x) => x.id === Number(loadingWeightId));
          return { d, i, w, c: d ? customerOf(d) : null };
        }
        function syncItemTaskLoad(i) {
          const rows = i?.weighings || [];
          i.tankLoaded =
            Boolean(rows.length) && rows.every((w) => Boolean(w.loadedAt));
          i.tankLoadedAt = i.tankLoaded
            ? rows
                .map((w) => w.loadedAt)
                .filter(Boolean)
                .sort()
                .slice(-1)[0] || new Date().toISOString()
            : null;
          if (!i.tankLoaded) i.checked = false;
        }
        function resetTaskWorkflow(w) {
          if (!w) return;
          Object.assign(w, {
            calledAt: null,
            calledBy: "",
            repeatConfirmedAt: null,
            repeatConfirmedBy: "",
            bandVerifiedAt: null,
            bandVerifiedBy: "",
            tankVerifiedAt: null,
            tankVerifiedBy: "",
            verifiedVehicle: "",
            verifiedTank: 0,
            loadedAt: null,
            loadedBy: "",
            lastError: "",
          });
        }
        function resetAllTaskWorkflow(i) {
          (i?.weighings || []).forEach(resetTaskWorkflow);
          if (i) {
            i.tankLoaded = false;
            i.tankLoadedAt = null;
            i.checked = false;
          }
        }
        function recordTaskLog(w, type, message) {
          w.verificationLog = Array.isArray(w.verificationLog)
            ? w.verificationLog
            : [];
          w.verificationLog.push({
            id: newId(),
            type,
            message,
            at: new Date().toISOString(),
            by: state.profile.driverName || "담당자 미설정",
          });
          w.verificationLog = w.verificationLog.slice(-20);
        }
        function bandColorHex(value) {
          const v = String(value || "").toLowerCase();
          if (/빨|적|red/.test(v)) return "#e53935";
          if (/파|청|blue/.test(v)) return "#1e88e5";
          if (/노|황|yellow/.test(v)) return "#fdd835";
          if (/초|녹|green/.test(v)) return "#43a047";
          if (/검|흑|black/.test(v)) return "#212121";
          if (/분홍|핑크|pink/.test(v)) return "#ec407a";
          if (/주황|오렌지|orange/.test(v)) return "#fb8c00";
          if (/보라|자주|purple/.test(v)) return "#8e24aa";
          return "#fff";
        }
        function weightRuleFor(species) {
          const name = String(species || "").trim(),
            rules = normalizeWeightRules(state.preferences?.weightRules);
          const key = Object.keys(rules).find(
            (candidate) => name === candidate || name.includes(candidate),
          );
          const resolved = key || "기타 활어";
          return rules[resolved]
            ? { species: resolved, ...rules[resolved] }
            : null;
        }
        function abnormalWeightWarning(i, weight) {
          const rule = weightRuleFor(i?.species);
          if (!rule || (weight >= rule.min && weight <= rule.max)) return "";
          return `${i.species} 정상 중량 기준 ${rule.min}~${rule.max}kg을 벗어난 ${Number(weight).toFixed(3)}kg입니다.`;
        }
        function bandSummaryRows(date = workDate) {
          const groups = new Map();
          state.deliveries
            .filter((d) => d.deliveryDate === date && d.status !== "cancelled")
            .forEach((d) => {
              const c = customerOf(d);
              (d.items || [])
                .filter((i) => isWeighable(i) && taskBandRequired(i))
                .forEach((i) => {
                  const color = String(
                      i.rubberBandColor || "색상 미입력",
                    ).trim(),
                    qty = Math.max(1, Number(i.rubberBandQuantity) || 1),
                    plannedFish = Math.max(
                      targetFishCount(i),
                      (i.weighings || []).length,
                      1,
                    ),
                    verifiedFish = (i.weighings || []).filter(
                      (w) => w.bandVerifiedAt,
                    ).length,
                    current = groups.get(color) || {
                      color,
                      total: 0,
                      verified: 0,
                      details: [],
                    };
                  current.total += plannedFish * qty;
                  current.verified += Math.min(plannedFish, verifiedFish) * qty;
                  current.details.push({
                    store: c.name,
                    species: i.species,
                    total: plannedFish * qty,
                    verified: Math.min(plannedFish, verifiedFish) * qty,
                  });
                  groups.set(color, current);
                });
            });
          return [...groups.values()]
            .map((row) => ({
              ...row,
              remaining: Math.max(0, row.total - row.verified),
            }))
            .sort(
              (a, b) =>
                b.remaining - a.remaining ||
                a.color.localeCompare(b.color, "ko"),
            );
        }
        function errorStats(date = workDate) {
          const details = [];
          let tasks = 0,
            loaded = 0,
            tankErrors = 0,
            bandErrors = 0,
            weightWarnings = 0,
            weightEdits = 0,
            resets = 0,
            tankChanges = 0;
          state.deliveries
            .filter((d) => d.deliveryDate === date && d.status !== "cancelled")
            .forEach((d) => {
              const c = customerOf(d);
              (d.items || []).forEach((i) => {
                tankChanges += (i.tankHistory || []).length;
                (i.tankHistory || []).forEach((history) =>
                  details.push({
                    label: "수조 위치 변경",
                    store: c.name,
                    species: i.species,
                    task: "",
                    message: `${tankLabel(history.from)} → ${tankLabel(history.to)} · ${history.reason}`,
                    at: history.at,
                    by: state.profile.driverName || "",
                  }),
                );
                (i.weighings || []).forEach((w) => {
                  tasks += 1;
                  if (w.loadedAt) loaded += 1;
                  (w.verificationLog || []).forEach((log) => {
                    let label = "";
                    if (log.type === "tank-error") {
                      tankErrors += 1;
                      label = "수조 오류 방지";
                    } else if (log.type === "band-error") {
                      bandErrors += 1;
                      label = "밴드 오류 방지";
                    } else if (log.type === "weight-warning") {
                      weightWarnings += 1;
                      label = "비정상 계근 경고";
                    } else if (log.type === "weight-edit") {
                      weightEdits += 1;
                      label = "계근값 수정";
                    } else if (log.type === "reset") {
                      resets += 1;
                      label = "상차 재확인";
                    }
                    if (label)
                      details.push({
                        label,
                        store: c.name,
                        species: i.species,
                        task: taskCode(w),
                        message: log.message || label,
                        at: log.at || w.at,
                        by: log.by || "",
                      });
                  });
                });
              });
            });
          details.sort((a, b) => String(b.at).localeCompare(String(a.at)));
          return {
            tasks,
            loaded,
            tankErrors,
            bandErrors,
            weightWarnings,
            weightEdits,
            resets,
            tankChanges,
            prevented: tankErrors + bandErrors + weightWarnings,
            details,
          };
        }
        function isWorkClosed(date = workDate) {
          return Boolean(state.workClosures?.[date]);
        }
        function ensureWorkOpen() {
          if (!isWorkClosed()) return true;
          alert(
            `${workDate} 업무는 마감·보관되어 수정할 수 없습니다.\n‘업무 마감 기록’에서 마감 취소 사유를 입력하면 다시 수정할 수 있습니다.`,
          );
          return false;
        }
        function loadingSpeech(d, i, w) {
          const vehicle = state.profile.vehicleNumber || "미설정",
            band = taskBandRequired(i)
              ? `, ${i.rubberBandColor || "색상 미입력"} 밴드 ${i.rubberBandQuantity}개`
              : `, 밴드 없음`;
          return `${vehicle}호차 ${i.tankNumber || "미지정"}번 수조, ${i.species} ${Number(w.weight).toFixed(3)}킬로${band}`;
        }
        function speakText(text) {
          try {
            if (!("speechSynthesis" in window)) return false;
            speechSynthesis.cancel();
            const utterance = new SpeechSynthesisUtterance(text);
            utterance.lang = "ko-KR";
            utterance.rate = 0.86;
            utterance.pitch = 1;
            speechSynthesis.speak(utterance);
            return true;
          } catch {
            return false;
          }
        }
        function deliveryWeighingReady(d) {
          return (d.items || [])
            .filter(isWeighable)
            .every((i) => i.weighingConfirmed);
        }
        function tankLabel(value) {
          const n = Number(value) || 0;
          return n ? `${n}번 수조` : "박스·별도";
        }
        function tankRows() {
          return activeDeliveries()
            .filter((d) => d.status !== "completed")
            .flatMap((d) =>
              (d.items || []).map((i) => ({ d, i, c: customerOf(d) })),
            );
        }
        function findTankItem() {
          const d = state.deliveries.find((x) => x.id === tankDeliveryId),
            i = d?.items.find((x) => x.id === tankItemId);
          return { d, i, c: d ? customerOf(d) : null };
        }
        function urgentRows() {
          return activeDeliveries().filter(
            (d) =>
              d.status !== "completed" &&
              d.isUrgentAdditional &&
              !d.urgentAcknowledged,
          );
        }
        function tankLoadRows() {
          return tankRows().filter(({ i }) => Number(i.tankNumber) > 0);
        }
        function boxCompareRows() {
          return activeDeliveries().filter(
            (d) => d.status !== "completed" && d.boxes.length > 0,
          );
        }
        function departureIssues() {
          const issues = [],
            rows = activeDeliveries().filter((d) => d.status !== "completed");
          if (!rows.length)
            issues.push({
              type: "empty",
              title: "오늘 출차할 배송이 없습니다.",
              detail: "배송 내용을 먼저 등록해 주세요.",
            });
          rows.forEach((d) => {
            const c = customerOf(d);
            if (hasHandover(c) && !handoverAcknowledged(d, c))
              issues.push({
                type: "handover",
                d,
                title: `${c.name} 점포 특이사항 미확인`,
                detail: "출입 방법·물건 위치·금지사항을 확인해 주세요.",
              });
            if (d.isUrgentAdditional && !d.urgentAcknowledged)
              issues.push({
                type: "urgent",
                d,
                title: `${c.name} 긴급 추가 발주 미확인`,
                detail: "추가 품목과 수조·배송 순서를 확인해 주세요.",
              });
            else if (d.status === "new")
              issues.push({
                type: "new",
                d,
                title: `${c.name} 신규 발주 미확인`,
                detail: "신규 발주 접수 확인이 필요합니다.",
              });
            d.items.forEach((i) => {
              const tasks = i.weighings || [],
                workflowIncomplete =
                  isWeighable(i) &&
                  tasks.length &&
                  tasks.some((w) => !w.loadedAt);
              if (isWeighable(i) && !i.weighingConfirmed)
                issues.push({
                  type: "weigh",
                  d,
                  i,
                  title: `${c.name} ${i.species} 계근 미확정`,
                  detail: "개별 계근값과 합계를 확정해 주세요.",
                });
              if (isWeighable(i) && !i.tankNumber)
                issues.push({
                  type: "tank",
                  d,
                  i,
                  title: `${c.name} ${i.species} 수조 미지정`,
                  detail: "1~6번 수조를 지정해 주세요.",
                });
              if (
                i.rubberBand &&
                (!String(i.rubberBandColor || "").trim() ||
                  Number(i.rubberBandQuantity) <= 0)
              )
                issues.push({
                  type: "band",
                  d,
                  i,
                  title: `${c.name} ${i.species} 밴드 지시 미완성`,
                  detail: "밴드 색상과 수량을 정확하게 입력해 주세요.",
                });
              if (workflowIncomplete)
                issues.push({
                  type: "workflow",
                  d,
                  i,
                  title: `${c.name} ${i.species} 상차 관제 미완료`,
                  detail: `콜·복창·밴드·${tankLabel(i.tankNumber)} 확인이 끝나지 않았습니다.`,
                });
              else if (i.tankNumber && !i.tankLoaded)
                issues.push({
                  type: "load",
                  d,
                  i,
                  title: `${c.name} ${i.species} 실제 상차 미확인`,
                  detail: `${tankLabel(i.tankNumber)}에 실제로 넣었는지 확인해 주세요.`,
                });
              if (Number(i.unitPrice) <= 0)
                issues.push({
                  type: "price",
                  d,
                  i,
                  title: `${c.name} ${i.species} 단가 미입력`,
                  detail: "거래명세서 확정 단가를 입력해 주세요.",
                });
            });
            if (d.boxes.length && !d.boxCountConfirmed)
              issues.push({
                type: "box",
                d,
                title: `${c.name} 박스 수량 미확인`,
                detail: `계획 ${d.boxes.length}박스와 실제 상차 수량을 대조해 주세요.`,
              });
            else if (d.boxes.length && d.loadedBoxCount !== d.boxes.length)
              issues.push({
                type: "box",
                d,
                title: `${c.name} 박스 수량 불일치`,
                detail: `계획 ${d.boxes.length}박스 / 실제 ${d.loadedBoxCount}박스입니다.`,
              });
          });
          return issues;
        }
        function departureFingerprint() {
          return JSON.stringify({
            driver: state.profile.driverName || "",
            vehicle: state.profile.vehicleNumber || "",
            deliveries: activeDeliveries()
              .filter((d) => d.status !== "completed")
              .map((d) => {
                const c = customerOf(d);
                return {
                  id: d.id,
                  customerId: d.customerId,
                  status: d.status,
                  route: d.routeOrder,
                  urgent: d.isUrgentAdditional,
                  urgentOk: d.urgentAcknowledged,
                  handoverVersion: hasHandover(c) ? handoverVersion(c) : "",
                  handoverAck: d.handoverAcknowledgedVersion || "",
                  handoverBy: d.handoverAcknowledgedBy || "",
                  handoverVehicle: d.handoverAcknowledgedVehicle || "",
                  previousBalance: d.previousBalance,
                  loadedBoxes: d.loadedBoxCount,
                  boxOk: d.boxCountConfirmed,
                  boxes: d.boxes.map((b) => ({
                    id: b.id,
                    contents: b.contents,
                  })),
                  items: d.items.map((i) => ({
                    id: i.id,
                    category: i.category,
                    species: i.species,
                    size: i.size,
                    origin: i.originCountry,
                    qty: i.requestedQty,
                    unit: i.unit,
                    weight: i.actualWeight,
                    price: i.unitPrice,
                    processing: i.processing,
                    processingFee: i.processingFeePerKg,
                    tank: i.tankNumber,
                    tankLoaded: i.tankLoaded,
                    weighOk: i.weighingConfirmed,
                    band: i.rubberBand
                      ? `${i.rubberBandColor}-${i.rubberBandQuantity}`
                      : "",
                    note: i.includedNote,
                    tasks: (i.weighings || []).map((w) => ({
                      id: w.id,
                      no: w.taskNumber,
                      called: w.calledAt,
                      repeat: w.repeatConfirmedAt,
                      band: w.bandVerifiedAt,
                      tank: w.tankVerifiedAt,
                      actualTank: w.verifiedTank,
                      loaded: w.loadedAt,
                    })),
                  })),
                };
              }),
          });
        }
        function departureReady() {
          const record = state.departureChecks?.[workDate];
          return Boolean(
            record &&
              record.fingerprint === departureFingerprint() &&
              !departureIssues().length,
          );
        }
        function progress(d) {
          const all = [...(d.items || []), ...(d.boxes || [])];
          return {
            done: all.filter((x) => x.checked).length,
            total: all.length,
          };
        }
        function statusLabel(status) {
          return (
            {
              new: "신규 발주",
              ready: "배송 준비",
              completed: "배송 완료",
              cancelled: "발주 취소",
            }[status] || status
          );
        }
        function renderHeader() {
          $("#companyHeader").textContent =
            state.profile.companyName || "회사 정보 설정";
          $("#driverHeader").textContent =
            `${state.profile.vehicleNumber ? state.profile.vehicleNumber + "호차" : "호차 미설정"} · ${state.profile.driverName || "담당자 미설정"}`;
          $("#workDate").value = workDate;
        }
        function setView(next) {
          view = next;
          document
            .querySelectorAll("nav button")
            .forEach((b) =>
              b.classList.toggle("active", b.dataset.nav === view),
            );
          $("#todayView").classList.toggle("hidden", view !== "today");
          $("#customersView").classList.toggle("hidden", view !== "customers");
          $("#settingsView").classList.toggle("hidden", view !== "settings");
          render();
        }
        function render() {
          renderHeader();
          if (view === "today") renderToday();
          if (view === "customers") renderCustomers();
          if (view === "settings") renderSettings();
        }

        function renderToday() {
          const rows = deliveries(),
            active = rows.filter((d) => d.status !== "cancelled"),
            unfinished = active.filter((d) => d.status !== "completed"),
            newCount = active.filter((d) => d.status === "new").length,
            ready = active.filter((d) => d.status === "ready").length,
            done = active.filter((d) => d.status === "completed").length,
            ws = weighingStats(),
            ls = loadingStats(),
            urgent = urgentRows(),
            issues = departureIssues(),
            departOk = departureReady(),
            loads = tankLoadRows(),
            loadedCount = loads.filter(({ i }) => i.tankLoaded).length,
            boxRows = boxCompareRows(),
            boxOkCount = boxRows.filter(
              (d) => d.boxCountConfirmed && d.loadedBoxCount === d.boxes.length,
            ).length,
            departureRecord = state.departureChecks?.[workDate],
            closed = isWorkClosed(),
            closure = state.workClosures?.[workDate],
            bands = bandSummaryRows(),
            bandRemaining = bands.reduce((sum, row) => sum + row.remaining, 0),
            errors = errorStats();
          const tankHtml = Array.from({ length: 6 }, (_, idx) => {
            const n = idx + 1,
              tankItems = unfinished.flatMap((d) =>
                (d.items || [])
                  .filter((i) => Number(i.tankNumber) === n)
                  .map((i) => ({ d, i, c: customerOf(d) })),
              ),
              items = tankItems
                .map(({ d, i, c }) => {
                  const tasks = i.weighings || [],
                    taskDone = tasks.filter((w) => w.loadedAt).length;
                  return `<button class="tank-drag-item ${i.tankLoaded ? "loaded" : ""}" type="button" data-action="open-tank-info" data-tank="${n}" data-drag-tank-item data-delivery-id="${d.id}" data-item-id="${i.id}" data-source-tank="${n}" aria-label="${esc(c.name)} ${esc(i.species)}. 길게 눌러 수조 이동"><strong>${i.tankLoaded ? "✓" : "○"} ${esc(c.name)}</strong><small>${esc(i.species)} · ${esc(quantityText(i))}${tasks.length ? ` · 개체상차 ${taskDone}/${tasks.length}` : ""}</small></button>`;
                })
                .join("");
            return `<article class="tank ${tankItems.length ? "" : "empty-tank"}" data-tank-drop="${n}"><button class="tank-open" type="button" data-action="open-tank-info" data-tank="${n}"><strong>${n}번 수조</strong><small>눌러서 상세 정보 보기</small></button><div class="tank-item-list">${items || `<span class="tank-empty-text">비어 있음</span>`}</div><small class="tank-tap-hint">${tankItems.length ? "품목을 길게 눌러 다른 수조로 이동" : "품목을 이곳에 놓을 수 있습니다"}</small></article>`;
          }).join("");
          const routeRows = rows.filter((d) => d.status !== "cancelled");
          const stops = rows.length
            ? rows
                .map((d) =>
                  renderStop(
                    d,
                    routeRows.findIndex((x) => x.id === d.id),
                    routeRows,
                  ),
                )
                .join("")
            : `<div class="empty">등록된 배송이 없습니다.<br>점주 앱에서 발주하면 자동으로 표시됩니다.</div>`;
          $("#todayView").innerHTML =
            `${centralPanelHTML()}<div class="stats"><div class="stat new"><small>신규 발주</small><strong>${newCount}</strong></div><div class="stat"><small>배송 준비</small><strong>${ready}</strong></div><div class="stat done"><small>배송 완료</small><strong>${done}</strong></div></div>${closed ? `<div class="closed-day-banner"><div><strong>✓ ${esc(workDate)} 업무 마감·보관 완료</strong><small>${closure?.at ? new Date(closure.at).toLocaleString("ko-KR") : ""} · ${esc(closure?.by || "담당자 미설정")}</small></div><button type="button" data-action="open-work-close">마감 기록</button></div>` : ""}${urgent.length ? `<div class="urgent-hero"><div><h2>🚨 긴급 추가 발주 ${urgent.length}건</h2><p>추가 품목·수조·배송 순서를 먼저 확인하세요.</p></div><button type="button" data-action="open-urgent">긴급 발주 확인</button></div>` : ""}<div class="departure-hero ${departOk ? "ready" : ""}"><div><h2>${departOk ? "✓ 출차 준비 완료" : "🚚 출차 전 최종 점검"}</h2><p>${departOk ? `${departureRecord?.at ? new Date(departureRecord.at).toLocaleString("ko-KR") : ""} 점검 완료` : `미확인·불일치 ${issues.length}건을 확인해야 출차 준비가 완료됩니다.`}</p></div><button type="button" data-action="open-departure">${departOk ? "점검 결과 보기" : "최종 점검 시작"}</button></div><div class="quick-actions"><button class="excel" type="button" data-action="export-excel" ${active.length ? "" : "disabled"}>📊 당일 Excel 저장</button><button class="purchase" type="button" data-action="open-purchase" ${unfinished.length ? "" : "disabled"}>📋 당일 매입발주서</button><button class="excel" type="button" data-action="open-tank-manager" ${tankRows().length ? "" : "disabled"}>💧 수조 상차 ${loadedCount}/${loads.length}</button><button class="purchase" type="button" data-action="open-box-compare" ${boxRows.length ? "" : "disabled"}>📦 박스 대조 ${boxOkCount}/${boxRows.length}</button></div><div class="weigh-hero ${ws.allDone ? "complete" : ""}"><div><h2>⚖️ 호차 활어 계근</h2><p>${ws.totalItems ? `활어 ${ws.entered}/${ws.target || "-"}마리 입력 · ${ws.confirmed}/${ws.totalItems}품목 확정` : `오늘 계근할 활어가 없습니다.`}</p></div><button type="button" data-action="open-weigh-list" ${ws.totalItems ? "" : "disabled"}>${ws.allDone ? "계근 완료 확인" : "계근 시작"}</button></div><div class="loading-hero ${ls.allDone ? "ready" : ""}"><div><h2>${ls.allDone ? "✓ 개체별 상차 관제 완료" : "📣 실시간 상차 오류 방지"}</h2><p>${ls.total ? `콜 ${ls.called}/${ls.total} · 복창 ${ls.repeated}/${ls.total} · 수조 상차 ${ls.loaded}/${ls.total}` : "계근값이 입력되면 활어 한 마리별 작업번호가 생성됩니다."}</p></div><button type="button" data-action="open-loading-control" ${ls.total ? "" : "disabled"}>${ls.allDone ? "완료 내역" : "상차 관제 시작"}</button></div><div class="dashboard-tools"><button type="button" data-action="open-band-summary">🎨 밴드 현황 · 남음 ${bandRemaining}개</button><button type="button" data-action="open-error-stats">📈 오류 방지 ${errors.prevented}건</button><button type="button" data-action="open-weight-rules">⚖️ 비정상 계근 기준</button><button class="close-day ${closed ? "closed" : ""}" type="button" data-action="open-work-close">${closed ? "✓ 업무 마감 기록" : "📁 오늘 업무 마감·보관"}</button></div><section class="section"><div class="heading"><div><h2>1~6번 수조 현황</h2><p>품목 카드는 길게 눌러 원하는 수조로 끌어 놓으세요. 수조 제목을 누르면 상세 정보가 열립니다.</p></div><button class="mini tank-change-button" type="button" data-action="open-tank-manager" ${tankRows().length ? "" : "disabled"}>전체 상차 관리</button></div><div class="tank-grid">${tankHtml}</div></section><section class="section"><div class="heading"><div><h2>배송 순서</h2><p>거래처를 눌러 하차 물품을 확인하세요.</p></div><div class="heading-actions">${rows.length ? `<button class="mini" type="button" data-action="toggle-reorder">${reorderMode ? "순서 저장 완료" : "순서·삭제"}</button>` : ""}<button class="mini primary" type="button" data-action="new-delivery" ${state.customers.length ? "" : "disabled"}>＋ 수동 추가</button></div></div><div class="stop-list">${stops}</div></section>`;
        }
        function renderStop(d, index, rows) {
          const c = customerOf(d),
            p = progress(d),
            names = (d.items || [])
              .map((i) => i.species)
              .slice(0, 3)
              .join(" · ");
          if (d.status === "cancelled")
            return `<article class="stop cancelled"><div class="stop-main"><span class="order-badge">×</span><span class="stop-copy"><span class="status-tag" style="background:var(--red)">발주 취소</span><strong>${esc(c.name)}</strong><small>절대 상차하거나 배송하지 마세요.</small></span></div><div class="stop-actions"><button class="ack-button" type="button" data-action="ack-cancel" data-id="${d.id}">취소 확인 · 목록에서 삭제</button></div></article>`;
          if (reorderMode)
            return `<article class="stop"><div class="reorder-row"><span class="order-badge">${d.routeOrder}</span><strong>${esc(c.name)}</strong><select aria-label="${esc(c.name)} 배송 순서" data-action="route-position" data-id="${d.id}">${rows.map((_, i) => `<option value="${i + 1}" ${i === index ? "selected" : ""}>${i + 1}번</option>`).join("")}</select><button type="button" data-action="move-up" data-id="${d.id}" ${index === 0 ? "disabled" : ""}>↑</button><button type="button" data-action="move-down" data-id="${d.id}" ${index === rows.length - 1 ? "disabled" : ""}>↓</button></div><div style="padding:0 12px 12px"><button class="full-button danger-button delete-route" type="button" data-action="delete-delivery" data-id="${d.id}">배송 삭제</button></div></article>`;
          const mapUrl = `https://map.kakao.com/link/search/${encodeURIComponent(c.address || c.name)}`,
            hasLive = (d.items || []).some(isWeighable),
            weighReady = deliveryWeighingReady(d),
            tankItems = (d.items || []).filter((i) => i.tankNumber),
            tankReady = tankItems.every((i) => i.tankLoaded),
            boxReady =
              !d.boxes.length ||
              (d.boxCountConfirmed && d.loadedBoxCount === d.boxes.length),
            guideExists = hasHandover(c),
            guideOk = handoverAcknowledged(d, c);
          return `<article class="stop ${d.status === "new" ? "new-order" : ""} ${d.status === "completed" ? "completed" : ""}"><button class="stop-main" type="button" data-action="open-check" data-id="${d.id}"><span class="order-badge">${d.routeOrder}</span><span class="stop-copy">${d.isUrgentAdditional ? `<span class="status-tag" style="background:${d.urgentAcknowledged ? "var(--green)" : "var(--red)"}">긴급 추가 발주 · ${d.urgentAcknowledged ? "확인 완료" : "확인 필요"}</span>` : d.status === "new" ? `<span class="status-tag">새 발주 · 확인 필요</span>` : ""}${guideExists ? `<span class="status-tag" style="background:${guideOk ? "var(--green)" : "#7650a8"}">점포 인계 ${guideOk ? "확인 완료" : "확인 필요"}</span>` : ""}${hasLive ? `<span class="status-tag" style="background:${weighReady ? "var(--green)" : "#1976a3"}">계근 ${weighReady ? "확정" : "필요"}</span>` : ""}${tankItems.length ? `<span class="status-tag" style="background:${tankReady ? "var(--green)" : "#1976a3"}">수조 ${tankReady ? "상차완료" : "상차확인"}</span>` : ""}${d.boxes.length ? `<span class="status-tag" style="background:${boxReady ? "var(--green)" : "#8c5a12"}">박스 ${boxReady ? "일치" : "대조필요"}</span>` : ""}<strong>${esc(c.name)}</strong><small>${esc(names || "품목 없음")} · ${d.boxes.length}박스</small></span><span class="progress">${p.done}/${p.total}</span></button><div class="stop-actions"><a href="${mapUrl}" target="_blank" rel="noopener">🗺️ 길찾기</a><button type="button" data-action="open-check" data-id="${d.id}">📦 하차 확인</button>${guideExists ? `<button class="handover-stop-button" type="button" data-action="open-store-guide" data-id="${d.id}" data-source="today">📝 점포 특이사항 ${guideOk ? "보기" : "확인 필요"}</button>` : ""}${d.status === "new" || (d.isUrgentAdditional && !d.urgentAcknowledged) ? `<button class="ack-button" style="background:${d.isUrgentAdditional ? "var(--red)" : "var(--amber)"}!important" type="button" data-action="${d.isUrgentAdditional ? "ack-urgent-order" : "ack-order"}" data-id="${d.id}">${d.isUrgentAdditional ? "🚨 긴급 추가 발주·순서 확인 완료" : "✓ 신규 발주 접수 확인"}</button>` : ""}</div></article>`;
        }

        function renderCustomers() {
          const list = customers();
          $("#customersView").innerHTML =
            `<div class="heading"><div><h2>거래처 관리</h2><p>주소·연락처와 점포별 인수인계 정보를 관리합니다.</p></div><button class="mini primary" type="button" data-action="new-customer">＋ 추가</button></div><div class="customer-list">${
              list.length
                ? list
                    .map((c, i) => {
                      const count = handoverFields(c).filter(Boolean).length;
                      return `<article class="customer-row"><span class="order-badge">${i + 1}</span><span><strong>${esc(c.name)}</strong><small>${esc(c.deliveryPlace || c.address || "주소 미입력")}</small><span class="handover-mini ${count ? "ready" : ""}">${count ? `인수인계 ${count}항목 등록` : "인수인계 미등록"}</span></span><button type="button" data-action="edit-customer" data-id="${c.id}">수정</button></article>`;
                    })
                    .join("")
                : `<div class="empty">등록된 거래처가 없습니다.</div>`
            }</div>`;
        }
        function renderSettings() {
          const saved = localStorage.getItem(LAST_SAVED_KEY);
          $("#settingsView").innerHTML =
            `<div class="heading"><div><h2>내 계정·업무 설정</h2><p>이름과 호차는 관리자가 배정하며 배송원이 변경할 수 없습니다.</p></div></div><form id="settingsForm" class="settings-card"><div class="assigned-profile"><strong>✓ 관리자 배정 정보</strong><small>${esc(assignedDriverProfile?.employee_code || "-")} · ${esc(state.profile.driverName)} · ${esc(state.profile.vehicleNumber)}호차</small></div><label class="field"><span>회사명</span><input class="control" name="companyName" value="${esc(state.profile.companyName)}" readonly required></label><label class="field"><span>배송담당자 이름</span><input class="control" name="driverName" value="${esc(state.profile.driverName)}" readonly required></label><label class="field"><span>관리자 배정 호차</span><input class="control" name="vehicleNumber" value="${esc(state.profile.vehicleNumber)}" readonly required></label><label class="setting-toggle"><input name="autoNextLoading" type="checkbox" ${state.preferences?.autoNextLoading !== false ? "checked" : ""}><span>상차 완료 후 다음 미완료 활어를 자동으로 열기</span></label><button class="full-button primary-button" type="submit">개인 업무 설정 저장</button><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="open-weight-rules">⚖️ 어종별 정상 중량 기준 설정</button><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="open-qr-labels">🏷️ 내 호차 1~6번 수조 QR 라벨</button><div class="notice">휴대폰과 중앙 서버에 업무 자료를 함께 저장합니다.<br>최근 저장: ${saved ? esc(new Date(saved).toLocaleString("ko-KR")) : "저장 기록 없음"}</div><button class="full-button warning-button" type="button" data-action="open-backups">🛟 자동 백업 확인·복구</button><div class="backup-grid"><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="backup">백업 파일 저장</button><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="restore">백업 파일 복원</button></div><button class="full-button danger-button" type="button" data-action="driver-logout">배송원 로그아웃</button></form>`;
        }

        function openBandSummary() {
          const rows = bandSummaryRows(),
            total = rows.reduce((sum, row) => sum + row.total, 0),
            verified = rows.reduce((sum, row) => sum + row.verified, 0),
            body = rows
              .map(
                (row) =>
                  `<article class="band-summary-row ${row.remaining ? "" : "done"}"><span class="band-swatch" style="background:${bandColorHex(row.color)}"></span><div><strong>${esc(row.color)} 밴드</strong><small>${esc(row.details.map((d) => `${d.store} ${d.species} ${d.verified}/${d.total}`).join(" · "))}</small></div><b>${row.remaining ? `남음 ${row.remaining}개` : "완료"}</b></article>`,
              )
              .join("");
          $("#bandModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>🎨 ${esc(workDate)} 밴드 작업 현황</h2><p>색상별 준비 수량과 실물 확인 완료 수량입니다.</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-band-summary">×</button></div><div class="modal-body"><div class="loading-summary"><div><small>준비 수량</small><strong>${total}</strong></div><div><small>확인 완료</small><strong>${verified}</strong></div><div><small>남은 수량</small><strong>${Math.max(0, total - verified)}</strong></div><div><small>사용 색상</small><strong>${rows.length}</strong></div></div><div class="senior-guide"><b>확인 방법</b>밴드를 미리 색상별로 준비하고, 활어 꼬리에 작업한 뒤 개체 상차 화면에서 ‘밴드 일치’를 누르세요.</div><div class="band-summary-list">${body || `<div class="empty">오늘 밴드 작업 지시가 없습니다.</div>`}</div><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="close-band-summary">배송 화면으로 돌아가기</button></div></div>`;
          $("#bandModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function openWeightRules() {
          const rules = normalizeWeightRules(state.preferences?.weightRules),
            rows = Object.entries(rules)
              .map(
                ([species, rule]) =>
                  `<div class="weight-rule-row"><strong>${esc(species)}</strong><label>최소 kg<input type="number" inputmode="decimal" min="0.001" step="0.001" name="min_${esc(species)}" value="${rule.min}" required></label><label>최대 kg<input type="number" inputmode="decimal" min="0.001" step="0.001" name="max_${esc(species)}" value="${rule.max}" required></label></div>`,
              )
              .join("");
          $("#weightRuleModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>⚖️ 어종별 정상 중량 기준</h2><p>한 마리 계근값이 범위를 벗어나면 저장 전에 큰 경고가 나옵니다.</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-weight-rules">×</button></div><form id="weightRulesForm" class="modal-body"><div class="weigh-notice">현장 규격에 맞게 최소·최대 kg을 수정하세요. 범위를 벗어난 값도 담당자가 확인하면 저장할 수 있으며 경고 기록이 남습니다.</div><div class="weight-rule-list">${rows}</div><button class="full-button primary-button sticky-save" type="submit">정상 중량 기준 저장</button><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="reset-weight-rules">기본 기준으로 되돌리기</button></form></div>`;
          $("#weightRuleModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function saveWeightRules(form) {
          const fd = new FormData(form),
            next = {};
          for (const [species, defaults] of Object.entries(
            DEFAULT_WEIGHT_RULES,
          )) {
            const min = Number(fd.get(`min_${species}`)),
              max = Number(fd.get(`max_${species}`));
            if (!Number.isFinite(min) || !Number.isFinite(max) || min <= 0)
              return alert(`${species} 최소 중량을 확인해 주세요.`);
            if (max < min)
              return alert(`${species} 최대 중량은 최소 중량보다 커야 합니다.`);
            next[species] = { min, max };
          }
          state.preferences = state.preferences || {};
          state.preferences.weightRules = normalizeWeightRules(next);
          saveState("어종별 정상 중량 기준 변경 전");
          closeModal("weightRuleModal");
          if (view === "settings") renderSettings();
          alert("어종별 정상 중량 기준을 저장했습니다.");
        }
        function openErrorStats() {
          const stats = errorStats(),
            details = stats.details
              .map(
                (row) =>
                  `<article class="error-detail-row"><strong>${esc(row.label)} · ${esc(row.store)} ${esc(row.species)} ${esc(row.task)}</strong><small>${esc(row.message)}<br>${row.at ? esc(new Date(row.at).toLocaleString("ko-KR")) : ""}${row.by ? ` · ${esc(row.by)}` : ""}</small></article>`,
              )
              .join("");
          $("#statsModal").innerHTML =
