            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>📈 ${esc(workDate)} 오류·예방 통계</h2><p>현장에서 발견하고 바로잡은 기록을 자동 집계합니다.</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-error-stats">×</button></div><div class="modal-body"><div class="error-stat-grid"><div><small>수조 오류 방지</small><strong>${stats.tankErrors}건</strong></div><div><small>밴드 오류 방지</small><strong>${stats.bandErrors}건</strong></div><div><small>비정상 계근 경고</small><strong>${stats.weightWarnings}건</strong></div><div><small>수조 위치 변경</small><strong>${stats.tankChanges}건</strong></div><div><small>상차 재확인</small><strong>${stats.resets}건</strong></div><div><small>개체 상차 완료</small><strong>${stats.loaded}/${stats.tasks}</strong></div></div><div class="senior-guide"><b>오늘 프로그램이 막은 오류</b>수조·밴드·계근 이상을 합쳐 ${stats.prevented}건을 출차 전에 확인했습니다.</div><div class="error-detail-list">${details || `<div class="empty">오늘 기록된 오류가 없습니다.</div>`}</div><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="close-error-stats">배송 화면으로 돌아가기</button></div></div>`;
          $("#statsModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function openWorkClosure() {
          const rows = deliveries().filter((d) => d.status !== "cancelled"),
            completed = rows.filter((d) => d.status === "completed").length,
            closure = state.workClosures?.[workDate],
            stats = closure?.stats || errorStats(),
            history = (state.workClosureHistory || [])
              .filter((row) => row.date === workDate)
              .slice(-8)
              .reverse()
              .map(
                (row) =>
                  `<div class="workflow-log">${esc(new Date(row.at).toLocaleString("ko-KR"))} · ${esc(row.by || "담당자 미설정")}<br>${row.type === "reopen" ? `마감 취소: ${esc(row.reason)}` : "업무 마감·보관 완료"}</div>`,
              )
              .join("");
          $("#closeDayModal").innerHTML = closure
            ? `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>📁 업무 마감 기록</h2><p>${esc(workDate)} 자료는 수정 잠금 상태입니다.</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-work-close">×</button></div><div class="modal-body"><div class="departure-ready-card"><div class="icon">✓</div><h2>업무 마감·보관 완료</h2><p>${esc(new Date(closure.at).toLocaleString("ko-KR"))}</p><p>${esc(closure.by || "담당자 미설정")} · ${esc(closure.vehicle || "-")}호차</p></div><div class="error-stat-grid"><div><small>배송 완료</small><strong>${closure.completedCount}/${closure.deliveryCount}</strong></div><div><small>오류 방지</small><strong>${stats.prevented || 0}건</strong></div><div><small>상차 완료</small><strong>${stats.loaded || 0}/${stats.tasks || 0}</strong></div><div><small>밴드 남음</small><strong>${closure.bandRemaining || 0}개</strong></div></div>${history}<button class="full-button warning-button" type="button" data-action="reopen-work-day">마감 취소 · 다시 수정</button><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="close-work-close">닫기</button></div></div>`
            : `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>📁 오늘 업무 마감·보관</h2><p>마감하면 오늘 자료가 잠기고 자동 백업이 남습니다.</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-work-close">×</button></div><div class="modal-body"><div class="loading-summary"><div><small>전체 배송</small><strong>${rows.length}</strong></div><div><small>배송 완료</small><strong>${completed}</strong></div><div><small>미완료</small><strong>${Math.max(0, rows.length - completed)}</strong></div><div><small>오류 방지</small><strong>${stats.prevented}</strong></div></div>${rows.length && completed === rows.length ? `<div class="weigh-ready">✓ 모든 배송이 완료되어 마감할 수 있습니다.</div>` : `<div class="weigh-notice">모든 배송의 하차 완료를 확인해야 업무를 마감할 수 있습니다.</div>`}<button class="full-button primary-button" type="button" data-action="close-work-day" ${rows.length && completed === rows.length ? "" : "disabled"}>오늘 업무 마감·자동 백업</button><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="close-work-close">취소</button></div></div>`;
          $("#closeDayModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function closeWorkDay() {
          if (isWorkClosed()) return openWorkClosure();
          const rows = deliveries().filter((d) => d.status !== "cancelled"),
            completed = rows.filter((d) => d.status === "completed").length;
          if (!rows.length || completed !== rows.length)
            return alert("모든 배송의 하차 완료를 먼저 확인해 주세요.");
          if (
            !confirm(
              `${workDate} 업무를 마감할까요?\n마감 후에는 자료가 잠기며, 사유를 입력해야 다시 수정할 수 있습니다.`,
            )
          )
            return;
          saveAutoSnapshot(JSON.stringify(state), "당일 업무 마감 직전");
          const stats = errorStats(),
            bandRemaining = bandSummaryRows().reduce(
              (sum, row) => sum + row.remaining,
              0,
            ),
            record = {
              id: newId(),
              date: workDate,
              at: new Date().toISOString(),
              by: state.profile.driverName || "담당자 미설정",
              vehicle: state.profile.vehicleNumber || "",
              deliveryCount: rows.length,
              completedCount: completed,
              bandRemaining,
              stats,
            };
          state.workClosures = state.workClosures || {};
          state.workClosures[workDate] = record;
          state.workClosureHistory = state.workClosureHistory || [];
          state.workClosureHistory.push({
            type: "close",
            date: workDate,
            at: record.at,
            by: record.by,
          });
          state.workClosureHistory = state.workClosureHistory.slice(-200);
          saveState("당일 업무 마감 전");
          renderToday();
          openWorkClosure();
        }
        function reopenWorkDay() {
          const closure = state.workClosures?.[workDate];
          if (!closure) return;
          const reason = prompt(
            "마감을 취소하고 다시 수정하는 이유를 입력해 주세요.\n예: 오배송 확인으로 거래명세 수정",
            "",
          );
          if (reason === null) return;
          if (!String(reason).trim())
            return alert("마감 취소 사유를 반드시 입력해 주세요.");
          state.workClosureHistory = state.workClosureHistory || [];
          state.workClosureHistory.push({
            type: "reopen",
            date: workDate,
            at: new Date().toISOString(),
            by: state.profile.driverName || "담당자 미설정",
            reason: String(reason).trim(),
          });
          delete state.workClosures[workDate];
          saveState("업무 마감 취소 전");
          closeModal("closeDayModal");
          renderToday();
          alert(
            "업무 마감을 취소했습니다. 오늘 자료를 다시 수정할 수 있습니다.",
          );
        }

        function openSetup() {
          const p = state.profile;
          $("#setupModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>회사·차량 최초 설정</h2><p>처음 한 번만 입력하면 자동 저장됩니다.</p></div></div><form id="setupForm" class="modal-body"><label class="field"><span>회사명</span><input class="control" name="companyName" value="${esc(p.companyName)}" placeholder="예: 장백수산" required></label><label class="field"><span>배송담당자 이름</span><input class="control" name="driverName" value="${esc(p.driverName)}" required></label><label class="field"><span>차량 호차·연동 코드</span><input class="control" name="vehicleNumber" value="${esc(p.vehicleNumber)}" placeholder="예: 1" required></label><button class="full-button primary-button" type="submit">설정 저장하고 시작</button></form></div>`;
          $("#setupModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function openCustomer(id) {
          customerEditId = id || null;
          const c =
              state.customers.find((x) => x.id === id) ||
              normalizeCustomer({ routeOrder: customers().length + 1 }),
            updated = c.handoverUpdatedAt
              ? `${new Date(c.handoverUpdatedAt).toLocaleString("ko-KR")} · ${c.handoverUpdatedBy || "작성자 미입력"}`
              : "아직 작성된 인수인계 정보가 없습니다.";
          $("#formModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>${id ? "거래처 수정" : "거래처 등록"}</h2><p>거래처 정보와 다음 배송원에게 전달할 내용을 입력합니다.</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-modal">×</button></div><form id="customerForm" class="modal-body"><label class="field"><span>거래처명</span><input class="control" name="name" value="${esc(c.name)}" required></label><label class="field"><span>납품처</span><input class="control" name="deliveryPlace" value="${esc(c.deliveryPlace || "")}"></label><label class="field"><span>주소</span><textarea class="control" name="address">${esc(c.address || "")}</textarea></label><label class="field"><span>연락처</span><input class="control" name="phone" type="tel" value="${esc(c.phone || "")}"></label><label class="field"><span>기본 배송순서</span><input class="control" name="routeOrder" type="number" min="1" value="${c.routeOrder}"></label><section class="handover-form-section"><h3>📝 점포 인수인계·특이사항</h3><p>내용이 바뀌면 배송 화면에 다시 확인하라는 표시가 자동으로 나타납니다.</p><label class="field"><span>매장 입고 가능 시간</span><input class="control" name="receivingTime" value="${esc(c.receivingTime)}" placeholder="예: 오전 7시 이전 / 월요일 8시 이후"></label><label class="field"><span>출입 비밀번호·공동현관 번호</span><div class="secret-edit-row"><input id="customerAccessPassword" class="control" name="accessPassword" type="password" autocomplete="off" value="${esc(c.accessPassword)}" placeholder="필요한 경우에만 입력"><button type="button" data-action="toggle-form-secret">보기</button></div></label><label class="field"><span>매장 진입 방법</span><textarea class="control" name="entryMethod" placeholder="예: 건물 뒤편 주차장 입구 → 왼쪽 계단 이용">${esc(c.entryMethod)}</textarea></label><label class="field"><span>물건 놓는 자리</span><textarea class="control" name="dropLocation" placeholder="예: 주방 안쪽 냉장고 앞 파란 팔레트">${esc(c.dropLocation)}</textarea></label><label class="field"><span>절대 하지 말아야 할 사항</span><textarea class="control" name="deliveryCautions" placeholder="예: 정문 사용 금지 / 오전 8시 이후 벨 누르지 않기">${esc(c.deliveryCautions)}</textarea></label><label class="field"><span>주차·엘리베이터 정보</span><textarea class="control" name="parkingInfo" placeholder="예: 지하 2층 15분 무료 / 화물 엘리베이터 사용">${esc(c.parkingInfo)}</textarea></label><label class="field"><span>그 밖의 인수인계 메모</span><textarea class="control" name="handoverNote" placeholder="점포 담당자 성향, 반품 위치 등 추가 전달 내용">${esc(c.handoverNote)}</textarea></label><div class="guide-meta">최근 수정: ${esc(updated)}</div></section><button class="full-button primary-button sticky-save" type="submit">거래처·인수인계 저장</button>${id ? `<button class="full-button danger-button" type="button" data-action="delete-customer" data-id="${id}">거래처 삭제</button>` : ""}</form></div>`;
          $("#formModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function saveCustomer(form) {
          const fd = Object.fromEntries(new FormData(form)),
            desired = Math.max(1, Number(fd.routeOrder) || 1),
            old = customerEditId
              ? state.customers.find((c) => c.id === customerEditId)
              : null,
            value = {
              name: String(fd.name || "").trim(),
              deliveryPlace: String(fd.deliveryPlace || "").trim(),
              address: String(fd.address || "").trim(),
              phone: String(fd.phone || "").trim(),
              routeOrder: desired,
              accessPassword: String(fd.accessPassword || "").trim(),
              entryMethod: String(fd.entryMethod || "").trim(),
              dropLocation: String(fd.dropLocation || "").trim(),
              deliveryCautions: String(fd.deliveryCautions || "").trim(),
              receivingTime: String(fd.receivingTime || "").trim(),
              parkingInfo: String(fd.parkingInfo || "").trim(),
              handoverNote: String(fd.handoverNote || "").trim(),
            },
            changed =
              !old ||
              handoverFields(old).join("\n") !==
                handoverFields(value).join("\n");
          value.handoverUpdatedAt = changed
            ? new Date().toISOString()
            : old?.handoverUpdatedAt || null;
          value.handoverUpdatedBy = changed
            ? state.profile.driverName || "담당자 미설정"
            : old?.handoverUpdatedBy || "";
          let savedId = customerEditId;
          if (customerEditId) {
            const i = state.customers.findIndex((c) => c.id === customerEditId);
            state.customers[i] = normalizeCustomer(
              { ...state.customers[i], ...value },
              i,
            );
          } else {
            savedId = newId();
            state.customers.push(
              normalizeCustomer(
                { id: savedId, ...value },
                state.customers.length,
              ),
            );
          }
          const target = state.customers.find((c) => c.id === savedId),
            list = customers().filter((c) => c.id !== savedId);
          list.splice(
            Math.max(0, Math.min(list.length, desired - 1)),
            0,
            target,
          );
          list.forEach((c, i) => (c.routeOrder = i + 1));
          saveState("거래처 인수인계 저장 전");
          closeModal("formModal");
          renderCustomers();
        }
        function normalizeCustomerOrder() {
          customers().forEach((c, i) => (c.routeOrder = i + 1));
        }
        function guideRow(label, value, extra = "") {
          return `<div class="guide-row ${extra}"><span>${esc(label)}</span><strong>${esc(value || "미입력")}</strong></div>`;
        }
        function openStoreGuide(deliveryId, source = "today", message = "") {
          storeGuideDeliveryId = Number(deliveryId);
          storeGuideReturn = source || "today";
          clearTimeout(guideSecretTimer);
          const d = state.deliveries.find((x) => x.id === storeGuideDeliveryId);
          if (!d) return;
          const c = customerOf(d),
            exists = hasHandover(c),
            ack = handoverAcknowledged(d, c),
            updated = c.handoverUpdatedAt
              ? `${new Date(c.handoverUpdatedAt).toLocaleString("ko-KR")} · ${c.handoverUpdatedBy || "작성자 미입력"}`
              : "수정 기록 없음",
            mapUrl = `https://map.kakao.com/link/search/${encodeURIComponent(c.address || c.name)}`;
          $("#storeGuideModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>📝 ${esc(c.name)} 점포 인수인계</h2><p>${d.routeOrder}번째 배송지 · ${ack ? "확인 완료" : "확인 필요"}</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-store-guide">×</button></div><div class="modal-body">${message ? `<div class="weigh-ready">✓ ${esc(message)}</div>` : ""}${exists ? `<div class="guide-grid">${guideRow("매장 입고 가능 시간", c.receivingTime)}<div class="guide-row"><span>출입 비밀번호·공동현관 번호</span><div class="guide-secret"><strong id="guideSecret">${c.accessPassword ? "••••••" : "미입력"}</strong>${c.accessPassword ? `<button type="button" data-action="toggle-guide-secret">15초 보기</button>` : ""}</div></div>${guideRow("매장 진입 방법", c.entryMethod)}${guideRow("물건 놓는 자리", c.dropLocation)}${guideRow("절대 하지 말아야 할 사항", c.deliveryCautions, "caution")}${guideRow("주차·엘리베이터 정보", c.parkingInfo)}${guideRow("그 밖의 인수인계 메모", c.handoverNote)}</div><div class="guide-meta">최근 수정: ${esc(updated)}<br>${d.handoverAcknowledgedAt ? `마지막 확인: ${esc(new Date(d.handoverAcknowledgedAt).toLocaleString("ko-KR"))} · ${esc(d.handoverAcknowledgedBy || "담당자 미설정")}` : "아직 이 배송 담당자가 확인하지 않았습니다."}</div>` : `<div class="empty"><b>등록된 점포 인수인계 정보가 없습니다.</b><br>거래처 수정에서 출입 방법과 물건 위치를 등록해 주세요.</div>`}<div class="guide-actions"><a href="${mapUrl}" target="_blank" rel="noopener">🗺️ 위치 확인</a>${c.phone ? `<a href="tel:${esc(c.phone)}">📞 매장 전화</a>` : ""}</div>${exists && d.status !== "completed" ? `<button class="full-button primary-button" type="button" data-action="confirm-store-guide">${ack ? "✓ 다시 확인했습니다" : "✓ 점포 특이사항 확인 완료"}</button>` : ""}<button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="edit-store-handover" data-customer-id="${c.id}">점포 인수인계 내용 수정</button><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="close-store-guide">${storeGuideReturn === "departure" ? "출차 점검으로 돌아가기" : storeGuideReturn === "check" ? "하차 확인으로 돌아가기" : "배송 화면으로 돌아가기"}</button></div></div>`;
          $("#storeGuideModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function closeStoreGuide() {
          clearTimeout(guideSecretTimer);
          closeModal("storeGuideModal");
          if (storeGuideReturn === "departure") return openDepartureCheck();
          if (storeGuideReturn === "check")
            return openChecklist(storeGuideDeliveryId);
        }
        function confirmStoreGuide() {
          const d = state.deliveries.find((x) => x.id === storeGuideDeliveryId);
          if (!d) return;
          const c = customerOf(d);
          d.handoverAcknowledgedVersion = handoverVersion(c);
          d.handoverAcknowledgedAt = new Date().toISOString();
          d.handoverAcknowledgedBy =
            state.profile.driverName || "담당자 미설정";
          d.handoverAcknowledgedVehicle = state.profile.vehicleNumber || "";
          saveState("점포 인수인계 확인 전");
          renderToday();
          openStoreGuide(
            d.id,
            storeGuideReturn,
            "점포 특이사항을 확인 완료했습니다.",
          );
        }
        function toggleGuideSecret(button) {
          const d = state.deliveries.find((x) => x.id === storeGuideDeliveryId),
            c = d ? customerOf(d) : null,
            secret = $("#guideSecret");
          if (!c || !secret) return;
          const revealed = button.dataset.revealed === "true";
          clearTimeout(guideSecretTimer);
          button.dataset.revealed = String(!revealed);
          secret.textContent = revealed ? "••••••" : c.accessPassword;
          button.textContent = revealed ? "15초 보기" : "다시 숨기기";
          if (!revealed)
            guideSecretTimer = setTimeout(() => {
              if (secret) {
                secret.textContent = "••••••";
                button.dataset.revealed = "false";
                button.textContent = "15초 보기";
              }
            }, 15000);
        }
        function toggleFormSecret(button) {
          const input = $("#customerAccessPassword");
          if (!input) return;
          const show = input.type === "password";
          input.type = show ? "text" : "password";
          button.textContent = show ? "숨기기" : "보기";
        }

        function blankItem() {
          return normalizeItem({
            category: "활어",
            species: "광어",
            size: "기본 규격",
            originCountry: "국내산",
            requestedQty: 1,
            unit: "마리",
            priceUnit: "kg",
            processing: "찍어바리",
          });
        }
        function openDelivery(id) {
          deliveryEditId = id || null;
          const first = customers()[0];
          if (!first) return alert("거래처를 먼저 등록해 주세요.");
          const old = state.deliveries.find((d) => d.id === id);
          formDraft = old
            ? JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(old))
            : normalizeDelivery({
                customerId: first.id,
                deliveryDate: workDate,
                routeOrder: deliveries().length + 1,
                status: "ready",
                items: [blankItem()],
                boxes: [],
              });
          renderDeliveryForm();
          $("#formModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function rerenderDeliveryForm(options = {}) {
          const oldCard = $("#formModal .modal-card"),
            active = document.activeElement,
            itemCard = active?.closest?.("[data-form-item]"),
            boxRow = active?.closest?.("[data-form-box]"),
            position = {
              scrollTop: oldCard?.scrollTop || 0,
              itemIndex: itemCard?.dataset.formItem ?? null,
              boxIndex: boxRow?.dataset.formBox ?? null,
              itemField: active?.dataset?.itemField || "",
              boxField: active?.hasAttribute?.("data-box-field") || false,
              name: active?.name || "",
            };
          renderDeliveryForm();
          requestAnimationFrame(() => {
            const card = $("#formModal .modal-card");
            if (!card) return;
            if (options.focusNewItem) {
              const newCard = card.querySelector(
                  `[data-form-item="${formDraft.items.length - 1}"]`,
                ),
                field = newCard?.querySelector('[data-item-field="species"]');
              if (newCard) {
                const headerHeight =
                    card.querySelector(".modal-head")?.offsetHeight || 55,
                  targetTop =
                    card.scrollTop +
                    newCard.getBoundingClientRect().top -
                    card.getBoundingClientRect().top -
                    headerHeight -
                    8;
                card.scrollTop = Math.max(0, targetTop);
                newCard.classList.add("new-item-flash");
                setTimeout(
                  () => newCard.classList.remove("new-item-flash"),
                  1100,
                );
                if (field) {
                  try {
                    field.focus({ preventScroll: true });
                  } catch {
                    field.focus();
                  }
                  card.scrollTop = Math.max(0, targetTop);
                }
              }
              return;
            }
            card.scrollTop = position.scrollTop;
            let target = null;
            if (position.itemIndex !== null && position.itemField)
              target = card.querySelector(
                `[data-form-item="${position.itemIndex}"] [data-item-field="${position.itemField}"]`,
              );
            else if (position.boxIndex !== null && position.boxField)
              target = card.querySelector(
                `[data-form-box="${position.boxIndex}"] [data-box-field]`,
              );
            else if (position.name)
              target = card.querySelector(`[name="${position.name}"]`);
            if (target) {
              try {
                target.focus({ preventScroll: true });
              } catch {
                target.focus();
              }
              card.scrollTop = position.scrollTop;
            }
          });
        }
        function addFormItem() {
          syncFormDraft();
          formDraft.items.push(blankItem());
          rerenderDeliveryForm({ focusNewItem: true });
        }
        function renderDeliveryForm() {
          const d = formDraft;
          $("#formModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>${deliveryEditId ? "발주·포장 수정" : "수동 배송 추가"}</h2><p>입력 내용은 하차 체크와 명세서에 연결됩니다.</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-modal">×</button></div><form id="deliveryForm" class="modal-body"><label class="field"><span>거래처</span><select class="control" name="customerId">${customers()
              .map(
                (c) =>
                  `<option value="${c.id}" ${c.id === d.customerId ? "selected" : ""}>${esc(c.name)}</option>`,
              )
              .join(
                "",
              )}</select></label><div class="two"><label class="field"><span>배송일</span><input class="control" name="deliveryDate" type="date" value="${esc(d.deliveryDate)}"></label><label class="field"><span>배송순서</span><input class="control" name="routeOrder" type="number" min="1" value="${d.routeOrder}"></label></div><label class="band-line" style="border-color:#d46a61;color:#8e1711;background:var(--red-soft)"><input name="isUrgentAdditional" type="checkbox" ${d.isUrgentAdditional ? "checked" : ""}>🚨 긴급 추가 발주로 등록</label><div class="heading" style="margin:6px 0 0"><h2 style="font-size:18px">어종·제품</h2><button class="mini" type="button" data-action="add-form-item">＋ 품목</button></div><div id="formItems">${d.items.map(renderItemEditor).join("")}</div><button class="full-button add-next-item" type="button" data-action="add-form-item">＋ 다음 품목 추가<small>현재 ${d.items.length}개 · 누르면 새 품목 입력칸으로 바로 이동</small></button><div class="heading" style="margin:6px 0 0"><h2 style="font-size:18px">박스·동봉품</h2><button class="mini" type="button" data-action="add-form-box">＋ 박스</button></div><div id="formBoxes">${d.boxes.map(renderBoxEditor).join("") || `<div class="empty">박스가 없으면 추가하지 않아도 됩니다.</div>`}</div><label class="field"><span>동봉품 전체 메모</span><textarea class="control" name="coPackNote">${esc(d.coPackNote)}</textarea></label><label class="field"><span>전날 미수금액</span><input class="control" name="previousBalance" type="number" min="0" value="${d.previousBalance || ""}"></label><label class="field"><span>전체 메모</span><textarea class="control" name="notes">${esc(d.notes)}</textarea></label><div class="total-preview"><span>예상 합계</span><b id="formTotal">${money(d.items.reduce((s, i) => s + itemAmount(i), 0) + Number(d.previousBalance || 0))}원</b></div><button class="full-button primary-button sticky-save" type="submit">발주 내용 저장</button></form></div>`;
        }
        function renderItemEditor(i, index) {
          return `<article class="item-editor" data-form-item="${index}"><div class="item-editor-head"><strong>${index + 1}번 품목</strong><button type="button" data-action="remove-form-item" data-index="${index}" ${formDraft.items.length === 1 ? "disabled" : ""}>삭제</button></div><div class="three"><label class="field"><span>구분</span><select class="control" data-item-field="category">${categories.map((v) => `<option ${v === i.category ? "selected" : ""}>${v}</option>`).join("")}</select></label><label class="field"><span>어종·품목</span><input class="control" data-item-field="species" value="${esc(i.species)}"></label><label class="field"><span>규격</span><input class="control" data-item-field="size" value="${esc(i.size)}"></label></div><div class="three"><label class="field"><span>원산지</span><input class="control" data-item-field="originCountry" list="originList" value="${esc(i.originCountry)}"></label><label class="field"><span>주문 수량</span><input class="control" data-item-field="requestedQty" type="number" min="0" step=".01" value="${i.requestedQty}"></label><label class="field"><span>주문 단위</span><select class="control" data-item-field="unit">${units.map((v) => `<option ${v === i.unit ? "selected" : ""}>${v}</option>`).join("")}</select></label></div><div class="three"><label class="field"><span>${(i.weighings || []).length ? "계근 자동 합계 kg" : "실제 중량 kg"}</span><input class="control" data-item-field="actualWeight" type="number" min="0" step=".001" value="${i.actualWeight ?? ""}" ${(i.weighings || []).length ? "disabled" : ""}></label><label class="field"><span>판매 단가</span><input class="control" data-item-field="unitPrice" type="number" min="0" value="${i.unitPrice || ""}"></label><label class="field"><span>가격 기준</span><select class="control" data-item-field="priceUnit">${units.map((v) => `<option value="${v}" ${v === i.priceUnit ? "selected" : ""}>${v}당</option>`).join("")}</select></label></div><div class="three"><label class="field"><span>수조 위치</span><select class="control" data-item-field="tankNumber"><option value="0">박스·별도</option>${Array.from({ length: 6 }, (_, n) => `<option value="${n + 1}" ${Number(i.tankNumber) === n + 1 ? "selected" : ""}>${n + 1}번 수조</option>`).join("")}</select></label><label class="field"><span>작업·보관</span><input class="control" data-item-field="processing" value="${esc(i.processing)}"></label><label class="field"><span>필렛 작업비/kg</span><input class="control" data-item-field="processingFeePerKg" type="number" min="0" value="${i.processingFeePerKg || ""}" ${i.category === "필렛 제품" ? "" : "disabled"}></label></div><label class="band-line"><input data-item-field="rubberBand" type="checkbox" ${i.rubberBand ? "checked" : ""}>꼬리 고무밴드 작업</label><div class="two"><label class="field"><span>밴드 색상</span><input class="control" data-item-field="rubberBandColor" value="${esc(i.rubberBandColor)}" ${i.rubberBand ? "" : "disabled"}></label><label class="field"><span>밴드 수량</span><input class="control" data-item-field="rubberBandQuantity" type="number" min="0" value="${i.rubberBandQuantity || ""}" ${i.rubberBand ? "" : "disabled"}></label></div><label class="field"><span>품목별 메모</span><input class="control" data-item-field="includedNote" value="${esc(i.includedNote)}"></label></article>`;
        }
        function renderBoxEditor(b, index) {
          return `<div class="box-row" data-form-box="${index}"><span class="box-number">${index + 1}</span><input class="control" data-box-field="contents" value="${esc(b.contents)}" placeholder="박스 동봉 내역"><button type="button" data-action="remove-form-box" data-index="${index}">삭제</button></div>`;
        }
        function syncFormDraft() {
          const form = $("#deliveryForm");
          if (!form) return;
          form.querySelectorAll("[data-form-item]").forEach((card) => {
            const item = formDraft.items[Number(card.dataset.formItem)];
            card.querySelectorAll("[data-item-field]").forEach((el) => {
              const key = el.dataset.itemField;
              item[key] = el.type === "checkbox" ? el.checked : el.value;
            });
          });
          form.querySelectorAll("[data-form-box]").forEach((row) => {
            const box = formDraft.boxes[Number(row.dataset.formBox)];
            box.contents = row.querySelector("[data-box-field]").value;
          });
          const fd = Object.fromEntries(new FormData(form));
          Object.assign(formDraft, {
            customerId: Number(fd.customerId),
            deliveryDate: fd.deliveryDate,
            routeOrder: Math.max(1, Number(fd.routeOrder) || 1),
            isUrgentAdditional: Boolean(
              form.querySelector('[name="isUrgentAdditional"]')?.checked,
            ),
            coPackNote: String(fd.coPackNote || ""),
            notes: String(fd.notes || ""),
            previousBalance: Math.max(0, Number(fd.previousBalance) || 0),
          });
        }
        function normalizeFormDraft() {
          formDraft.items = formDraft.items.map(normalizeItem);
          formDraft.boxes = formDraft.boxes.map(normalizeBox);
        }
        function saveDelivery() {
          syncFormDraft();
          normalizeFormDraft();
          const desired = formDraft.routeOrder;
          if (deliveryEditId) {
            const idx = state.deliveries.findIndex(
                (d) => d.id === deliveryEditId,
              ),
              old = state.deliveries[idx];
            formDraft.items.forEach((item) => {
              const before = old.items.find((x) => x.id === item.id),
                from = Number(before?.tankNumber) || 0,
                to = Number(item.tankNumber) || 0,
                loadingChanged =
                  before &&
                  (from !== to ||
                    before.species !== item.species ||
                    Number(before.requestedQty) !== Number(item.requestedQty) ||
                    Number(before.actualWeight) !== Number(item.actualWeight) ||
                    before.rubberBand !== item.rubberBand ||
                    before.rubberBandColor !== item.rubberBandColor ||
                    Number(before.rubberBandQuantity) !==
                      Number(item.rubberBandQuantity));
              if (before && from !== to) {
                item.tankHistory = item.tankHistory || [];
                item.tankHistory.push(
                  normalizeTankChange({
                    from,
                    to,
                    reason: "발주·포장 내용 수정",
                  }),
                );
              }
              if (loadingChanged) resetAllTaskWorkflow(item);
            });
            if (
              formDraft.boxes.length !== old.boxes.length ||
              formDraft.boxes.some(
                (b, n) => b.contents !== old.boxes[n]?.contents,
              )
            ) {
              formDraft.boxCountConfirmed = false;
              formDraft.boxCountConfirmedAt = null;
            }
            if (formDraft.isUrgentAdditional && !old.isUrgentAdditional) {
              formDraft.urgentAcknowledged = false;
              formDraft.urgentAcknowledgedAt = null;
              formDraft.status = "new";
            }
            if (!formDraft.isUrgentAdditional) {
              formDraft.urgentAcknowledged = true;
              formDraft.urgentAcknowledgedAt = null;
            }
            formDraft.id = deliveryEditId;
            state.deliveries[idx] = formDraft;
          } else {
            formDraft.id = newId();
            formDraft.status = formDraft.isUrgentAdditional ? "new" : "ready";
            formDraft.urgentAcknowledged = !formDraft.isUrgentAdditional;
            formDraft.urgentAcknowledgedAt = null;
            formDraft.createdAt = new Date().toISOString();
            state.deliveries.push(formDraft);
          }
          workDate = formDraft.deliveryDate;
          const target = formDraft,
            list = state.deliveries
              .filter(
                (d) =>
                  d.deliveryDate === workDate &&
                  d.status !== "cancelled" &&
                  d.id !== target.id,
              )
              .sort(byOrder);
          list.splice(
            Math.max(0, Math.min(list.length, desired - 1)),
            0,
            target,
          );
          list.forEach((d, i) => (d.routeOrder = i + 1));
          saveState();
          closeModal("formModal");
          render();
        }

        function openTankInfo(number, message = "") {
          tankInfoNumber = Math.max(1, Math.min(6, Number(number) || 1));
          tankDeliveryId = null;
          tankItemId = null;
          tankPendingNumber = 0;
          tankReturn = "tank-info";
          const rows = tankRows().filter(
              ({ i }) => Number(i.tankNumber) === tankInfoNumber,
            ),
            totalWeight = rows.reduce(
              (s, { i }) => s + (Number(i.actualWeight) || 0),
              0,
            ),
            cards = rows
              .map(
                ({ d, i, c }) =>
                  `<article class="tank-info-row"><div><strong>${d.routeOrder}번 ${esc(c.name)} · ${esc(i.species)}</strong><small>${esc(i.category)} · ${esc(i.originCountry)} · ${esc(i.processing)}<br>수량 ${esc(quantityText(i))}${i.rubberBand ? ` · 밴드 ${esc(i.rubberBandColor)} ${i.rubberBandQuantity}개` : ""}${i.includedNote ? ` · ${esc(i.includedNote)}` : ""}</small><span class="load-status ${i.tankLoaded ? "done" : ""}">${i.tankLoaded ? "✓ 실제 상차 완료" : "○ 실제 상차 확인 필요"}</span></div><div class="tank-info-actions"><button type="button" data-action="open-tank-change" data-delivery-id="${d.id}" data-item-id="${i.id}" data-source="tank-info">수조 위치 변경</button><button class="${i.tankLoaded ? "loaded" : ""}" type="button" data-action="toggle-tank-loaded" data-delivery-id="${d.id}" data-item-id="${i.id}" data-source="tank-info">${i.tankLoaded ? "상차 완료 취소" : "✓ 상차 완료"}</button></div></article>`,
              )
              .join("");
          $("#tankModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>💧 ${tankInfoNumber}번 수조 정보</h2><p>${rows.length}개 품목${totalWeight ? ` · 실제 중량 합계 ${totalWeight.toFixed(3)}kg` : ""}</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-tank">×</button></div><div class="modal-body">${message ? `<div class="weigh-ready">✓ ${esc(message)}</div>` : ""}<div class="senior-guide"><b>${tankInfoNumber}번 수조를 눌러 열었습니다.</b>아래 품목에서 ‘수조 위치 변경’을 누르면 다른 수조를 바로 선택할 수 있습니다.</div><div class="tank-info-list">${cards || `<div class="empty"><b>${tankInfoNumber}번 수조는 비어 있습니다.</b><br>현재 배치된 어종이나 제품이 없습니다.</div>`}</div><button class="full-button warning-button" type="button" data-action="open-tank-manager">전체 수조 상차 관리</button><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="close-tank">배송 화면으로 돌아가기</button></div></div>`;
          $("#tankModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function openTankManager(message = "") {
          tankInfoNumber = 0;
          tankDeliveryId = null;
          tankItemId = null;
          tankPendingNumber = 0;
          tankReturn = "manager";
          const rows = tankRows(),
            cards = rows
              .map(({ d, i, c }) => {
                const changes = i.tankHistory || [],
                  last = changes[changes.length - 1],
                  hasTank = Number(i.tankNumber) > 0;
                return `<article class="tank-manager-row"><div><strong>${d.routeOrder}번 ${esc(c.name)} · ${esc(i.species)}</strong><small>${esc(quantityText(i))}${last ? ` · 최근 변경 ${tankLabel(last.from)} → ${tankLabel(last.to)}` : ""}</small><span class="tank-badge">현재 ${tankLabel(i.tankNumber)}</span>${hasTank ? `<span class="load-status ${i.tankLoaded ? "done" : ""}">${i.tankLoaded ? "✓ 실제 상차 완료" : "○ 실제 상차 확인 필요"}</span>` : ""}</div><div class="load-controls" style="grid-template-columns:1fr;min-width:170px"><button type="button" data-action="open-tank-change" data-delivery-id="${d.id}" data-item-id="${i.id}" data-source="manager" style="font-size:16px">수조 바꾸기</button>${hasTank ? `<button class="load-toggle ${i.tankLoaded ? "done" : ""}" type="button" data-action="toggle-tank-loaded" data-delivery-id="${d.id}" data-item-id="${i.id}" data-source="manager" style="font-size:16px">${i.tankLoaded ? "상차 완료 취소" : "✓ 실제 상차 완료"}</button>` : ""}</div></article>`;
              })
              .join("");
          $("#tankModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>💧 수조 실제 상차 확인</h2><p>어종을 수조에 넣은 직후 큰 완료 버튼을 누르세요.</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-tank">×</button></div><div class="modal-body">${message ? `<div class="weigh-ready">✓ ${esc(message)}</div>` : ""}<div class="senior-guide"><b>현장 순서</b>① 거래처·어종 확인 → ② 실제 수조에 넣기 → ③ ‘실제 상차 완료’ 누르기</div><div class="tank-manager-list">${cards || `<div class="empty">수조에 상차할 배송 품목이 없습니다.</div>`}</div><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="close-tank">배송 화면으로 돌아가기</button></div></div>`;
          $("#tankModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function openTankChange(deliveryId, itemId, source = "manager") {
          tankDeliveryId = Number(deliveryId);
          tankItemId = Number(itemId);
          tankReturn = source || "manager";
          const { d, i, c } = findTankItem();
          if (!d || !i || d.status === "completed")
            return alert(
              "배송 완료된 품목은 하차 완료를 취소한 뒤 수정해 주세요.",
            );
          tankPendingNumber = Number(i.tankNumber) || 0;
          const history = [...(i.tankHistory || [])]
            .reverse()
            .slice(0, 5)
            .map(
              (h) =>
                `<div class="tank-history-row">${esc(new Date(h.at).toLocaleString("ko-KR"))} · ${tankLabel(h.from)} → ${tankLabel(h.to)} · ${esc(h.reason)}</div>`,
            )
            .join("");
          const choices = [0, 1, 2, 3, 4, 5, 6]
            .map(
              (n) =>
                `<button class="tank-choice ${n === 0 ? "box-choice" : ""} ${tankPendingNumber === n ? "selected" : ""}" type="button" data-action="choose-tank" data-tank="${n}">${n ? tankLabel(n) : "박스·별도 보관"}</button>`,
            )
            .join("");
          $("#tankModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>${esc(c.name)} · ${esc(i.species)}</h2><p>${d.routeOrder}번째 배송지 · ${esc(quantityText(i))}</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-tank-change">×</button></div><div class="modal-body"><div id="tankChangePreview" class="tank-change-preview"><small>변경 전 → 변경 후</small><strong>${tankLabel(i.tankNumber)} → ${tankLabel(tankPendingNumber)}</strong></div><div class="senior-guide"><b>새로 넣을 위치를 한 번 누르세요.</b>선택한 수조는 진한 초록색으로 표시됩니다.</div><div class="tank-choice-grid">${choices}</div><label class="field"><span>변경 이유</span><select id="tankReason" class="control"><option>추가 발주로 수조 재배치</option><option>수조 공간 부족</option><option>어종 분리</option><option>현장 작업 변경</option><option>기타</option></select></label><button id="confirmTankButton" class="full-button primary-button" type="button" data-action="confirm-tank-change" disabled>선택한 수조로 변경 확정</button>${history ? `<div class="heading" style="margin:8px 0 0"><div><h2 style="font-size:19px">최근 변경 기록</h2><p>실수 여부를 확인할 수 있습니다.</p></div></div><div class="tank-history">${history}</div>` : ""}<button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="close-tank-change">${tankReturn === "manager" ? "품목 목록으로" : "변경하지 않고 돌아가기"}</button></div></div>`;
          $("#tankModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function chooseTank(value) {
          const { d, i } = findTankItem();
          if (!d || !i) return;
          tankPendingNumber = Math.max(0, Math.min(6, Number(value) || 0));
          document
            .querySelectorAll("#tankModal .tank-choice")
            .forEach((b) =>
              b.classList.toggle(
                "selected",
                Number(b.dataset.tank) === tankPendingNumber,
              ),
            );
          $("#tankChangePreview").innerHTML =
            `<small>변경 전 → 변경 후</small><strong>${tankLabel(i.tankNumber)} → ${tankLabel(tankPendingNumber)}</strong>`;
          $("#confirmTankButton").disabled =
            tankPendingNumber === Number(i.tankNumber || 0);
        }
        function recordTankChange(d, i, to, reason) {
          if (!ensureWorkOpen()) return false;
          const from = Number(i.tankNumber) || 0,
            next = Math.max(0, Math.min(6, Number(to) || 0));
          if (from === next) return false;
          i.tankNumber = next;
          i.tankHistory = i.tankHistory || [];
          i.tankHistory.push(normalizeTankChange({ from, to: next, reason }));
          resetAllTaskWorkflow(i);
          saveState("수조 변경 전");
          renderToday();
          return true;
        }
        function showTankDragToast(message, warn = false) {
          const el = $("#tankDragToast");
          if (!el) return;
          clearTimeout(tankDragToastTimer);
          el.textContent = message;
          el.classList.toggle("warn", warn);
          el.classList.add("show");
          tankDragToastTimer = setTimeout(
            () => el.classList.remove("show"),
            2600,
          );
        }
        function tankDragItem(deliveryId, itemId) {
          const d = state.deliveries.find((x) => x.id === Number(deliveryId)),
            i = d?.items.find((x) => x.id === Number(itemId));
          return { d, i, c: d ? customerOf(d) : null };
        }
        function startTankDrag() {
          if (!tankDrag || tankDrag.active) return;
          const { d, i, c } = tankDragItem(
            tankDrag.deliveryId,
            tankDrag.itemId,
          );
          if (!d || !i || d.status === "completed") {
            cancelTankDrag();
            return;
          }
          tankDrag.active = true;
          tankDrag.element.classList.add("dragging");
          tankDrag.element
            .closest("[data-tank-drop]")
            ?.classList.add("drag-source");
          const ghost = document.createElement("div");
          ghost.className = "tank-drag-ghost";
          ghost.innerHTML = `${esc(c.name)} · ${esc(i.species)}<small>${tankLabel(i.tankNumber)}에서 이동 중</small>`;
          document.body.appendChild(ghost);
          tankDrag.ghost = ghost;
          if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(35);
          updateTankDrag(tankDrag.x, tankDrag.y);
        }
        function updateTankDrag(x, y) {
          if (!tankDrag?.active) return;
          tankDrag.x = x;
          tankDrag.y = y;
          tankDrag.ghost.style.left = `${x}px`;
          tankDrag.ghost.style.top = `${y}px`;
          document
            .querySelectorAll("[data-tank-drop].drag-over")
            .forEach((el) => el.classList.remove("drag-over"));
          const target = document
              .elementFromPoint(x, y)
              ?.closest("[data-tank-drop]"),
            number = Number(target?.dataset.tankDrop) || 0;
          tankDrag.targetTank = number;
          if (target) target.classList.add("drag-over");
        }
        function cleanTankDrag() {
          if (!tankDrag) return;
          clearTimeout(tankDrag.timer);
          tankDrag.element?.classList.remove("dragging");
          document
            .querySelectorAll(
              "[data-tank-drop].drag-source,[data-tank-drop].drag-over",
            )
            .forEach((el) => el.classList.remove("drag-source", "drag-over"));
          tankDrag.ghost?.remove();
          try {
            tankDrag.element?.releasePointerCapture(tankDrag.pointerId);
          } catch {}
          tankDrag = null;
        }
        function cancelTankDrag() {
          cleanTankDrag();
        }
        function finishTankDrag() {
          if (!tankDrag) return;
          const wasActive = tankDrag.active,
            target = Number(tankDrag.targetTank) || 0,
            deliveryId = tankDrag.deliveryId,
            itemId = tankDrag.itemId,
            from = Number(tankDrag.sourceTank) || 0;
          cleanTankDrag();
          if (!wasActive) return;
          tankDragSuppressUntil = Date.now() + 650;
          if (!target)
            return showTankDragToast(
              "수조 안에 놓아야 위치가 변경됩니다.",
              true,
            );
          if (target === from)
            return showTankDragToast(
              `${target}번 수조 그대로 유지했습니다.`,
              true,
            );
          const { d, i, c } = tankDragItem(deliveryId, itemId);
          if (!d || !i || d.status === "completed")
            return showTankDragToast(
              "이 품목은 지금 변경할 수 없습니다.",
              true,
            );
          if (
            recordTankChange(d, i, target, "메인 수조 화면에서 끌어서 이동")
          ) {
            showTankDragToast(
              `✓ ${c.name} ${i.species}: ${target}번 수조로 변경 완료`,
            );
            if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([35, 45, 35]);
          }
        }
        function toggleTankLoaded(deliveryId, itemId, source = "manager") {
          const d = state.deliveries.find((x) => x.id === Number(deliveryId)),
            i = d?.items.find((x) => x.id === Number(itemId));
          if (!d || !i || d.status === "completed") return;
          if (!i.tankNumber) return alert("먼저 1~6번 수조를 지정해 주세요.");
          if (isWeighable(i) && (i.weighings || []).length) {
            closeModal("tankModal");
            return openLoadingControl(
              "활어는 콜·복창·밴드·수조 확인 후 한 마리씩 상차 완료합니다.",
              d.id,
              i.id,
            );
          }
          i.tankLoaded = !i.tankLoaded;
          i.tankLoadedAt = i.tankLoaded ? new Date().toISOString() : null;
          i.checked = false;
          saveState("수조 실제 상차 상태 변경 전");
          renderToday();
          const message = `${customerOf(d).name} ${i.species} · ${i.tankLoaded ? "실제 상차를 완료했습니다." : "상차 완료를 취소했습니다."}`;
          if (source === "tank-info")
            return openTankInfo(tankInfoNumber, message);
          openTankManager(message);
        }
        function confirmTankChange() {
          const { d, i, c } = findTankItem();
          if (!d || !i || d.status === "completed") return;
          const from = Number(i.tankNumber) || 0,
            reason = $("#tankReason")?.value || "현장 수조 변경";
          if (!recordTankChange(d, i, tankPendingNumber, reason))
            return alert(
              "현재 수조와 같은 위치입니다. 다른 수조를 선택해 주세요.",
            );
          const message = `${c.name} ${i.species}: ${tankLabel(from)}에서 ${tankLabel(tankPendingNumber)}로 변경했습니다. 상차 확인은 콜부터 다시 진행합니다.`;
          if (tankReturn === "check") {
            closeModal("tankModal");
            return openChecklist(d.id, message);
          }
          if (tankReturn === "weigh") {
            closeModal("tankModal");
            return openWeighItem(d.id, i.id);
          }
          if (tankReturn === "loading") {
            closeModal("tankModal");
            loadingError = "";
            return openLoadingTask(d.id, i.id, loadingWeightId, message);
          }
          if (tankReturn === "tank-info")
            return openTankInfo(tankInfoNumber, message);
          openTankManager(message);
        }
        function closeTankChange() {
          if (tankReturn === "manager") return openTankManager();
          if (tankReturn === "tank-info") return openTankInfo(tankInfoNumber);
          if (tankReturn === "loading") {
            closeModal("tankModal");
            return openLoadingTask(
              loadingDeliveryId,
              loadingItemId,
              loadingWeightId,
            );
          }
          closeModal("tankModal");
        }
        function openLoadingTankChange() {
          const { d, i } = findLoadingTask();
          if (!d || !i) return;
          closeModal("loadingModal");
          openTankChange(d.id, i.id, "loading");
        }

        function openWeighingList() {
          weighDeliveryId = null;
          weighItemId = null;
          const ws = weighingStats(),
            rows = ws.rows
              .map(({ d, i, c }) => {
                const count = (i.weighings || []).length,
                  target = targetFishCount(i),
                  total = weightTotal(i);
                return `<article class="weigh-row ${i.weighingConfirmed ? "confirmed" : ""}"><div><strong>${d.routeOrder}번 ${esc(c.name)} · ${esc(i.species)}</strong><small>${target ? `발주 ${target}마리 · ` : ""}계근 ${count}마리 / ${total.toFixed(3)}kg · ${i.tankNumber ? i.tankNumber + "번 수조" : "수조 미지정"}</small>${i.weighingConfirmed ? `<span class="tag" style="color:#155d32;background:#dff4e6">✓ 계근 확정</span>` : `<span class="tag">계근 필요</span>`}</div><button type="button" data-action="open-weigh-item" data-delivery-id="${d.id}" data-item-id="${i.id}">${i.weighingConfirmed ? "확인·수정" : "계근 입력"}</button></article>`;
              })
              .join("");
          $("#weighModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>⚖️ ${esc(state.profile.vehicleNumber)}호차 활어 계근</h2><p>한 마리씩 입력하면 거래명세서에 자동 합산됩니다.</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-weigh">×</button></div><div class="modal-body"><div class="weigh-summary"><div><small>발주 마릿수</small><strong>${ws.target || "-"}</strong></div><div><small>입력 마릿수</small><strong>${ws.entered}</strong></div><div><small>확정 품목</small><strong>${ws.confirmed}/${ws.totalItems}</strong></div></div>${ws.allDone ? `<div class="weigh-ready">✓ 호차 계근 완료 · 거래명세서 자동 작성 준비 완료</div>` : `<div class="weigh-notice">발주 거래처와 어종을 확인하고, 저울에서 나온 숫자를 순서대로 입력하세요.</div>`}<div class="weigh-list">${rows || `<div class="empty">오늘 계근할 활어가 없습니다.</div>`}</div><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="close-weigh">배송 화면으로 돌아가기</button></div></div>`;
          $("#weighModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function findWeighItem() {
          const d = state.deliveries.find((x) => x.id === weighDeliveryId),
            i = d?.items.find((x) => x.id === weighItemId);
          return { d, i, c: d ? customerOf(d) : null };
        }
        function openWeighItem(deliveryId, itemId) {
          weighDeliveryId = Number(deliveryId);
          weighItemId = Number(itemId);
          const { d, i, c } = findWeighItem();
          if (!d || !i) return openWeighingList();
          const locked = d.status === "completed",
            count = (i.weighings || []).length,
            target = targetFishCount(i),
            total = weightTotal(i),
            mismatch = target > 0 && count !== target,
            history = (i.weighings || [])
              .map(
                (w, index) =>
                  `<div class="weight-history-row" data-weight-row="${w.id}"><span>${index + 1}</span><input type="number" inputmode="decimal" min="0.001" step="0.001" value="${w.weight}" data-weight-entry="${w.id}" aria-label="${index + 1}번째 활어 중량" ${locked ? "disabled" : ""}><button type="button" data-action="delete-weight" data-id="${w.id}" ${locked ? "disabled" : ""}>삭제</button></div>`,
              )
              .join("");
          $("#weighModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>${esc(c.name)} · ${esc(i.species)}</h2><p>${d.routeOrder}번째 배송지 · ${target ? `발주 ${target}마리` : `수량 ${i.requestedQty}${esc(i.unit)}`}</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-weigh">×</button></div><div class="modal-body weight-panel"><div class="weight-focus"><small>현재 계근 합계</small><strong>${total.toFixed(3)}kg</strong><small>${count}마리 입력${target ? ` / 발주 ${target}마리` : ""}</small>${mismatch && count ? `<b>마릿수가 ${count < target ? target - count + "마리 부족" : count - target + "마리 초과"}합니다.</b>` : ""}</div><div class="tank-current"><div><span>상차할 위치</span><strong>${tankLabel(i.tankNumber)}</strong></div>${locked ? "" : `<button type="button" data-action="open-tank-change" data-delivery-id="${d.id}" data-item-id="${i.id}" data-source="weigh">🔄 수조 변경</button>`}</div>${locked ? `<div class="weigh-ready">배송 완료된 기록입니다.</div>` : `<form id="weighingForm" class="weight-entry"><input id="weightInput" class="weight-input" name="weight" type="number" inputmode="decimal" min="0.001" max="99.999" step="0.001" placeholder="0.000" aria-label="한 마리 중량 kg" required><button type="submit">저장 후 다음 마리</button></form>`}<div class="heading" style="margin:4px 0 0"><div><h2 style="font-size:19px">개별 계근 내역</h2><p>잘못 입력한 값은 바로 수정하거나 삭제합니다.</p></div>${count && !locked ? `<button class="mini" type="button" data-action="undo-last-weight">마지막 취소</button>` : ""}</div><div class="weight-history">${history || `<div class="empty">아직 입력한 중량이 없습니다.</div>`}</div>${locked ? "" : i.weighingConfirmed ? `<button class="full-button warning-button" type="button" data-action="reopen-weighing">계근 확정 취소 · 다시 수정</button>` : `<button class="full-button primary-button" type="button" data-action="confirm-weighing" ${count ? "" : "disabled"}>${mismatch ? "마릿수 확인 후 계근 확정" : "계근 완료 · 합계 확정"}</button>`}<button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="back-weigh-list">계근 목록으로</button></div></div>`;
          $("#weighModal").classList.remove("hidden");
          setTimeout(() => $("#weightInput")?.focus(), 60);
        }
        function resetTankLoad(i, resetTasks = false) {
          if (resetTasks) resetAllTaskWorkflow(i);
          else {
            i.tankLoaded = false;
            i.tankLoadedAt = null;
            i.checked = false;
          }
        }
        function addWeight(value) {
          const { d, i } = findWeighItem(),
            weight = Number(value);
          if (
            !d ||
            !i ||
            d.status === "completed" ||
            !Number.isFinite(weight) ||
            weight <= 0
          )
            return alert("한 마리 중량을 kg 단위로 입력해 주세요.");
          const warning = abnormalWeightWarning(i, weight);
          if (
            warning &&
            !confirm(
              `${warning}\n\n숫자를 다시 확인했습니다. 그래도 저장할까요?`,
            )
          ) {
            setTimeout(() => $("#weightInput")?.focus(), 30);
            return;
          }
          i.weighings = i.weighings || [];
          const entry = normalizeWeighing({
            weight,
            taskNumber: nextTaskNumber(d.deliveryDate),
          });
          if (warning)
            recordTaskLog(
              entry,
              "weight-warning",
              `${warning} 담당자 재확인 후 저장`,
            );
          i.weighings.push(entry);
          i.weighingConfirmed = false;
          i.weighingConfirmedAt = null;
          syncItemTaskLoad(i);
          syncWeightTotal(i);
          saveState("개별 계근 입력 전");
          openWeighItem(d.id, i.id);
        }
        function editWeight(id, value) {
          const { d, i } = findWeighItem(),
            entry = i?.weighings?.find((w) => w.id === Number(id)),
            weight = Number(value),
            previousWeight = Number(entry?.weight) || 0;
          if (
            !d ||
            !i ||
            !entry ||
            d.status === "completed" ||
            !Number.isFinite(weight) ||
            weight <= 0
          )
            return;
          const warning = abnormalWeightWarning(i, weight);
          if (
            warning &&
            !confirm(
              `${warning}\n\n수정한 숫자를 다시 확인했습니다. 그래도 저장할까요?`,
            )
          ) {
            openWeighItem(d.id, i.id);
            return;
          }
          entry.weight = weight;
          resetTaskWorkflow(entry);
          recordTaskLog(
            entry,
            "weight-edit",
            `개별 계근값 ${previousWeight.toFixed(3)}kg → ${weight.toFixed(3)}kg 수정 · 상차 확인 초기화`,
          );
          if (warning)
            recordTaskLog(
              entry,
              "weight-warning",
              `${warning} 담당자 재확인 후 수정`,
            );
          i.weighingConfirmed = false;
          i.weighingConfirmedAt = null;
          syncItemTaskLoad(i);
          syncWeightTotal(i);
          saveState("개별 계근 수정 전");
          openWeighItem(d.id, i.id);
        }
        function deleteWeight(id) {
          const { d, i } = findWeighItem();
          if (!d || !i || d.status === "completed") return;
          i.weighings = (i.weighings || []).filter((w) => w.id !== Number(id));
          i.weighingConfirmed = false;
          i.weighingConfirmedAt = null;
          syncItemTaskLoad(i);
          syncWeightTotal(i);
          saveState("개별 계근 삭제 전");
          openWeighItem(d.id, i.id);
        }
        function confirmWeighing() {
          const { d, i } = findWeighItem();
          if (!d || !i || !(i.weighings || []).length) return;
          if (!i.tankNumber)
            return alert("상차한 수조를 1~6번 중에서 먼저 선택해 주세요.");
          const target = targetFishCount(i),
            count = i.weighings.length;
          if (
            target &&
            count !== target &&
            !confirm(
              `발주는 ${target}마리, 계근 입력은 ${count}마리입니다. 이대로 확정할까요?`,
            )
          )
            return;
          i.weighingConfirmed = true;
          i.weighingConfirmedAt = new Date().toISOString();
          syncWeightTotal(i);
          saveState("활어 계근 확정 전");
          openWeighingList();
          renderToday();
        }

        function workflowStep(done, number, text) {
          return `<div class="workflow-step ${done ? "done" : ""}"><span>${done ? "✓" : number}</span><div>${esc(text)}</div></div>`;
        }
        function openLoadingControl(
          message = "",
          deliveryId = loadingFilterDeliveryId,
          itemId = loadingFilterItemId,
        ) {
          stopQrScanner();
          loadingFilterDeliveryId = Number(deliveryId) || 0;
          loadingFilterItemId = Number(itemId) || 0;
          const all = loadingTaskRows(),
            rows = all.filter(
              ({ d, i }) =>
                (!loadingFilterDeliveryId ||
                  d.id === loadingFilterDeliveryId) &&
                (!loadingFilterItemId || i.id === loadingFilterItemId),
            ),
            called = rows.filter(({ w }) => w.calledAt).length,
            repeated = rows.filter(({ w }) => w.repeatConfirmedAt).length,
            loaded = rows.filter(({ w }) => w.loadedAt).length,
            current = rows.find(({ w }) => !w.loadedAt),
            cards = rows
              .map(({ d, i, w, c }) => {
                const done = Boolean(w.loadedAt),
                  isCurrent = current?.w.id === w.id;
                return `<article class="loading-task-row ${done ? "done" : isCurrent ? "current" : ""}"><span class="task-number">${taskCode(w)}</span><div><strong>${d.routeOrder}번 ${esc(c.name)} · ${esc(i.species)}</strong><small>${Number(w.weight).toFixed(3)}kg · ${esc(state.profile.vehicleNumber || "-")}호차 ${tankLabel(i.tankNumber)} · ${esc(taskBandText(i))}</small><span class="task-status ${done ? "done" : ""}">${esc(taskStatus(i, w))} · ${taskStepCount(i, w)}/5</span></div><button type="button" data-action="open-loading-task" data-delivery-id="${d.id}" data-item-id="${i.id}" data-weight-id="${w.id}">${done ? "기록 보기" : isCurrent ? "이 작업 시작" : "열기"}</button></article>`;
              })
              .join("");
          const title = loadingFilterItemId
            ? `${rows[0] ? esc(rows[0].i.species) : "품목"} 개체별 상차`
            : `${esc(state.profile.vehicleNumber || "-")}호차 실시간 상차 관제`;
          $("#loadingModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>📣 ${title}</h2><p>콜을 듣고 기억하는 방식 대신 단계마다 확인합니다.</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-loading">×</button></div><div class="modal-body">${message ? `<div class="weigh-ready">✓ ${esc(message)}</div>` : ""}<div class="loading-summary"><div><small>전체 개체</small><strong>${rows.length}</strong></div><div><small>콜 전달</small><strong>${called}</strong></div><div><small>복창 확인</small><strong>${repeated}</strong></div><div><small>상차 완료</small><strong>${loaded}</strong></div></div><div class="senior-guide"><b>현장 확인 순서</b>① 앱의 지시대로 콜 → ② 활어를 받은 직원 복창 → ③ 실제 밴드 확인 → ④ 수조 QR 또는 번호 확인 → ⑤ 투입 후 완료</div><div class="verify-actions"><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="open-qr-labels">🏷️ 내 호차 수조 QR 라벨</button>${loadingFilterItemId ? `<button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="clear-loading-filter">전체 활어 보기</button>` : `<button class="full-button warning-button" type="button" data-action="open-weigh-list">⚖️ 계근 목록 확인</button>`}</div><div class="loading-task-list">${cards || `<div class="empty">계근된 활어가 없습니다.<br>활어를 한 마리씩 계근하면 작업번호가 자동 생성됩니다.</div>`}</div><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="close-loading">배송 화면으로 돌아가기</button></div></div>`;
          $("#loadingModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function openLoadingTask(deliveryId, itemId, weightId, notice = "") {
          loadingDeliveryId = Number(deliveryId);
          loadingItemId = Number(itemId);
          loadingWeightId = Number(weightId);
          stopQrScanner();
          const { d, i, w, c } = findLoadingTask();
          if (!d || !i || !w) return openLoadingControl();
          const callDone = Boolean(w.calledAt),
            repeatDone = Boolean(w.repeatConfirmedAt),
            bandDone = !taskBandRequired(i) || Boolean(w.bandVerifiedAt),
            tankDone = Boolean(w.tankVerifiedAt),
            loaded = Boolean(w.loadedAt),
            logs = [...(w.verificationLog || [])]
              .reverse()
              .slice(0, 6)
              .map(
                (log) =>
                  `<div class="workflow-log">${esc(new Date(log.at).toLocaleString("ko-KR"))} · ${esc(log.by || "")}<br>${esc(log.message || log.type || "")}</div>`,
              )
              .join(""),
            tankButtons = Array.from(
              { length: 6 },
              (_, n) =>
                `<button class="${n + 1 === Number(i.tankNumber) ? "expected" : ""}" type="button" data-action="verify-loading-tank" data-tank="${n + 1}" ${bandDone && repeatDone ? "" : "disabled"}>${n + 1}번 수조</button>`,
            ).join("");
          $("#loadingModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>활어 개체 상차 확인</h2><p>${d.routeOrder}번 ${esc(c.name)} · ${esc(taskStatus(i, w))}</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-loading">×</button></div><div class="modal-body">${notice ? `<div class="weigh-ready">✓ ${esc(notice)}</div>` : ""}${loadingError ? `<div class="workflow-error">⚠ ${esc(loadingError)}</div>` : ""}<div class="call-board"><span class="task-code">작업 ${taskCode(w)}</span><h2>${esc(state.profile.vehicleNumber || "미설정")}호차</h2><strong class="tank-call">${i.tankNumber ? `${i.tankNumber}번 수조` : "수조 미지정"}</strong><p>${esc(i.species)} · ${Number(w.weight).toFixed(3)}kg</p><p>${esc(c.name)}</p><div class="band-call"><span class="band-swatch" style="background:${bandColorHex(i.rubberBandColor)}"></span>${esc(taskBandText(i))}</div></div><div class="workflow-steps">${workflowStep(callDone, 1, "콜 담당자가 앱 내용을 그대로 읽었습니다.")}${workflowStep(repeatDone, 2, "활어를 받은 직원이 호차와 수조를 복창했습니다.")}${workflowStep(bandDone, 3, taskBandRequired(i) ? "지시 색상과 실제 밴드를 비교했습니다." : "밴드 작업이 없는 활어입니다.")}${workflowStep(tankDone, 4, "실제 차량·수조 위치를 확인했습니다.")}${workflowStep(loaded, 5, "활어를 수조에 넣고 상차 완료했습니다.")}</div>${!loaded ? `<div class="verify-actions"><button class="full-button primary-button" type="button" data-action="call-loading-task">📣 ${callDone ? "콜 다시 읽기" : "콜 읽기·전달 완료"}</button>${callDone && !repeatDone ? `<button class="full-button warning-button" type="button" data-action="confirm-loading-repeat">✓ 직원 복창 확인</button>` : ""}</div>${repeatDone && taskBandRequired(i) && !w.bandVerifiedAt ? `<div class="heading" style="margin:5px 0 0"><div><h2 style="font-size:18px">3단계 · 밴드 실물 확인</h2><p>다른 사람이 활어 꼬리와 화면을 직접 비교합니다.</p></div></div><div class="verify-actions"><button class="full-button primary-button" type="button" data-action="confirm-loading-band">✓ 밴드 색상·수량 일치</button><button class="full-button danger-button" type="button" data-action="report-band-mismatch">⚠ 밴드 불일치</button></div>` : ""}${repeatDone && bandDone && !tankDone ? `<div class="heading" style="margin:5px 0 0"><div><h2 style="font-size:18px">4단계 · 실제 수조 확인</h2><p>수조 앞 QR을 비추거나 실제 앞에 있는 번호를 누르세요.</p></div></div><button class="full-button primary-button" type="button" data-action="open-qr-scanner">📷 수조 QR 카메라 확인</button><div class="tank-verify-grid">${tankButtons}</div>` : ""}${tankDone ? `<div class="weigh-ready">✓ ${esc(w.verifiedVehicle)}호차 ${w.verifiedTank}번 수조 확인 완료</div><button class="full-button primary-button" type="button" data-action="complete-loading-task">🐟 활어 투입 완료 · 상차 확정</button>` : ""}<button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="open-loading-tank-change">🔄 긴급 수조 위치 변경</button>` : `<div class="departure-ready-card"><div class="icon">✓</div><h2>상차 완료</h2><p>${esc(new Date(w.loadedAt).toLocaleString("ko-KR"))} · ${esc(w.loadedBy || "담당자 미설정")}</p><p>${esc(w.verifiedVehicle)}호차 ${w.verifiedTank}번 수조</p></div><button class="full-button warning-button" type="button" data-action="reset-loading-task">상차 완료 취소 · 다시 확인</button>`}${logs ? `<div class="heading" style="margin:6px 0 0"><div><h2 style="font-size:18px">확인·오류 기록</h2><p>잘못된 수조와 밴드 확인 시도도 남습니다.</p></div></div>${logs}` : ""}<button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="back-loading-list">상차 작업 목록으로</button></div></div>`;
          $("#loadingModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function callLoadingTask() {
          const { d, i, w } = findLoadingTask();
          if (!d || !i || !w) return;
          if (!i.tankNumber) return alert("먼저 1~6번 수조를 지정해 주세요.");
          if (taskBandRequired(i) && !String(i.rubberBandColor || "").trim())
            return alert("밴드 색상을 먼저 입력해 주세요.");
          if (!w.calledAt) {
            w.calledAt = new Date().toISOString();
            w.calledBy = state.profile.driverName || "담당자 미설정";
            recordTaskLog(w, "call", `콜 전달: ${loadingSpeech(d, i, w)}`);
          }
          loadingError = "";
          speakText(loadingSpeech(d, i, w));
          saveState("활어 상차 콜 확인 전");
          openLoadingTask(
            d.id,
            i.id,
            w.id,
            w.calledAt
              ? "콜 내용을 읽었습니다. 활어를 받은 직원의 복창을 확인하세요."
              : "",
          );
        }
        function confirmLoadingRepeat() {
          const { d, i, w } = findLoadingTask();
          if (!d || !i || !w || !w.calledAt) return;
          if (
            !confirm(
              `${state.profile.vehicleNumber || "-"}호차 ${i.tankNumber}번 수조라고 직원이 정확하게 복창했습니까?`,
            )
          )
            return;
          w.repeatConfirmedAt = new Date().toISOString();
          w.repeatConfirmedBy = state.profile.driverName || "담당자 미설정";
          recordTaskLog(w, "repeat", "호차·수조 복창 확인 완료");
          loadingError = "";
          saveState("활어 복창 확인 전");
          openLoadingTask(d.id, i.id, w.id, "복창 확인을 완료했습니다.");
        }
        function confirmLoadingBand(match = true) {
          const { d, i, w } = findLoadingTask();
          if (!d || !i || !w || !w.repeatConfirmedAt) return;
          if (!match) {
            w.bandVerifiedAt = null;
            w.bandVerifiedBy = "";
            w.tankVerifiedAt = null;
            w.loadedAt = null;
            w.lastError = `밴드 불일치: 지시 ${taskBandText(i)}`;
            recordTaskLog(w, "band-error", w.lastError);
            loadingError = `밴드가 지시와 다릅니다. ${taskBandText(i)}로 바로잡은 후 다시 확인하세요.`;
            if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([400, 180, 400]);
            saveState("밴드 불일치 기록 전");
            return openLoadingTask(d.id, i.id, w.id);
          }
          w.bandVerifiedAt = new Date().toISOString();
          w.bandVerifiedBy = state.profile.driverName || "담당자 미설정";
          w.lastError = "";
          recordTaskLog(w, "band", `밴드 실물 확인: ${taskBandText(i)}`);
          loadingError = "";
          saveState("밴드 실물 확인 전");
          openLoadingTask(d.id, i.id, w.id, "밴드 색상과 수량이 일치합니다.");
        }
        function normalizeVehicleCode(value) {
          return String(value || "")
            .trim()
            .replace(/호차/g, "")
            .replace(/\s+/g, "")
            .toLowerCase();
        }
        function verifyLoadingTank(
          actualTank,
          actualVehicle = state.profile.vehicleNumber,
          source = "번호 직접 확인",
        ) {
          const { d, i, w } = findLoadingTask();
          if (
            !d ||
            !i ||
            !w ||
            !w.repeatConfirmedAt ||
            (taskBandRequired(i) && !w.bandVerifiedAt)
          )
            return;
          const expectedVehicle = normalizeVehicleCode(
              state.profile.vehicleNumber,
            ),
            seenVehicle = normalizeVehicleCode(actualVehicle),
            expectedTank = Number(i.tankNumber),
            seenTank = Number(actualTank),
            vehicleOk = expectedVehicle && expectedVehicle === seenVehicle,
            tankOk = expectedTank === seenTank;
          if (!vehicleOk || !tankOk) {
            w.tankVerifiedAt = null;
            w.tankVerifiedBy = "";
            w.verifiedVehicle = actualVehicle || "미확인";
            w.verifiedTank = seenTank || 0;
            w.loadedAt = null;
            w.lastError = `잘못된 위치 확인: ${actualVehicle || "-"}호차 ${seenTank || "-"}번 / 지정 ${state.profile.vehicleNumber || "-"}호차 ${expectedTank}번`;
            recordTaskLog(w, "tank-error", `${source} · ${w.lastError}`);
            loadingError = `잘못된 수조입니다. 지정 위치는 ${state.profile.vehicleNumber || "-"}호차 ${expectedTank}번 수조입니다.`;
            if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([600, 200, 600, 200, 600]);
            saveState("잘못된 수조 확인 기록 전");
            return openLoadingTask(d.id, i.id, w.id);
          }
          w.tankVerifiedAt = new Date().toISOString();
          w.tankVerifiedBy = state.profile.driverName || "담당자 미설정";
          w.verifiedVehicle = state.profile.vehicleNumber;
          w.verifiedTank = expectedTank;
          w.lastError = "";
          recordTaskLog(
            w,
            "tank",
            `${source} · ${state.profile.vehicleNumber}호차 ${expectedTank}번 수조 일치`,
          );
          loadingError = "";
          if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([40, 50, 40]);
          saveState("수조 위치 확인 전");
          openLoadingTask(d.id, i.id, w.id, "지정된 차량과 수조가 일치합니다.");
        }
        function completeLoadingTask() {
          const { d, i, w } = findLoadingTask();
          if (!d || !i || !w || !w.tankVerifiedAt)
            return alert("실제 수조를 먼저 확인해 주세요.");
          if (
            Number(w.verifiedTank) !== Number(i.tankNumber) ||
            normalizeVehicleCode(w.verifiedVehicle) !==
              normalizeVehicleCode(state.profile.vehicleNumber)
          )
            return verifyLoadingTank(
              w.verifiedTank,
              w.verifiedVehicle,
              "완료 직전 재검사",
            );
          w.loadedAt = new Date().toISOString();
          w.loadedBy = state.profile.driverName || "담당자 미설정";
          recordTaskLog(
            w,
            "loaded",
            `${state.profile.vehicleNumber}호차 ${i.tankNumber}번 수조 활어 투입 완료`,
          );
          syncItemTaskLoad(i);
          loadingError = "";
          saveState("활어 개체 상차 완료 전");
          renderToday();
          if (state.preferences?.autoNextLoading !== false) {
            const remaining = loadingTaskRows().filter(
                ({ w: task }) => !task.loadedAt,
              ),
              sameFilter = remaining.find(
                ({ d: nextDelivery, i: nextItem }) =>
                  (!loadingFilterDeliveryId ||
                    nextDelivery.id === loadingFilterDeliveryId) &&
                  (!loadingFilterItemId || nextItem.id === loadingFilterItemId),
              ),
              next = sameFilter || remaining[0];
            if (next) {
              if (!sameFilter) {
                loadingFilterDeliveryId = 0;
                loadingFilterItemId = 0;
              }
              return openLoadingTask(
                next.d.id,
                next.i.id,
                next.w.id,
                `${taskCode(w)} 상차 완료 · 다음 작업 ${taskCode(next.w)}을 자동으로 열었습니다.`,
              );
            }
            return openLoadingControl(
              "모든 활어의 개체별 상차를 완료했습니다.",
              0,
              0,
            );
          }
          openLoadingTask(
            d.id,
            i.id,
            w.id,
            "활어 한 마리의 상차를 완료했습니다.",
          );
        }
        function resetLoadingTask() {
          const { d, i, w } = findLoadingTask();
          if (
            !d ||
            !i ||
            !w ||
            !confirm(
              "이 활어의 상차 완료와 모든 확인 단계를 취소하고 처음부터 다시 확인할까요?",
            )
          )
            return;
          recordTaskLog(w, "reset", "상차 완료 취소 후 처음부터 재확인");
          resetTaskWorkflow(w);
          syncItemTaskLoad(i);
          loadingError = "";
          saveState("활어 상차 완료 취소 전");
          renderToday();
          openLoadingTask(
            d.id,
            i.id,
            w.id,
            "상차 완료를 취소했습니다. 콜부터 다시 확인해 주세요.",
          );
        }
        function tankQrValue(tank) {
          return `JB-TANK|${encodeURIComponent(String(state.profile.vehicleNumber || ""))}|${Number(tank)}`;
        }
        function openQrLabels() {
          stopQrScanner();
          qrReturnView = view === "settings" ? "settings" : "loading";
          const vehicle = state.profile.vehicleNumber;
          if (!vehicle)
            return alert("설정에서 차량 호차를 먼저 입력해 주세요.");
          const labels = Array.from(
            { length: 6 },
            (_, n) =>
              `<article class="qr-label"><strong>${esc(vehicle)}호차 ${n + 1}번 수조</strong><div class="qr-code" data-qr-value="${esc(tankQrValue(n + 1))}"><small>QR 생성 중</small></div><small>${esc(tankQrValue(n + 1))}</small></article>`,
          ).join("");
          $("#qrModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>🏷️ ${esc(vehicle)}호차 수조 QR 라벨</h2><p>방수 코팅 후 각 수조 앞에 크게 부착하세요.</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-qr">×</button></div><div class="modal-body"><div id="qrLabelSheet" class="qr-label-sheet">${labels}</div><button class="full-button primary-button" type="button" data-action="print-qr-labels">🖨️ 1~6번 QR 라벨 인쇄</button><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="close-qr">${qrReturnView === "settings" ? "설정으로 돌아가기" : "상차 관제로 돌아가기"}</button></div></div>`;
          $("#loadingModal").classList.add("hidden");
          $("#qrModal").classList.remove("hidden");
          requestAnimationFrame(renderQrLabels);
        }
        function renderQrLabels() {
          document
            .querySelectorAll("#qrLabelSheet [data-qr-value]")
            .forEach((node) => {
              const value = node.dataset.qrValue;
              node.innerHTML = "";
              if (typeof QRCode === "function")
                new QRCode(node, {
                  text: value,
                  width: 150,
                  height: 150,
                  colorDark: "#000000",
                  colorLight: "#ffffff",
                  correctLevel: QRCode.CorrectLevel.H,
                });
              else
                node.innerHTML = `<div class="workflow-error">QR 모듈을 불러오지 못했습니다.<br>${esc(value)}</div>`;
            });
        }
        function printQrLabels() {
          const labels = [
            ...document.querySelectorAll("#qrLabelSheet .qr-label"),
          ]
            .map((label, index) => {
              const canvas = label.querySelector("canvas"),
                img = label.querySelector("img"),
                src = canvas?.toDataURL?.("image/png") || img?.src || "";
              return `<article class="qr-label"><strong>${esc(state.profile.vehicleNumber)}호차 ${index + 1}번 수조</strong>${src ? `<img style="width:150px;height:150px" src="${src}" alt="${index + 1}번 수조 QR">` : ""}<small>${esc(tankQrValue(index + 1))}</small></article>`;
            })
            .join("");
          printElement(`<div class="qr-label-sheet">${labels}</div>`);
        }
        async function openQrScanner() {
          const { d, i, w } = findLoadingTask();
          if (!d || !i || !w) return;
          if (
            !w.repeatConfirmedAt ||
            (taskBandRequired(i) && !w.bandVerifiedAt)
          )
            return alert("복창과 밴드 확인을 먼저 완료해 주세요.");
          stopQrScanner();
          qrReturnView = "task";
          $("#loadingModal").classList.add("hidden");
          $("#qrModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>📷 수조 QR 확인</h2><p>지정 위치: ${esc(state.profile.vehicleNumber)}호차 ${i.tankNumber}번 수조</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-qr-scanner">×</button></div><div class="modal-body"><div id="qrScanMessage" class="weigh-notice">카메라를 수조의 QR 라벨에 가까이 비춰 주세요.</div><div class="qr-scanner"><video id="qrVideo" playsinline muted></video><div class="qr-guide"></div></div><canvas id="qrCanvas" class="hidden"></canvas><div class="tank-verify-grid">${Array.from({ length: 6 }, (_, n) => `<button type="button" data-action="verify-loading-tank" data-tank="${n + 1}">${n + 1}번 수동 확인</button>`).join("")}</div><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="close-qr-scanner">카메라 닫기</button></div></div>`;
          $("#qrModal").classList.remove("hidden");
          try {
            if (!navigator.mediaDevices?.getUserMedia)
              throw new Error("카메라 기능을 지원하지 않습니다.");
            qrStream = await navigator.mediaDevices.getUserMedia({
              video: { facingMode: { ideal: "environment" } },
              audio: false,
            });
            const video = $("#qrVideo");
            video.srcObject = qrStream;
            await video.play();
            scanQrFrame();
          } catch (error) {
            const message = $("#qrScanMessage");
            if (message) {
              message.className = "workflow-error";
              message.textContent = `카메라를 열지 못했습니다. 아래 수조 번호로 직접 확인하세요. (${error.message || "권한 확인"})`;
            }
          }
        }
        function scanQrFrame() {
          const video = $("#qrVideo"),
            canvas = $("#qrCanvas");
          if (!video || !canvas || !qrStream) return;
          if (video.readyState >= 2 && video.videoWidth) {
            canvas.width = video.videoWidth;
            canvas.height = video.videoHeight;
            const ctx = canvas.getContext("2d", { willReadFrequently: true });
            ctx.drawImage(video, 0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height);
            if (typeof jsQR === "function") {
