              const image = ctx.getImageData(0, 0, canvas.width, canvas.height),
                code = jsQR(image.data, image.width, image.height, {
                  inversionAttempts: "dontInvert",
                });
              if (code?.data) return handleTankQr(code.data);
            }
          }
          qrTimer = requestAnimationFrame(scanQrFrame);
        }
        function handleTankQr(value) {
          const match = /^JB-TANK\|(.+)\|([1-6])$/.exec(String(value || ""));
          if (!match) {
            const message = $("#qrScanMessage");
            if (message) {
              message.className = "workflow-error";
              message.textContent =
                "장백수산 수조 QR이 아닙니다. 올바른 라벨을 비춰 주세요.";
            }
            return;
          }
          let vehicle = "";
          try {
            vehicle = decodeURIComponent(match[1]);
          } catch {
            vehicle = match[1];
          }
          const tank = Number(match[2]);
          stopQrScanner();
          closeModal("qrModal");
          $("#loadingModal").classList.remove("hidden");
          verifyLoadingTank(tank, vehicle, "QR 카메라 확인");
        }
        function stopQrScanner() {
          if (qrTimer) {
            cancelAnimationFrame(qrTimer);
            qrTimer = null;
          }
          if (qrStream) {
            qrStream.getTracks().forEach((track) => track.stop());
            qrStream = null;
          }
        }
        function closeQr(returnToTask = false) {
          stopQrScanner();
          closeModal("qrModal");
          if ((returnToTask || qrReturnView === "task") && findLoadingTask().w)
            return openLoadingTask(
              loadingDeliveryId,
              loadingItemId,
              loadingWeightId,
            );
          if (qrReturnView === "settings") {
            renderSettings();
            return;
          }
          openLoadingControl("", loadingFilterDeliveryId, loadingFilterItemId);
        }

        function openUrgentList(message = "") {
          const rows = urgentRows(),
            cards = rows
              .map((d) => {
                const c = customerOf(d),
                  items = d.items
                    .map(
                      (i) =>
                        `${esc(i.species)} ${esc(i.requestedQty)}${esc(i.unit)} · ${tankLabel(i.tankNumber)}`,
                    )
                    .join("<br>");
                return `<article class="urgent-row"><div><strong>🚨 ${d.routeOrder}번 ${esc(c.name)}</strong><small>${items || "품목 없음"}</small></div><div class="two"><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="edit-urgent" data-id="${d.id}">내용·수조 수정</button><button class="full-button danger-button" type="button" data-action="ack-urgent-order" data-id="${d.id}">추가 발주·순서 확인 완료</button></div></article>`;
              })
              .join("");
          $("#urgentModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>🚨 긴급 추가 발주 확인</h2><p>추가 품목과 수조, 배송 순서를 확인합니다.</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-urgent">×</button></div><div class="modal-body">${message ? `<div class="weigh-ready">✓ ${esc(message)}</div>` : ""}<div class="senior-guide"><b>꼭 확인할 3가지</b>① 추가 품목 ② 넣을 수조 ③ 바뀐 배송 순서</div>${cards || `<div class="departure-ready-card"><div class="icon">✓</div><h2>긴급 추가 발주 확인 완료</h2><p>미확인 추가 발주가 없습니다.</p></div>`}<button class="full-button warning-button" type="button" data-action="urgent-reorder">배송 순서 수정하기</button><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="close-urgent">배송 화면으로 돌아가기</button></div></div>`;
          $("#urgentModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function acknowledgeUrgent(id) {
          const d = state.deliveries.find((x) => x.id === Number(id));
          if (!d || d.status === "completed" || d.status === "cancelled")
            return;
          d.isUrgentAdditional = true;
          d.urgentAcknowledged = true;
          d.urgentAcknowledgedAt = new Date().toISOString();
          if (d.status === "new") d.status = "ready";
          saveState("긴급 추가 발주 확인 전");
          stopAlarm();
          renderToday();
          openUrgentList(
            `${customerOf(d).name} 긴급 추가 발주를 확인했습니다.`,
          );
        }

        function openBoxCompare(message = "") {
          const rows = boxCompareRows(),
            cards = rows
              .map((d) => {
                const c = customerOf(d),
                  planned = d.boxes.length,
                  actual = d.loadedBoxCount,
                  ok = d.boxCountConfirmed && actual === planned;
                return `<article class="box-compare-row ${d.boxCountConfirmed && !ok ? "mismatch" : ""}" data-box-compare="${d.id}"><div><strong>${d.routeOrder}번 ${esc(c.name)}</strong><small>계획된 박스 내용을 먼저 보고 실제 상차 박스를 세어 주세요.</small></div><div class="load-controls"><button type="button" data-action="box-step" data-step="-1">−</button><input data-box-count-input type="number" inputmode="numeric" min="0" max="99" value="${actual}" aria-label="${esc(c.name)} 실제 상차 박스 수"><button type="button" data-action="box-step" data-step="1">＋</button></div><div class="box-count-result ${ok ? "ok" : d.boxCountConfirmed ? "bad" : ""}">계획 ${planned}박스 / 실제 ${actual}박스 · ${ok ? "✓ 일치" : d.boxCountConfirmed ? "⚠ 불일치" : "대조 전"}</div><button class="full-button ${ok ? "warning-button" : "primary-button"}" type="button" data-action="confirm-box-count" data-id="${d.id}">${ok ? "수량 다시 확인" : "이 수량으로 대조 확인"}</button></article>`;
              })
              .join("");
          $("#boxModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>📦 박스 수량 대조</h2><p>계획 수량과 실제 차량 상차 수량을 비교합니다.</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-box">×</button></div><div class="modal-body">${message ? `<div class="weigh-ready">${esc(message)}</div>` : ""}<div class="senior-guide"><b>확인 방법</b>① 실제 박스 세기 → ② −/＋로 수량 맞추기 → ③ 대조 확인 누르기</div>${cards || `<div class="empty">오늘 대조할 박스가 없습니다.</div>`}<button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="close-box">배송 화면으로 돌아가기</button></div></div>`;
          $("#boxModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function confirmBoxCount(id, button) {
          const d = state.deliveries.find((x) => x.id === Number(id)),
            input = button
              .closest("[data-box-compare]")
              ?.querySelector("[data-box-count-input]");
          if (!d || !input) return;
          d.loadedBoxCount = Math.max(0, Math.floor(Number(input.value) || 0));
          d.boxCountConfirmed = true;
          d.boxCountConfirmedAt = new Date().toISOString();
          saveState("박스 수량 대조 전");
          renderToday();
          const ok = d.loadedBoxCount === d.boxes.length;
          openBoxCompare(
            `${customerOf(d).name} · 계획 ${d.boxes.length}박스 / 실제 ${d.loadedBoxCount}박스 ${ok ? "일치했습니다." : "불일치합니다. 박스를 다시 확인해 주세요."}`,
          );
        }

        function issueButtonLabel(type) {
          return (
            {
              empty: "배송 추가",
              new: "발주 확인",
              urgent: "긴급 확인",
              handover: "특이사항 확인",
              weigh: "계근하기",
              tank: "수조 지정",
              workflow: "상차 관제",
              band: "밴드 수정",
              load: "상차 확인",
              box: "박스 대조",
              price: "단가 입력",
            }[type] || "확인"
          );
        }
        function issueIcon(type) {
          return (
            {
              empty: "＋",
              new: "!",
              urgent: "🚨",
              handover: "📝",
              weigh: "⚖",
              tank: "💧",
              workflow: "📣",
              band: "●",
              load: "✓",
              box: "📦",
              price: "₩",
            }[type] || "!"
          );
        }
        function openDepartureCheck() {
          const issues = departureIssues(),
            loads = tankLoadRows(),
            boxes = boxCompareRows(),
            handovers = pendingHandoverRows(),
            record = state.departureChecks?.[workDate],
            ready = departureReady(),
            confirmedAt = record?.at
              ? new Date(record.at).toLocaleString("ko-KR")
              : "";
          const rows = issues
            .map(
              (issue, index) =>
                `<article class="issue-row"><span class="issue-icon">${issueIcon(issue.type)}</span><div><strong>${esc(issue.title)}</strong><small>${esc(issue.detail)}</small></div><button type="button" data-action="resolve-departure-issue" data-index="${index}">${issueButtonLabel(issue.type)}</button></article>`,
            )
            .join("");
          $("#departureModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>🚚 출차 전 최종 점검</h2><p>${esc(workDate)} · ${esc(state.profile.vehicleNumber)}호차</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-departure">×</button></div><div class="modal-body"><div class="check-summary"><div><small>인계 미확인</small><strong>${handovers.length}</strong></div><div><small>수조 상차</small><strong>${loads.filter((x) => x.i.tankLoaded).length}/${loads.length}</strong></div><div><small>박스 일치</small><strong>${boxes.filter((d) => d.boxCountConfirmed && d.loadedBoxCount === d.boxes.length).length}/${boxes.length}</strong></div><div><small>문제 항목</small><strong>${issues.length}</strong></div></div>${ready ? `<div class="departure-ready-card"><div class="icon">✓</div><h2>출차 준비 완료</h2><p>${esc(confirmedAt)} · ${esc(state.profile.driverName)} 확인</p><p>이후 발주·수조·박스·계근·점포 특이사항이 바뀌면 자동으로 재점검 상태가 됩니다.</p></div>` : issues.length ? `<div class="weigh-notice">아래 빨간 항목을 모두 처리하면 ‘출차 준비 완료’ 버튼이 나타납니다.</div><div class="issue-list">${rows}</div>` : `<div class="weigh-ready">모든 항목이 일치합니다. 아래 버튼으로 최종 확인해 주세요.</div><button class="full-button primary-button" type="button" data-action="confirm-departure">✓ 모든 내용 확인 · 출차 준비 완료</button>`}<button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="close-departure">배송 화면으로 돌아가기</button></div></div>`;
          $("#departureModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function confirmDeparture() {
          const issues = departureIssues();
          if (issues.length) return openDepartureCheck();
          state.departureChecks = state.departureChecks || {};
          state.departureChecks[workDate] = {
            fingerprint: departureFingerprint(),
            at: new Date().toISOString(),
            driverName: state.profile.driverName,
            vehicleNumber: state.profile.vehicleNumber,
          };
          saveState("출차 준비 완료 전");
          renderToday();
          openDepartureCheck();
        }
        function resolveDepartureIssue(index) {
          const issue = departureIssues()[Number(index)];
          if (!issue) return openDepartureCheck();
          closeModal("departureModal");
          if (issue.type === "empty") return openDelivery();
          if (issue.type === "new") {
            issue.d.status = "ready";
            saveState("신규 발주 확인 전");
            stopAlarm();
            renderToday();
            return openDepartureCheck();
          }
          if (issue.type === "urgent") return openUrgentList();
          if (issue.type === "handover")
            return openStoreGuide(issue.d.id, "departure");
          if (issue.type === "weigh")
            return openWeighItem(issue.d.id, issue.i.id);
          if (issue.type === "workflow")
            return openLoadingControl("", issue.d.id, issue.i.id);
          if (issue.type === "band") return openDelivery(issue.d.id);
          if (issue.type === "tank" || issue.type === "load")
            return openTankManager();
          if (issue.type === "box") return openBoxCompare();
          if (issue.type === "price") return openChecklist(issue.d.id);
        }

        function backupRows() {
          return readJSON(AUTO_BACKUP_KEY, []).slice().reverse();
        }
        function createAutoBackup() {
          saveAutoSnapshot(JSON.stringify(state), "사용자 직접 백업");
          openAutoBackups("현재 내용을 안전하게 백업했습니다.");
        }
        function openAutoBackups(message = "") {
          const rows = backupRows(),
            cards = rows
              .map((entry) => {
                let info = "내용 확인 불가";
                try {
                  const raw = JSON.parse(entry.data),
                    dateCount = new Set(
                      (raw.deliveries || []).map((d) => d.deliveryDate),
                    ).size;
                  info = `거래처 ${(raw.customers || []).length}곳 · 배송 ${(raw.deliveries || []).length}건 · 업무일 ${dateCount}일`;
                } catch {}
                return `<article class="backup-row"><div><strong>${esc(new Date(entry.at).toLocaleString("ko-KR"))}</strong><small>${esc(entry.reason)}<br>${esc(info)}</small></div><button type="button" data-action="restore-auto-backup" data-id="${entry.id}">이 시점으로 복구</button></article>`;
              })
              .join("");
          $("#backupModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>🛟 자동 백업·복구</h2><p>최근 변경 전 자료를 최대 8개까지 보관합니다.</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-backups">×</button></div><div class="modal-body">${message ? `<div class="weigh-ready">✓ ${esc(message)}</div>` : ""}<button class="full-button primary-button" type="button" data-action="create-auto-backup">지금 상태 백업 만들기</button>${cards || `<div class="empty">아직 자동 백업이 없습니다.<br>자료를 수정하면 변경 전 내용이 자동 보관됩니다.</div>`}<div class="notice">복구를 실행해도 현재 자료를 먼저 한 번 더 백업하므로 되돌릴 수 있습니다.</div><button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="close-backups">설정 화면으로 돌아가기</button></div></div>`;
          $("#backupModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function restoreAutoBackup(id) {
          const entry = readJSON(AUTO_BACKUP_KEY, []).find(
            (x) => String(x.id) === String(id),
          );
          if (!entry) return alert("선택한 백업을 찾지 못했습니다.");
          if (
            !confirm(
              `${new Date(entry.at).toLocaleString("ko-KR")} 자료로 복구할까요?\n현재 내용도 복구 전에 자동 백업됩니다.`,
            )
          )
            return;
          try {
            const raw = JSON.parse(entry.data);
            if (
              !raw.profile ||
              !Array.isArray(raw.customers) ||
              !Array.isArray(raw.deliveries)
            )
              throw new Error();
            saveAutoSnapshot(JSON.stringify(state), "백업 복구 직전");
            state = {
              version: 5,
              profile: {
                companyName: raw.profile.companyName || "",
                driverName: raw.profile.driverName || "",
                vehicleNumber: raw.profile.vehicleNumber || "",
              },
              customers: raw.customers.map((c, i) => ({
                ...c,
                id: Number(c.id) || newId(),
                routeOrder: Number(c.routeOrder) || i + 1,
              })),
              deliveries: raw.deliveries.map(normalizeDelivery),
              departureChecks:
                raw.departureChecks && typeof raw.departureChecks === "object"
                  ? raw.departureChecks
                  : {},
              preferences: {
                autoNextLoading:
                  raw.preferences?.autoNextLoading === undefined
                    ? true
                    : Boolean(raw.preferences.autoNextLoading),
                weightRules: normalizeWeightRules(raw.preferences?.weightRules),
              },
              workClosures:
                raw.workClosures && typeof raw.workClosures === "object"
                  ? raw.workClosures
                  : {},
              workClosureHistory: Array.isArray(raw.workClosureHistory)
                ? raw.workClosureHistory.slice(-200)
                : [],
            };
            saveState("자동 백업 복구 전");
            render();
            openAutoBackups("선택한 시점으로 복구했습니다.");
          } catch {
            alert("백업 자료를 읽을 수 없습니다.");
          }
        }

        function openChecklist(id, notice = "") {
          selectedDeliveryId = id;
          const d = state.deliveries.find((x) => x.id === id);
          if (!d) return;
          const c = customerOf(d),
            p = progress(d),
            locked = d.status === "completed",
            weighReady = deliveryWeighingReady(d),
            guideExists = hasHandover(c),
            guideOk = handoverAcknowledged(d, c);
          const itemHtml = d.items
            .map((i) => {
              const weightCount = (i.weighings || []).length;
              return `<article class="check-card ${i.checked ? "checked" : ""}" data-check-item="${i.id}"><div class="check-main"><input type="checkbox" data-check-toggle="item" ${i.checked ? "checked" : ""} ${locked ? "disabled" : ""}><span class="check-copy"><strong>${esc(i.species)} · ${esc(quantityText(i))}</strong><small>${esc(i.size)} / ${esc(i.originCountry)} / ${esc(i.processing)}</small><span class="important-tags"><span class="tag">${tankLabel(i.tankNumber)}</span>${i.tankNumber ? `<span class="tag" style="color:${i.tankLoaded ? "#155d32" : "#7b3f0c"};background:${i.tankLoaded ? "#dff4e6" : "#ffedda"}">수조 실제 상차 ${i.tankLoaded ? "완료" : "미확인"}</span>` : ""}${isWeighable(i) ? `<span class="tag" style="color:${i.weighingConfirmed ? "#155d32" : "#7b3f0c"};background:${i.weighingConfirmed ? "#dff4e6" : "#ffedda"}">계근 ${weightCount}마리 · ${weightTotal(i).toFixed(3)}kg ${i.weighingConfirmed ? "확정" : "미확정"}</span>` : ""}${i.rubberBand ? `<span class="tag">밴드 ${esc(i.rubberBandColor)} ${i.rubberBandQuantity}개</span>` : ""}${i.includedNote ? `<span class="tag memo">${esc(i.includedNote)}</span>` : ""}</span></span></div><div class="tank-current"><div><span>현재 상차 위치</span><strong>${tankLabel(i.tankNumber)}</strong></div>${locked ? "" : `<button type="button" data-action="open-tank-change" data-delivery-id="${d.id}" data-item-id="${i.id}" data-source="check">🔄 수조 변경</button>`}</div><div class="check-inputs"><label class="field"><span>${weightCount ? "계근 합계 kg" : "실제 중량 kg"}</span><input class="control" data-check-field="actualWeight" type="number" min="0" step=".001" value="${i.actualWeight ?? ""}" ${locked || weightCount ? "disabled" : ""}></label><label class="field"><span>확정 단가</span><input class="control" data-check-field="unitPrice" type="number" min="0" value="${i.unitPrice || ""}" ${locked ? "disabled" : ""}></label></div>${isWeighable(i) && !locked ? `<button class="full-button outline-button" type="button" data-action="open-weigh-item" data-delivery-id="${d.id}" data-item-id="${i.id}">⚖️ 개별 계근 ${weightCount ? "확인·수정" : "입력"}</button>` : ""}</article>`;
            })
            .join("");
          const boxes = d.boxes
            .map(
              (b) =>
                `<article class="check-card ${b.checked ? "checked" : ""}" data-check-box="${b.id}"><div class="check-main"><input type="checkbox" data-check-toggle="box" ${b.checked ? "checked" : ""} ${locked ? "disabled" : ""}><span class="check-copy"><strong>${b.boxNumber}번 박스</strong><small>${esc(b.contents || "내용 미입력")}</small></span>${locked ? "" : `<button class="mini" type="button" data-action="delete-check-box" data-id="${b.id}">삭제</button>`}</div>${locked ? "" : `<input class="control" data-check-box-content value="${esc(b.contents)}" placeholder="박스 동봉 내역">`}</article>`,
            )
            .join("");
          const amount = d.items.reduce((s, i) => s + itemAmount(i), 0),
            allChecked = p.total > 0 && p.done === p.total,
            canComplete = allChecked && weighReady,
            boxMatched =
              !d.boxes.length ||
              (d.boxCountConfirmed && d.loadedBoxCount === d.boxes.length);
          $("#checkModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>${esc(c.name)}</h2><p>${d.routeOrder}번째 배송지 · ${p.done}/${p.total} 확인</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-check">×</button></div><div class="modal-body">${notice ? `<div class="weigh-ready">✓ ${esc(notice)}<br>하차 확인 체크가 자동 해제되었습니다.</div>` : ""}${guideExists ? `<div class="handover-card ${guideOk ? "ready" : ""}"><div><strong>${guideOk ? "✓ 점포 특이사항 확인 완료" : "📝 점포 특이사항 확인 필요"}</strong><small>출입 방법·물건 위치·금지사항을 배송 전에 확인하세요.</small></div><button type="button" data-action="open-store-guide" data-id="${d.id}" data-source="check">내용 보기</button></div>` : ""}<div class="heading"><div><h2 style="font-size:18px">어종·수조·요구사항</h2><p>실물과 대조한 뒤 체크하세요.</p></div></div>${itemHtml || `<div class="empty">품목이 없습니다.</div>`}<div class="heading" style="margin-top:6px"><div><h2 style="font-size:18px">박스·동봉품</h2><p>${esc(d.coPackNote || "동봉품 전체 메모 없음")}</p></div>${locked ? "" : `<button class="mini" type="button" data-action="add-check-box">＋ 박스</button>`}</div>${d.boxes.length ? `<div class="box-count-result ${boxMatched ? "ok" : "bad"}">출차 대조: 계획 ${d.boxes.length}박스 / 실제 ${d.loadedBoxCount}박스 · ${boxMatched ? "일치" : "대조 필요"}</div>` : ""}${boxes || `<div class="empty">등록된 박스가 없습니다.</div>`}${weighReady ? "" : `<div class="weigh-notice no-print">활어 계근을 모두 확정해야 거래명세서를 출력하고 하차 완료할 수 있습니다.</div>`}<div class="balance-editor no-print"><div><strong>전미수(전날 미수)</strong><small>거래명세서에 항상 표시됩니다.</small></div><label class="field"><span>금액</span><input id="previousBalanceInput" class="control" type="number" inputmode="numeric" min="0" step="1" value="${Number(d.previousBalance) || 0}"></label><button type="button" data-action="save-previous-balance">수정 적용</button><small id="balanceSaved">금액을 수정한 뒤 ‘수정 적용’을 누르세요.</small></div><div id="statementView" class="statement">${statementHTML(d, c, amount)}</div><div class="output-grid no-print"><button type="button" data-action="print-statement" ${weighReady ? "" : "disabled"}>🖨️ 인쇄</button><button type="button" data-action="image-statement" data-format="png" ${weighReady ? "" : "disabled"}>PNG 저장</button><button type="button" data-action="image-statement" data-format="jpg" ${weighReady ? "" : "disabled"}>JPG 저장</button></div>${locked ? "" : `<button class="full-button outline-button no-print" type="button" data-action="edit-delivery" data-id="${d.id}">발주·포장 내용 수정</button>`}${locked ? `<button class="full-button warning-button no-print" type="button" data-action="undo-complete" data-id="${d.id}">하차 완료 취소 · 다시 확인</button>` : `<button class="full-button primary-button no-print" type="button" data-action="complete-delivery" data-id="${d.id}" ${canComplete ? "" : "disabled"}>${!weighReady ? "활어 계근을 먼저 확정해 주세요" : allChecked ? "모두 확인 · 하차 완료" : "어종과 박스를 모두 확인해 주세요"}</button>`}</div></div>`;
          $("#checkModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function statementHTML(d, c, amount) {
          const lines = d.items
            .map((i) => {
              const base = baseAmount(i),
                fee =
                  i.category === "필렛 제품"
                    ? (Number(i.actualWeight ?? i.requestedQty) || 0) *
                      (Number(i.processingFeePerKg) || 0)
                    : 0,
                weightNote = (i.weighings || []).length
                  ? ` / 개별계근 ${i.weighings.length}마리 ${weightTotal(i).toFixed(3)}kg${i.weighingConfirmed ? " 확정" : " 미확정"}`
                  : "";
              return `<div class="statement-line"><span>${esc(i.species)} · ${esc(i.originCountry)} · ${esc(quantityText(i))}<br><small>${esc(i.size)} / ${money(i.unitPrice)}원/${esc(i.priceUnit)}당${fee ? ` / 작업비 ${money(i.processingFeePerKg)}원/kg` : ""}${weightNote}</small></span><b>${money(base + fee)}원</b></div>`;
            })
            .join("");
          const previous = Number(d.previousBalance) || 0,
            due = amount + previous;
          return `<h1>거래명세서</h1><div class="statement-meta"><p><span>공급자</span><b>${esc(state.profile.companyName || "-")}</b></p><p><span>담당자</span><b>${esc(state.profile.driverName || "-")} · ${esc(state.profile.vehicleNumber || "-")}호차</b></p><p><span>거래처</span><b>${esc(c.name)}</b></p><p><span>납품처</span><b>${esc(c.deliveryPlace || "-")}</b></p><p class="wide"><span>주소</span><b>${esc(c.address || "-")}</b></p><p><span>연락처</span><b>${esc(c.phone || "-")}</b></p><p><span>배송일</span><b>${esc(d.deliveryDate)}</b></p></div>${lines}<div class="statement-sub"><span>당일 공급금액</span><b>${money(amount)}원</b></div><div class="statement-sub" style="color:var(--amber)"><span>전미수(전날 미수)</span><b>${money(previous)}원</b></div><div class="statement-total"><span>최종 합계</span><b>${money(due)}원</b></div>${d.notes ? `<div class="statement-note">${esc(d.notes)}</div>` : ""}`;
        }

        function updateCheckItem(itemId, key, value) {
          const d = state.deliveries.find((x) => x.id === selectedDeliveryId);
          if (!d || d.status === "completed") return;
          const item = d.items.find((i) => i.id === itemId);
          if (!item) return;
          const before = item[key];
          item[key] = ["tankNumber", "actualWeight", "unitPrice"].includes(key)
            ? value === ""
              ? null
              : Number(value)
            : value;
          if (key === "actualWeight" && Number(before) !== Number(item[key]))
            resetTankLoad(item);
          saveState("하차 품목 수정 전");
        }
        function updateCheckBox(boxId, key, value) {
          const d = state.deliveries.find((x) => x.id === selectedDeliveryId);
          if (!d || d.status === "completed") return;
          const box = d.boxes.find((b) => b.id === boxId);
          if (box) {
            box[key] = value;
            saveState();
          }
        }
        function savePreviousBalance() {
          const d = state.deliveries.find((x) => x.id === selectedDeliveryId),
            input = $("#previousBalanceInput"),
            message = $("#balanceSaved");
          if (!d || !input) return;
          const value = Math.max(0, Math.round(Number(input.value) || 0));
          d.previousBalance = value;
          input.value = value;
          saveState("전미수 수정 전");
          refreshStatement();
          renderToday();
          if (message) {
            message.textContent = `✓ 전미수 ${money(value)}원으로 저장했습니다.`;
            message.classList.add("balance-saved");
          }
        }
        function refreshStatement() {
          const d = state.deliveries.find((x) => x.id === selectedDeliveryId),
            node = $("#statementView");
          if (!d || !node) return;
          node.innerHTML = statementHTML(
            d,
            customerOf(d),
            d.items.reduce((s, i) => s + itemAmount(i), 0),
          );
        }
        function moveDelivery(id, target) {
          const list = deliveries().filter((d) => d.status !== "cancelled"),
            from = list.findIndex((d) => d.id === id),
            to = Math.max(0, Math.min(list.length - 1, target));
          if (from < 0 || from === to) return;
          const [moved] = list.splice(from, 1);
          list.splice(to, 0, moved);
          list.forEach((d, i) => {
            const real = state.deliveries.find((x) => x.id === d.id);
            real.routeOrder = i + 1;
          });
          saveState();
          renderToday();
        }
        function normalizeRoutes() {
          deliveries()
            .filter((d) => d.status !== "cancelled")
            .forEach((d, i) => (d.routeOrder = i + 1));
        }

        function purchaseGroups() {
          const groups = {};
          deliveries()
            .filter((d) => !["completed", "cancelled"].includes(d.status))
            .forEach((d) => {
              const c = customerOf(d);
              d.items.forEach((i) => {
                const key = [
                  i.category,
                  i.species,
                  i.size,
                  i.originCountry,
                  i.processing,
                  i.unit,
                  i.includedNote,
                  i.rubberBand
                    ? `${i.rubberBandColor}-${i.rubberBandQuantity}`
                    : "",
                ].join("||");
                if (!groups[key]) groups[key] = { ...i, stores: [], total: 0 };
                groups[key].stores.push({
                  name: c.name,
                  qty: Number(i.requestedQty) || 0,
                });
                groups[key].total += Number(i.requestedQty) || 0;
              });
            });
          return Object.values(groups);
        }
        function openPurchase() {
          const groups = purchaseGroups();
          const content = `<div id="purchaseSheet" class="purchase-sheet"><h2>당일 매입발주서</h2><p style="margin:3px 0;color:var(--muted);font-size:13px">${esc(workDate)} · ${esc(state.profile.vehicleNumber)}호차</p>${groups.map((g) => `<article class="purchase-group"><strong>${esc(g.species)} · ${esc(g.size)}</strong><small>${esc(g.category)} / ${esc(g.originCountry)} / ${esc(g.processing)}${g.includedNote ? ` / ${esc(g.includedNote)}` : ""}${g.rubberBand ? ` / 밴드 ${esc(g.rubberBandColor)} ${g.rubberBandQuantity}개` : ""}</small>${g.stores.map((s) => `<div class="purchase-store"><span>${esc(s.name)}</span><span>${s.qty}${esc(g.unit)}</span></div>`).join("")}<div class="purchase-total"><span>총 매입 수량</span><span>${g.total}${esc(g.unit)}</span></div></article>`).join("") || `<div class="empty">매입할 품목이 없습니다.</div>`}</div>`;
          $("#purchaseModal").innerHTML =
            `<div class="modal-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>당일 매입발주서</h2><p>원산지·작업·메모가 다르면 별도 품목으로 표시됩니다.</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-purchase">×</button></div><div class="modal-body">${content}<div class="output-grid"><button type="button" data-action="print-purchase">🖨️ 인쇄</button><button type="button" data-action="image-purchase" data-format="png">PNG 저장</button><button type="button" data-action="image-purchase" data-format="jpg">JPG 저장</button></div></div></div>`;
          $("#purchaseModal").classList.remove("hidden");
        }
        function printElement(html) {
          $("#printZone").innerHTML = html;
          window.print();
        }
        async function saveImage(node, format, name) {
          if (typeof html2canvas !== "function")
            return alert(
              "이미지 저장 모듈을 불러오지 못했습니다. 인터넷 연결을 확인해 주세요.",
            );
          try {
            const isJpg = format === "jpg",
              canvas = await html2canvas(node, {
                scale: 2,
                backgroundColor: "#ffffff",
                scrollX: 0,
                scrollY: 0,
                useCORS: true,
              }),
              data = canvas.toDataURL(isJpg ? "image/jpeg" : "image/png", 0.94);
            $("#imageModal").innerHTML =
              `<div class="modal-card image-card"><div class="modal-head"><div><h2>이미지 저장</h2><p>아래 버튼으로 기기에 저장하세요.</p></div><button class="close-button" type="button" data-action="close-image">×</button></div><div class="modal-body"><img src="${data}" alt="저장할 문서 이미지"><a class="full-button primary-button" style="display:grid;place-items:center;text-decoration:none" href="${data}" download="${safeName(name)}.${isJpg ? "jpg" : "png"}">이미지 다운로드</a></div></div>`;
            $("#imageModal").classList.remove("hidden");
          } catch {
            alert("이미지 생성 중 오류가 발생했습니다.");
          }
        }

        function exportExcel() {
          const rows = deliveries().filter((d) => d.status !== "cancelled"),
            summary = [],
            detail = [],
            individual = [],
            handover = customers()
              .filter(hasHandover)
              .map((c) => ({
                거래처명: c.name,
                납품처: c.deliveryPlace,
                주소: c.address,
                연락처: c.phone,
                "입고 가능 시간": c.receivingTime,
                "출입 비밀번호": c.accessPassword
                  ? "등록됨(앱에서 확인)"
                  : "미등록",
                "매장 진입 방법": c.entryMethod,
                "물건 놓는 자리": c.dropLocation,
                "절대 하지 말아야 할 사항": c.deliveryCautions,
                "주차·엘리베이터": c.parkingInfo,
                "기타 인수인계": c.handoverNote,
                "최근 수정일": c.handoverUpdatedAt
                  ? new Date(c.handoverUpdatedAt).toLocaleString("ko-KR")
                  : "",
                "최근 작성자": c.handoverUpdatedBy,
              }));
          rows.forEach((d) => {
            const c = customerOf(d),
              daily = d.items.reduce((s, i) => s + itemAmount(i), 0);
            summary.push({
              배송순서: d.routeOrder,
              긴급추가발주: d.isUrgentAdditional ? "예" : "아니오",
              긴급발주확인: d.isUrgentAdditional
                ? d.urgentAcknowledged
                  ? "확인 완료"
                  : "미확인"
                : "해당 없음",
              "점포 인수인계": hasHandover(c)
                ? handoverAcknowledged(d, c)
                  ? "확인 완료"
                  : "미확인"
                : "미등록",
              "인수인계 확인자": d.handoverAcknowledgedBy || "",
              거래처명: c.name,
              납품처: c.deliveryPlace,
              주소: c.address,
              연락처: c.phone,
              "당일 공급금액": daily,
              "전날 미수금액": d.previousBalance,
              "최종 합계": daily + Number(d.previousBalance || 0),
              "계획 박스 수": d.boxes.length,
              "실제 상차 박스 수": d.loadedBoxCount,
              "박스 대조": !d.boxes.length
                ? "해당 없음"
                : d.boxCountConfirmed && d.loadedBoxCount === d.boxes.length
                  ? "일치"
                  : "미확인·불일치",
              "활어 계근": deliveryWeighingReady(d) ? "확정" : "미확정",
              배송상태: statusLabel(d.status),
              특이사항: [d.coPackNote, d.notes].filter(Boolean).join(" / "),
            });
            d.items.forEach((i, index) => {
              const taskDone = (i.weighings || []).filter(
                (w) => w.loadedAt,
              ).length;
              detail.push({
                배송일: d.deliveryDate,
                배송순서: d.routeOrder,
                거래처명: c.name,
                구분: i.category,
                "어종·품목": i.species,
                규격: i.size,
                원산지: i.originCountry,
                작업방식: i.processing,
                주문수량: i.requestedQty,
                주문단위: i.unit,
                계근마릿수: (i.weighings || []).length,
                "개체 상차 완료": `${taskDone}/${(i.weighings || []).length}`,
                계근확정: i.weighingConfirmed ? "확정" : "미확정",
                "실제중량(kg)": i.actualWeight ?? "",
                가격기준: i.priceUnit,
                판매단가: i.unitPrice,
                상품금액: baseAmount(i),
                "작업비 kg단가": i.processingFeePerKg,
                "작업비 금액":
                  i.category === "필렛 제품"
                    ? (Number(i.actualWeight ?? i.requestedQty) || 0) *
                      (Number(i.processingFeePerKg) || 0)
                    : 0,
                "전날 미수금액": index === 0 ? d.previousBalance : "",
                상차위치: tankLabel(i.tankNumber),
                "수조 실제 상차": i.tankNumber
                  ? i.tankLoaded
                    ? "완료"
                    : "미확인"
                  : "해당 없음",
                수조변경이력: (i.tankHistory || [])
                  .map(
                    (h) =>
                      `${tankLabel(h.from)}→${tankLabel(h.to)}(${h.reason})`,
                  )
                  .join(" / "),
                고무밴드: i.rubberBand
                  ? `${i.rubberBandColor} ${i.rubberBandQuantity}개`
                  : "",
                메모: i.includedNote,
                하차확인: i.checked ? "확인 완료" : "미확인",
              });
              (i.weighings || []).forEach((w, n) =>
                individual.push({
                  배송일: d.deliveryDate,
                  배송순서: d.routeOrder,
                  작업번호: taskCode(w),
                  거래처명: c.name,
                  "어종·품목": i.species,
                  원산지: i.originCountry,
                  "개별중량(kg)": w.weight,
                  "밴드 지시": taskBandText(i),
                  "콜 전달": w.calledAt ? "완료" : "미확인",
                  "복창 확인": w.repeatConfirmedAt ? "완료" : "미확인",
                  "밴드 실물 확인": !taskBandRequired(i)
                    ? "해당 없음"
                    : w.bandVerifiedAt
                      ? "완료"
                      : "미확인",
                  "지정 수조": i.tankNumber
                    ? `${state.profile.vehicleNumber}호차 ${i.tankNumber}번`
                    : "미지정",
                  "실제 확인 수조": w.verifiedTank
                    ? `${w.verifiedVehicle}호차 ${w.verifiedTank}번`
                    : "미확인",
                  "개체 상차": w.loadedAt ? "완료" : "미확인",
                  상차확인자: w.loadedBy || "",
                  "경고·오류기록": (w.verificationLog || [])
                    .filter((log) =>
                      ["tank-error", "band-error", "weight-warning"].includes(
                        log.type,
                      ),
                    )
                    .map((log) => log.message)
                    .join(" / "),
                  계근순번: n + 1,
                  "품목합계(kg)": i.actualWeight ?? "",
                  계근상태: i.weighingConfirmed ? "확정" : "미확정",
                  입력시각: w.at || "",
                  상차완료시각: w.loadedAt || "",
                }),
              );
            });
          });
          const cancelled = deliveries()
            .filter((d) => d.status === "cancelled")
            .map((d) => ({
              거래처명: customerOf(d).name,
              배송일: d.deliveryDate,
              상태: "발주 취소",
            }));
          const bandExport = bandSummaryRows().map((row) => ({
              밴드색상: row.color,
              "준비 수량": row.total,
              "실물 확인 완료": row.verified,
              "남은 수량": row.remaining,
              거래처별내역: row.details
                .map(
                  (detail) =>
                    `${detail.store} ${detail.species} ${detail.verified}/${detail.total}`,
                )
                .join(" / "),
            })),
            stats = errorStats(),
            errorSummary = [
              {
                배송일: workDate,
                "수조 오류 방지": stats.tankErrors,
                "밴드 오류 방지": stats.bandErrors,
                "비정상 계근 경고": stats.weightWarnings,
                "계근값 수정": stats.weightEdits,
                "수조 위치 변경": stats.tankChanges,
                "상차 재확인": stats.resets,
                "오류 방지 합계": stats.prevented,
                "개체 상차 완료": `${stats.loaded}/${stats.tasks}`,
              },
            ],
            errorDetails = stats.details.map((row) => ({
              유형: row.label,
              거래처명: row.store,
              품목: row.species,
              작업번호: row.task,
              내용: row.message,
              시각: row.at ? new Date(row.at).toLocaleString("ko-KR") : "",
              확인자: row.by,
            }));
          if (typeof XLSX !== "undefined") {
            const wb = XLSX.utils.book_new(),
              info = XLSX.utils.aoa_to_sheet([
                ["회사명", state.profile.companyName],
                ["배송담당자", state.profile.driverName],
                ["차량 호차", state.profile.vehicleNumber],
                ["배송일", workDate],
                [
                  "업무 마감",
                  isWorkClosed()
                    ? new Date(state.workClosures[workDate].at).toLocaleString(
                        "ko-KR",
                      )
                    : "미마감",
                ],
              ]);
            XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(wb, info, "기본정보");
            XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(
              wb,
              XLSX.utils.json_to_sheet(summary),
              "거래처별 요약",
            );
            XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(
              wb,
              XLSX.utils.json_to_sheet(detail),
              "품목별 거래명세",
            );
            if (individual.length)
              XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(
                wb,
                XLSX.utils.json_to_sheet(individual),
                "활어 개별 계근",
              );
            if (handover.length)
              XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(
                wb,
                XLSX.utils.json_to_sheet(handover),
                "점포 인수인계",
              );
            if (cancelled.length)
              XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(
                wb,
                XLSX.utils.json_to_sheet(cancelled),
                "취소 내역",
              );
            if (bandExport.length)
              XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(
                wb,
                XLSX.utils.json_to_sheet(bandExport),
                "밴드 작업 현황",
              );
            XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(
              wb,
              XLSX.utils.json_to_sheet(errorSummary),
              "오류 통계",
            );
            if (errorDetails.length)
              XLSX.utils.book_append_sheet(
                wb,
                XLSX.utils.json_to_sheet(errorDetails),
                "오류 상세",
              );
            XLSX.writeFile(
              wb,
              `${safeName(state.profile.companyName || "배송")}_거래명세표_${workDate}.xlsx`,
            );
          } else {
            const headers = Object.keys(summary[0] || {}),
              csv = [
                headers.join(","),
                ...summary.map((r) =>
                  headers
                    .map((h) => `"${String(r[h] ?? "").replace(/"/g, '""')}"`)
                    .join(","),
                ),
              ].join("\n"),
              blob = new Blob(["\ufeff" + csv], {
                type: "text/csv;charset=utf-8",
              }),
              a = document.createElement("a");
            a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
            a.download = `거래명세표_${workDate}.csv`;
            a.click();
            setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href), 1000);
          }
        }
        function backup() {
          const blob = new Blob([JSON.stringify(state, null, 2)], {
              type: "application/json",
            }),
            a = document.createElement("a");
          a.href = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
          a.download = `배송관리_백업_${localDate()}.json`;
          a.click();
          setTimeout(() => URL.revokeObjectURL(a.href), 1000);
        }
        function restore(file) {
          const reader = new FileReader();
          reader.onload = () => {
            try {
              const raw = JSON.parse(reader.result);
              if (
                !raw.profile ||
                !Array.isArray(raw.customers) ||
                !Array.isArray(raw.deliveries)
              )
                throw new Error();
              if (
                confirm(
                  "현재 자료를 백업 내용으로 교체할까요?\n현재 내용도 교체 전에 자동 백업됩니다.",
                )
              ) {
                saveAutoSnapshot(JSON.stringify(state), "백업 파일 복원 직전");
                state = {
                  version: 5,
                  profile: {
                    companyName: raw.profile.companyName || "",
                    driverName: raw.profile.driverName || "",
                    vehicleNumber: raw.profile.vehicleNumber || "",
                  },
                  customers: raw.customers.map(normalizeCustomer),
                  deliveries: raw.deliveries.map(normalizeDelivery),
                  departureChecks:
                    raw.departureChecks &&
                    typeof raw.departureChecks === "object"
                      ? raw.departureChecks
                      : {},
                  preferences: {
                    autoNextLoading:
                      raw.preferences?.autoNextLoading === undefined
                        ? true
                        : Boolean(raw.preferences.autoNextLoading),
                    weightRules: normalizeWeightRules(
                      raw.preferences?.weightRules,
                    ),
                  },
                  workClosures:
                    raw.workClosures && typeof raw.workClosures === "object"
                      ? raw.workClosures
                      : {},
                  workClosureHistory: Array.isArray(raw.workClosureHistory)
                    ? raw.workClosureHistory.slice(-200)
                    : [],
                };
                saveState("백업 파일 복원 전");
                render();
                alert("복원했습니다.");
              }
            } catch {
              alert("올바른 배송관리 백업 파일이 아닙니다.");
            } finally {
              $("#restoreInput").value = "";
            }
          };
          reader.readAsText(file);
        }
        function closeModal(id) {
          $("#" + id).classList.add("hidden");
        }

        function triggerAlarm() {
          if (alarmTimer) return;
          $("#liveAlarm").classList.remove("hidden");
          if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([500, 250, 500]);
          alarmTimer = setInterval(() => {
            if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(350);
          }, 1200);
        }
        function stopAlarm() {
          clearInterval(alarmTimer);
          alarmTimer = null;
          $("#liveAlarm").classList.add("hidden");
        }
        function triggerCancel(store) {
          $("#cancelStore").textContent = store || "거래처";
          $("#cancelAlarm").classList.remove("hidden");
          if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate([700, 300, 700, 300, 700]);
          clearInterval(cancelTimer);
          cancelTimer = setInterval(() => {
            if (navigator.vibrate) navigator.vibrate(500);
          }, 1200);
        }
        function stopCancel() {
          clearInterval(cancelTimer);
          cancelTimer = null;
          $("#cancelAlarm").classList.add("hidden");
        }
        async function pollCloud() {
          const code = String(state.profile.vehicleNumber || "")
            .trim()
            .replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_-]/g, "");
          if (!code) {
            $("#networkDot").className = "dot loading";
            $("#networkText").textContent = "호차 설정 필요";
            return;
          }
          $("#networkDot").className = "dot loading";
          $("#networkText").textContent = "발주 확인 중...";
          try {
            const res = await fetch(`${CLOUD_RELAY_URL}${code}/json?poll=1`);
            if (!res.ok) throw new Error();
            const text = await res.text();
            $("#networkDot").className = "dot";
            $("#networkText").textContent = "발주 자동 수신중";
            if (!text.trim()) return;
            const events = text
                .trim()
                .split("\n")
                .map((line) => {
                  try {
                    const raw = JSON.parse(line),
                      packet = JSON.parse(raw.message || "{}");
                    return {
                      packet,
                      time:
                        Number(packet.serverTimestamp) || Number(raw.time) || 0,
                    };
                  } catch {
                    return null;
                  }
                })
                .filter(Boolean)
                .sort((a, b) => a.time - b.time),
              acked = readJSON(ACK_KEY, []),
              cancelledIds = new Set(
                events
                  .filter((e) => e.packet.status === "cancelled")
                  .map((e) => e.packet.orderId),
              );
            let changed = false,
              newArrived = false;
            for (const { packet } of events) {
              if (!packet.orderId || acked.includes(packet.orderId)) continue;
              const existing = state.deliveries.find(
                (d) => d.cloudOrderId === packet.orderId,
              );
              if (packet.status === "ordered") {
                if (existing || cancelledIds.has(packet.orderId)) continue;
                const store = String(packet.store || "").trim(),
                  orderDate = packet.orderDate || localDate(1);
                if (!store || !Array.isArray(packet.items)) continue;
                let customer = state.customers.find((c) => c.name === store);
                if (!customer) {
                  customer = normalizeCustomer(
                    {
                      id: newId(),
                      name: store,
                      deliveryPlace: store,
                      address: packet.address || "",
                      phone: packet.phone || "",
                      routeOrder: customers().length + 1,
                    },
                    state.customers.length,
                  );
                  state.customers.push(customer);
                } else {
                  if (packet.address) customer.address = packet.address;
                  if (packet.phone) customer.phone = packet.phone;
                }
                const sameStoreAlready = state.deliveries.some(
                    (d) =>
                      d.deliveryDate === orderDate &&
                      d.customerId === customer.id &&
                      !["cancelled", "completed"].includes(d.status),
                  ),
                  workStarted = Boolean(
                    state.departureChecks?.[orderDate] ||
                      state.deliveries.some(
                        (d) =>
                          d.deliveryDate === orderDate &&
                          (d.boxCountConfirmed ||
                            d.items?.some(
                              (i) => i.weighingConfirmed || i.tankLoaded,
                            )),
                      ),
                  ),
                  urgent = Boolean(
                    packet.isUrgentAdditional ||
                      sameStoreAlready ||
                      workStarted,
                  ),
                  items = packet.items.map((pi) =>
                    normalizeItem({
                      category: pi.category,
                      species: pi.item,
                      size: pi.size,
                      originCountry: pi.origin,
                      requestedQty: pi.qty,
                      unit: pi.unit,
                      processing: pi.process,
                      includedNote: pi.memo,
                      rubberBand: pi.rubberBand,
                      rubberBandColor: pi.rubberBandColor,
                      rubberBandQuantity: pi.rubberBandQuantity,
                    }),
                  ),
                  boxes = [];
                items
                  .filter((i) => i.unit === "박스")
                  .forEach((i) => {
                    const count = Math.max(
                      1,
                      Math.min(20, Math.floor(Number(i.requestedQty) || 1)),
                    );
                    for (let n = 0; n < count; n++)
                      boxes.push(
                        normalizeBox(
                          { contents: `${i.species} ${n + 1}/${count}박스` },
                          boxes.length,
                        ),
                      );
                  });
                state.deliveries.push(
                  normalizeDelivery({
                    id: newId(),
                    cloudOrderId: packet.orderId,
                    customerId: customer.id,
                    fallbackStoreName: store,
                    deliveryDate: orderDate,
                    routeOrder:
                      state.deliveries.filter(
                        (d) =>
                          d.deliveryDate === orderDate &&
                          d.status !== "cancelled",
                      ).length + 1,
                    status: "new",
                    isUrgentAdditional: urgent,
                    urgentAcknowledged: !urgent,
                    items,
                    boxes,
                    notes: "",
                    coPackNote: "",
                    previousBalance: 0,
                    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
                  }),
                );
                changed = true;
                newArrived = true;
              } else if (
                packet.status === "cancelled" &&
                existing &&
                existing.status !== "cancelled"
              ) {
                existing.status = "cancelled";
                changed = true;
                triggerCancel(packet.store || customerOf(existing).name);
              }
            }
            if (changed) {
              saveState("새 발주 수신 전");
              render();
              if (newArrived) triggerAlarm();
            }
          } catch {
            $("#networkDot").className = "dot loading";
            $("#networkText").textContent = navigator.onLine
              ? "발주 연결 재시도 중"
              : "인터넷 끊김";
          }
        }
        function startCloudSync() {
          clearInterval(cloudTimer);
          pollCloud();
          cloudTimer = setInterval(pollCloud, 5000);
        }

        document.addEventListener("pointerdown", (e) => {
          const item = e.target.closest("[data-drag-tank-item]");
          if (
            !item ||
            view !== "today" ||
            (e.pointerType === "mouse" && e.button !== 0)
          )
            return;
          cancelTankDrag();
          tankDrag = {
            pointerId: e.pointerId,
            element: item,
            deliveryId: Number(item.dataset.deliveryId),
            itemId: Number(item.dataset.itemId),
            sourceTank: Number(item.dataset.sourceTank),
            targetTank: Number(item.dataset.sourceTank),
            startX: e.clientX,
            startY: e.clientY,
            x: e.clientX,
            y: e.clientY,
            active: false,
            timer: null,
            ghost: null,
          };
          /*
           * 일반 세로 스크롤과 수조 끌기를 분리합니다.
           * 손가락을 움직이면 스크롤로 판단하고, 같은 위치에서 0.45초간
           * 누른 경우에만 포인터를 잡아 수조 이동을 시작합니다.
           */
          tankDrag.timer = setTimeout(() => {
            if (!tankDrag || tankDrag.pointerId !== e.pointerId) return;
            try {
              tankDrag.element.setPointerCapture(tankDrag.pointerId);
            } catch {}
            startTankDrag();
          }, 450);
        });
        document.addEventListener(
          "pointermove",
          (e) => {
            if (!tankDrag || e.pointerId !== tankDrag.pointerId) return;
            tankDrag.x = e.clientX;
            tankDrag.y = e.clientY;
            const distance = Math.hypot(
              e.clientX - tankDrag.startX,
              e.clientY - tankDrag.startY,
            );
            if (!tankDrag.active && distance > 10) {
              cancelTankDrag();
              return;
            }
            if (tankDrag?.active) {
              if (e.cancelable) e.preventDefault();
              updateTankDrag(e.clientX, e.clientY);
            }
          },
          { passive: false },
        );
        document.addEventListener("pointerup", (e) => {
          if (tankDrag && e.pointerId === tankDrag.pointerId) finishTankDrag();
        });
        document.addEventListener("pointercancel", (e) => {
          if (tankDrag && e.pointerId === tankDrag.pointerId) cancelTankDrag();
        });
        document.addEventListener("contextmenu", (e) => {
          if (e.target.closest("[data-drag-tank-item]")) e.preventDefault();
        });
        document.addEventListener("click", (e) => {
          if (Date.now() < tankDragSuppressUntil) {
            e.preventDefault();
            e.stopPropagation();
            return;
          }
          const b = e.target.closest("button");
          if (!b) return;
          const action = b.dataset.action;
          if (b.dataset.nav) return setView(b.dataset.nav);
          if (action === "driver-logout") {
            if (confirm("이 휴대폰에서 로그아웃할까요?")) driverLogout();
            return;
          }
          if (action && LOCKED_DAY_ACTIONS.has(action) && !ensureWorkOpen())
            return;
          if (action === "stop-alarm") return stopAlarm();
          if (action === "stop-cancel-alarm") return stopCancel();
          if (action === "open-departure") return openDepartureCheck();
          if (action === "close-departure") return closeModal("departureModal");
          if (action === "confirm-departure") return confirmDeparture();
          if (action === "resolve-departure-issue")
            return resolveDepartureIssue(b.dataset.index);
          if (action === "open-urgent") return openUrgentList();
          if (action === "close-urgent") return closeModal("urgentModal");
          if (action === "ack-urgent-order")
            return acknowledgeUrgent(b.dataset.id);
          if (action === "edit-urgent") {
            closeModal("urgentModal");
            return openDelivery(Number(b.dataset.id));
          }
          if (action === "urgent-reorder") {
            closeModal("urgentModal");
            reorderMode = true;
            renderToday();
            window.scrollTo({
              top: document.body.scrollHeight,
              behavior: "smooth",
            });
            return;
          }
          if (action === "open-box-compare") return openBoxCompare();
          if (action === "close-box") return closeModal("boxModal");
          if (action === "box-step") {
            const input = b
              .closest("[data-box-compare]")
              ?.querySelector("[data-box-count-input]");
            if (input)
              input.value = Math.max(
                0,
                Math.min(
                  99,
                  (Number(input.value) || 0) + Number(b.dataset.step),
                ),
              );
            return;
          }
          if (action === "confirm-box-count")
            return confirmBoxCount(b.dataset.id, b);
          if (action === "open-backups") return openAutoBackups();
          if (action === "close-backups") return closeModal("backupModal");
          if (action === "create-auto-backup") return createAutoBackup();
          if (action === "restore-auto-backup")
            return restoreAutoBackup(b.dataset.id);
          if (action === "open-store-guide")
            return openStoreGuide(b.dataset.id, b.dataset.source);
          if (action === "close-store-guide") return closeStoreGuide();
          if (action === "confirm-store-guide") return confirmStoreGuide();
          if (action === "toggle-guide-secret") return toggleGuideSecret(b);
          if (action === "toggle-form-secret") return toggleFormSecret(b);
          if (action === "open-band-summary") return openBandSummary();
          if (action === "close-band-summary") return closeModal("bandModal");
          if (action === "open-weight-rules") return openWeightRules();
          if (action === "close-weight-rules")
            return closeModal("weightRuleModal");
          if (action === "reset-weight-rules") {
            if (confirm("어종별 정상 중량 기준을 기본값으로 되돌릴까요?")) {
              state.preferences = state.preferences || {};
              state.preferences.weightRules = normalizeWeightRules({});
              saveState("정상 중량 기준 초기화 전");
              openWeightRules();
            }
            return;
          }
          if (action === "open-error-stats") return openErrorStats();
          if (action === "close-error-stats") return closeModal("statsModal");
          if (action === "open-work-close") return openWorkClosure();
          if (action === "close-work-close") return closeModal("closeDayModal");
          if (action === "close-work-day") return closeWorkDay();
          if (action === "reopen-work-day") return reopenWorkDay();
          if (action === "edit-store-handover") {
            closeModal("storeGuideModal");
            closeModal("checkModal");
            closeModal("departureModal");
            return openCustomer(Number(b.dataset.customerId));
          }
          if (action === "open-loading-control") {
            loadingError = "";
            return openLoadingControl("", 0, 0);
          }
          if (action === "close-loading") {
            loadingError = "";
            stopQrScanner();
            return closeModal("loadingModal");
          }
          if (action === "open-loading-task") {
            loadingError = "";
            return openLoadingTask(
              b.dataset.deliveryId,
              b.dataset.itemId,
              b.dataset.weightId,
            );
          }
          if (action === "back-loading-list") {
            loadingError = "";
            return openLoadingControl(
              "",
              loadingFilterDeliveryId,
              loadingFilterItemId,
            );
          }
          if (action === "clear-loading-filter") {
            loadingError = "";
            return openLoadingControl("", 0, 0);
          }
          if (action === "call-loading-task") return callLoadingTask();
          if (action === "confirm-loading-repeat")
            return confirmLoadingRepeat();
          if (action === "confirm-loading-band")
            return confirmLoadingBand(true);
          if (action === "report-band-mismatch")
            return confirmLoadingBand(false);
          if (action === "verify-loading-tank") {
            const fromScanner = !$("#qrModal").classList.contains("hidden");
            if (fromScanner) {
              stopQrScanner();
              closeModal("qrModal");
              $("#loadingModal").classList.remove("hidden");
            }
            return verifyLoadingTank(
              b.dataset.tank,
              state.profile.vehicleNumber,
              fromScanner ? "카메라 화면 수동 확인" : "수조 번호 직접 확인",
            );
          }
          if (action === "complete-loading-task") return completeLoadingTask();
          if (action === "reset-loading-task") return resetLoadingTask();
          if (action === "open-loading-tank-change")
            return openLoadingTankChange();
          if (action === "open-qr-labels") return openQrLabels();
          if (action === "print-qr-labels") return printQrLabels();
          if (action === "open-qr-scanner") return openQrScanner();
          if (action === "close-qr") return closeQr(false);
          if (action === "close-qr-scanner") return closeQr(true);
          if (action === "open-tank-info") return openTankInfo(b.dataset.tank);
          if (action === "open-tank-manager") return openTankManager();
          if (action === "toggle-tank-loaded")
            return toggleTankLoaded(
              b.dataset.deliveryId,
              b.dataset.itemId,
              b.dataset.source,
            );
          if (action === "open-tank-change")
            return openTankChange(
              b.dataset.deliveryId,
              b.dataset.itemId,
              b.dataset.source,
            );
          if (action === "choose-tank") return chooseTank(b.dataset.tank);
          if (action === "confirm-tank-change") return confirmTankChange();
          if (action === "close-tank-change") return closeTankChange();
          if (action === "close-tank") return closeModal("tankModal");
          if (action === "open-weigh-list") {
            closeModal("loadingModal");
            return openWeighingList();
          }
          if (action === "open-weigh-item") {
            closeModal("checkModal");
            return openWeighItem(b.dataset.deliveryId, b.dataset.itemId);
          }
          if (action === "close-weigh") return closeModal("weighModal");
          if (action === "back-weigh-list") return openWeighingList();
          if (action === "delete-weight") return deleteWeight(b.dataset.id);
          if (action === "undo-last-weight") {
            const { d, i } = findWeighItem();
            if (d && i?.weighings?.length) {
              i.weighings.pop();
              i.weighingConfirmed = false;
              i.weighingConfirmedAt = null;
              syncItemTaskLoad(i);
              syncWeightTotal(i);
              saveState("마지막 계근 취소 전");
              openWeighItem(d.id, i.id);
            }
            return;
          }
          if (action === "confirm-weighing") return confirmWeighing();
          if (action === "reopen-weighing") {
            const { d, i } = findWeighItem();
            if (d && i) {
              i.weighingConfirmed = false;
              i.weighingConfirmedAt = null;
              saveState("계근 확정 취소 전");
              openWeighItem(d.id, i.id);
            }
            return;
          }
          if (action === "toggle-reorder") {
            reorderMode = !reorderMode;
            return renderToday();
          }
          if (action === "move-up" || action === "move-down") {
            const list = deliveries(),
              idx = list.findIndex((d) => d.id === Number(b.dataset.id));
            return moveDelivery(
              Number(b.dataset.id),
              idx + (action === "move-up" ? -1 : 1),
            );
          }
          if (action === "new-customer") return openCustomer();
          if (action === "edit-customer")
            return openCustomer(Number(b.dataset.id));
          if (action === "new-delivery") return openDelivery();
          if (action === "open-check")
            return openChecklist(Number(b.dataset.id));
          if (action === "save-previous-balance") return savePreviousBalance();
          if (action === "ack-order") {
            const d = state.deliveries.find(
              (x) => x.id === Number(b.dataset.id),
            );
            if (d) d.status = "ready";
            saveState("신규 발주 확인 전");
            stopAlarm();
            return renderToday();
          }
          if (action === "ack-cancel") {
            const id = Number(b.dataset.id),
              d = state.deliveries.find((x) => x.id === id),
              acked = readJSON(ACK_KEY, []);
            if (d?.cloudOrderId && !acked.includes(d.cloudOrderId)) {
              acked.push(d.cloudOrderId);
              localStorage.setItem(ACK_KEY, JSON.stringify(acked));
            }
            state.deliveries = state.deliveries.filter((x) => x.id !== id);
            saveState();
            return renderToday();
          }
          if (action === "delete-delivery") {
            if (confirm("이 배송 기록을 삭제할까요?")) {
              state.deliveries = state.deliveries.filter(
                (d) => d.id !== Number(b.dataset.id),
              );
              normalizeRoutes();
              saveState();
              renderToday();
            }
            return;
          }
          if (action === "close-modal") return closeModal("formModal");
          if (action === "close-check") return closeModal("checkModal");
          if (action === "close-purchase") return closeModal("purchaseModal");
          if (action === "close-image") return closeModal("imageModal");
          if (action === "add-form-item") return addFormItem();
          if (action === "remove-form-item") {
            syncFormDraft();
            if (formDraft.items.length > 1)
              formDraft.items.splice(Number(b.dataset.index), 1);
            return rerenderDeliveryForm();
          }
          if (action === "add-form-box") {
            syncFormDraft();
            formDraft.boxes.push(
              normalizeBox({ contents: "" }, formDraft.boxes.length),
            );
            return rerenderDeliveryForm();
          }
          if (action === "remove-form-box") {
            syncFormDraft();
            formDraft.boxes.splice(Number(b.dataset.index), 1);
            formDraft.boxes = formDraft.boxes.map(normalizeBox);
            return rerenderDeliveryForm();
          }
          if (action === "edit-delivery") {
            closeModal("checkModal");
            return openDelivery(Number(b.dataset.id));
          }
          if (action === "add-check-box") {
            const d = state.deliveries.find((x) => x.id === selectedDeliveryId);
            d.boxes.push(normalizeBox({ contents: "" }, d.boxes.length));
            d.boxCountConfirmed = false;
            d.boxCountConfirmedAt = null;
            saveState("박스 추가 전");
            return openChecklist(d.id);
          }
          if (action === "delete-check-box") {
            const d = state.deliveries.find((x) => x.id === selectedDeliveryId);
            d.boxes = d.boxes
              .filter((x) => x.id !== Number(b.dataset.id))
              .map(normalizeBox);
            d.boxCountConfirmed = false;
            d.boxCountConfirmedAt = null;
            saveState("박스 삭제 전");
            return openChecklist(d.id);
          }
          if (action === "complete-delivery") {
            const d = state.deliveries.find(
              (x) => x.id === Number(b.dataset.id),
            );
            if (!deliveryWeighingReady(d))
              return alert("활어 계근을 먼저 확정해 주세요.");
            if ((d.items || []).some((i) => i.tankNumber && !i.tankLoaded))
              return alert(
                "콜·복창·밴드·수조 확인을 포함한 상차 관제를 먼저 완료해 주세요.",
              );
            d.status = "completed";
            d.completedAt = new Date().toISOString();
            saveState();
            closeModal("checkModal");
            return render();
          }
          if (action === "undo-complete") {
            if (confirm("하차 완료를 취소하고 다시 확인할까요?")) {
              const d = state.deliveries.find(
                (x) => x.id === Number(b.dataset.id),
              );
              d.status = "ready";
              d.completedAt = null;
              saveState();
              openChecklist(d.id);
            }
            return;
          }
          if (action === "print-statement")
            return printElement($("#statementView").outerHTML);
          if (action === "image-statement")
            return saveImage(
              $("#statementView"),
              b.dataset.format,
              `${customerOf(state.deliveries.find((d) => d.id === selectedDeliveryId)).name}_거래명세서_${workDate}`,
            );
          if (action === "open-purchase") return openPurchase();
          if (action === "print-purchase")
            return printElement($("#purchaseSheet").outerHTML);
          if (action === "image-purchase")
            return saveImage(
              $("#purchaseSheet"),
              b.dataset.format,
              `당일_매입발주서_${workDate}`,
            );
          if (action === "export-excel") return exportExcel();
          if (action === "backup") return backup();
          if (action === "restore") return $("#restoreInput").click();
          if (action === "delete-customer") {
            const id = Number(b.dataset.id);
            if (state.deliveries.some((d) => d.customerId === id))
              return alert("이 거래처의 배송 기록이 있어 삭제할 수 없습니다.");
            if (confirm("거래처를 삭제할까요?")) {
              state.customers = state.customers.filter((c) => c.id !== id);
              normalizeCustomerOrder();
              saveState();
              closeModal("formModal");
              renderCustomers();
            }
          }
        });
        document.addEventListener("submit", (e) => {
          e.preventDefault();
          if (
            ["deliveryForm", "weighingForm"].includes(e.target.id) &&
            !ensureWorkOpen()
          )
            return;
          if (e.target.id === "setupForm" || e.target.id === "settingsForm") {
            const fd = Object.fromEntries(new FormData(e.target));
            state.profile = assignedDriverProfile
              ? {
                  companyName: "장백수산",
                  driverName: assignedDriverProfile.full_name,
                  vehicleNumber: String(
                    assignedDriverProfile.vehicle_number,
                  ),
                }
              : {
                  companyName: String(fd.companyName).trim(),
                  driverName: String(fd.driverName).trim(),
                  vehicleNumber: String(fd.vehicleNumber).trim(),
                };
            if (e.target.id === "settingsForm") {
              state.preferences = state.preferences || {};
              state.preferences.autoNextLoading = fd.autoNextLoading === "on";
              state.preferences.weightRules = normalizeWeightRules(
                state.preferences.weightRules,
              );
            }
            saveState();
            closeModal("setupModal");
            render();
            startCloudSync();
            if (e.target.id === "settingsForm")
              alert("개인 업무 설정을 저장했습니다.");
          }
          if (e.target.id === "customerForm") saveCustomer(e.target);
          if (e.target.id === "deliveryForm") saveDelivery();
          if (e.target.id === "weightRulesForm") saveWeightRules(e.target);
          if (e.target.id === "weighingForm")
            addWeight(new FormData(e.target).get("weight"));
        });
        document.addEventListener("change", (e) => {
          if (e.target.id === "workDate") {
            workDate = e.target.value || localDate(1);
            reorderMode = false;
            render();
            scheduleCentralSync("업무 날짜 변경");
          }
          if (
            isWorkClosed() &&
            (e.target.dataset.action === "route-position" ||
              e.target.dataset.weightEntry ||
              e.target.dataset.checkToggle ||
              e.target.dataset.checkField)
          ) {
            ensureWorkOpen();
            render();
            return;
          }
          if (e.target.dataset.action === "route-position")
            moveDelivery(
              Number(e.target.dataset.id),
              Number(e.target.value) - 1,
            );
          if (e.target.dataset.weightEntry)
            editWeight(e.target.dataset.weightEntry, e.target.value);
          if (e.target.dataset.checkToggle) {
            const card = e.target.closest(
              e.target.dataset.checkToggle === "item"
                ? "[data-check-item]"
                : "[data-check-box]",
            );
            if (e.target.dataset.checkToggle === "item")
              updateCheckItem(
                Number(card.dataset.checkItem),
                "checked",
                e.target.checked,
              );
            else
              updateCheckBox(
                Number(card.dataset.checkBox),
                "checked",
                e.target.checked,
              );
            openChecklist(selectedDeliveryId);
          }
          if (e.target.dataset.checkField) {
            const card = e.target.closest("[data-check-item]");
            updateCheckItem(
              Number(card.dataset.checkItem),
              e.target.dataset.checkField,
              e.target.value,
            );
            renderToday();
            openChecklist(selectedDeliveryId);
          }
          if (e.target.id === "restoreInput" && e.target.files[0])
            restore(e.target.files[0]);
          if (e.target.dataset.itemField === "category") {
            syncFormDraft();
            normalizeFormDraft();
            rerenderDeliveryForm();
          }
          if (e.target.dataset.itemField === "rubberBand") {
            syncFormDraft();
            normalizeFormDraft();
            rerenderDeliveryForm();
          }
        });
        document.addEventListener("input", (e) => {
          if (
            isWorkClosed() &&
            (e.target.dataset.checkField ||
              e.target.hasAttribute("data-check-box-content") ||
              e.target.closest("#deliveryForm"))
          )
            return;
          if (e.target.dataset.checkField) {
            const card = e.target.closest("[data-check-item]");
            updateCheckItem(
              Number(card.dataset.checkItem),
              e.target.dataset.checkField,
              e.target.value,
            );
            refreshStatement();
          }
          if (e.target.hasAttribute("data-check-box-content")) {
            const card = e.target.closest("[data-check-box]");
            updateCheckBox(
              Number(card.dataset.checkBox),
              "contents",
              e.target.value,
            );
          }
          if (e.target.closest("#deliveryForm")) {
            syncFormDraft();
            normalizeFormDraft();
            const total =
              formDraft.items.reduce((s, i) => s + itemAmount(i), 0) +
              Number(formDraft.previousBalance || 0);
            if ($("#formTotal"))
              $("#formTotal").textContent = money(total) + "원";
          }
        });
        document.addEventListener("focusin", (e) => {
          if (e.target.dataset?.itemField === "rubberBandColor")
            e.target.setAttribute("list", "bandColorList");
        });
        document.addEventListener("click", async (e) => {
          const button = e.target.closest("button"),
            action = button?.dataset.action;
          if (!action?.startsWith("central-")) return;
          try {
            if (action === "central-modal-close")
              return closeModal("centralModal");
            if (action === "central-store-guides") return openCentralStores();
            if (action === "central-incident-new")
              return openCentralIncident();
            if (action === "central-refresh") {
              await loadCentralWork();
              return alert("관리자 자료를 새로 확인했습니다.");
            }
            if (centralWorkday?.is_closed)
              return alert("관리자가 오늘 업무를 마감하여 변경할 수 없습니다.");
            const id = Number(button.dataset.id);
            if (action === "central-urgent-ack") {
              if (!confirm("긴급 추가 발주와 배송 순서를 확인했습니까?"))
                return;
              await updateCentralUrgent(id, "acknowledged");
              return alert("긴급 발주 확인을 관리자에게 전달했습니다.");
            }
            if (action === "central-urgent-loaded") {
              if (!confirm("긴급 추가 품목을 차량에 실제로 상차했습니까?"))
                return;
              await updateCentralUrgent(id, "loaded");
              return alert("상차 완료를 관리자에게 전달했습니다.");
            }
            if (action === "central-urgent-delivered") {
              if (!confirm("긴급 추가 품목을 거래처에 납품했습니까?"))
                return;
              await updateCentralUrgent(id, "delivered");
              return alert("긴급 발주 납품을 완료했습니다.");
            }
            if (action === "central-urgent-impossible") {
              const reason = prompt("처리할 수 없는 이유를 입력해 주세요.");
              if (!reason) return;
              await updateCentralUrgent(id, "impossible", {
                impossible_reason: reason,
              });
              return alert("처리 불가 사유를 관리자에게 전달했습니다.");
            }
          } catch (error) {
            alert(error?.message || "관리자 서버에 저장하지 못했습니다.");
          }
        });
        document.addEventListener("submit", async (e) => {
          if (e.target.id !== "centralIncidentForm") return;
          const form = e.target,
            message = $("#centralIncidentMessage"),
            fd = Object.fromEntries(new FormData(form));
          if (centralWorkday?.is_closed) {
            message.textContent = "관리자가 오늘 업무를 마감했습니다.";
            return;
          }
          message.textContent = "관리자에게 보고하는 중입니다.";
          try {
            const { error } = await supabaseClient
              .from("incident_reports")
              .insert({
                work_date: workDate,
                driver_id: assignedDriverProfile.id,
                store_id: fd.storeId || null,
                vehicle_number: assignedDriverProfile.vehicle_number,
                incident_type: fd.incidentType,
                severity: fd.severity,
                description: String(fd.description || "").trim(),
                status: "reported",
                created_by: assignedDriverProfile.id,
              });
            if (error) throw error;
            closeModal("centralModal");
            await loadCentralWork();
            scheduleCentralSync("현장 오류 보고");
            alert("관리자에게 오류를 보고했습니다.");
          } catch (error) {
            message.textContent =
              error?.message || "오류 보고를 저장하지 못했습니다.";
          }
        });
        document.addEventListener("change", (e) => {
          if (e.target.id === "workDate")
            setTimeout(loadCentralWork, 0);
        });
        setInterval(
          () => saveAutoSnapshot(JSON.stringify(state), "5분 정기 자동 백업"),
          300000,
        );
        document.addEventListener("visibilitychange", () => {
          if (document.hidden) {
            stopQrScanner();
            saveAutoSnapshot(JSON.stringify(state), "화면 종료 전 자동 백업");
          }
        });
        window.addEventListener("pagehide", stopQrScanner);
        initDriverAuth();
      })();
    </script>
  </body>
</html>
